# 怡安印刷商城 — 核心业务设计（卷三-A）

> **所属文档**：系统设计方案 v2.9.0  
> **原章节**：第6章（下A）  
> **内容**：售后服务、物流配送、商品管理、优惠券促销、用户标签画像、Customer/Order/Pay/Delivery API设计  
> **读者**：后端开发工程师

---

## 6.40 售后服务子系统设计 (AfterSaleService)

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：状态机驱动、领域事件解耦、Action 类原子化、SLA 可监控。

---

### 6.40.1 设计概述

售后服务子系统采用**状态机（State Machine）+ 领域事件（Domain Event）**架构，核心设计原则如下：

1. **三套状态码严格隔离**：
   - **EM 枚举**（`AfterSaleStatus`）：售后单据自身生命周期状态，存储于 `after_sales.status`。
   - **AF 枚举**（`AfterSaleFlowStatus`）：售后内部流程子状态（退货物流环节），存储于 `after_sales.process_flow_status`。
   - **客户侧字符串**：由后端在 DTO 中根据 `EM + AF + 售后类型` 组合映射得出，**不存储于数据库**。

2. **枚举内聚状态校验**：所有状态流转合法性由 Backed Enum 的 `canTransitionTo()` 方法校验，禁止在 Service / Controller 中分散判断。

3. **事件解耦**：售后创建、状态变更、SLA 超时等节点通过 Laravel Event 触发异步通知、日志记录、统计聚合，避免长事务。

4. **Action 原子化**：每个业务动作（创建、审核、退货、验收、完成、撤销、驳回）封装为独立的 Action 类，内部使用数据库事务保证一致性。

5. **SLA 可监控**：退货 3 天、补印 7 天、退款 2 天的时效承诺通过 `AfterSaleTimeoutWarning` 事件 + 定时任务监控，超期自动预警。

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph 客户侧
        C1[发起售后] --> C2[填写物流]
        C2 --> C3[查看进度]
        C3 --> C4[留言沟通]
    end

    subgraph 运营侧
        O1[审核工作台] --> O2[通过/驳回/挂起]
        O2 --> O3[仓库验收]
        O3 --> O4[执行退款/补印]
    end

    subgraph 领域层
        A1[CreateAfterSaleAction] --> E1[AfterSaleCreated]
        A2[AuditAfterSaleAction] --> E2[AfterSaleStatusChanged]
        A3[WarehouseReceiveAction] --> E3[AfterSaleStatusChanged]
        A4[CompleteAfterSaleAction] --> E4[AfterSaleStatusChanged]
    end

    C1 --> A1
    O1 --> A2
    O3 --> A3
    O4 --> A4
```

---

### 6.40.2 枚举定义

#### AfterSaleStatus (EM 售后单据状态)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 售后单据生命周期状态（EM）
 * PRD键名: EM
 * submitted=已提交 / processing=处理中 / completed=已完成 / suspended=已挂起 / revoked=已撤销 / cancelled=已取消
 */
enum AfterSaleStatus: string
{
    case SUBMITTED  = 'submitted';   // 0=已提交
    case PROCESSING = 'processing';  // 1=处理中
    case COMPLETED  = 'completed';   // 2=已完成
    case SUSPENDED  = 'suspended';   // 10=已挂起
    case REVOKED    = 'revoked';     // 20=已撤销
    case CANCELLED  = 'cancelled';   // 100=已取消

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SUBMITTED  => '已提交',
            self::PROCESSING => '处理中',
            self::COMPLETED  => '已完成',
            self::SUSPENDED  => '已挂起',
            self::REVOKED    => '已撤销',
            self::CANCELLED  => '已取消',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 售后状态流转校验
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            // 已提交 -> 处理中 / 已挂起 / 已撤销 / 已取消
            [self::SUBMITTED, self::PROCESSING],
            [self::SUBMITTED, self::SUSPENDED],
            [self::SUBMITTED, self::REVOKED],
            [self::SUBMITTED, self::CANCELLED] => true,

            // 处理中 -> 已完成 / 已挂起 / 已取消
            [self::PROCESSING, self::COMPLETED],
            [self::PROCESSING, self::SUSPENDED],
            [self::PROCESSING, self::CANCELLED] => true,

            // 已挂起 -> 处理中 / 已撤销 / 已取消
            [self::SUSPENDED, self::PROCESSING],
            [self::SUSPENDED, self::REVOKED],
            [self::SUSPENDED, self::CANCELLED] => true,

            // 已撤销 -> 已提交（重新提交）
            [self::REVOKED, self::SUBMITTED] => true,

            default => false,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为终态
     */
    public function isTerminal(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::COMPLETED, self::CANCELLED], true);
    }

    /**
     * 映射为客户侧展示状态字符串
     */
    public function toCustomerStatus(?AfterSaleFlowStatus $flowStatus = null, ?AfterSaleType $type = null): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SUBMITTED  => 'pendingReview',
            self::SUSPENDED  => 'pendingReview', // 挂起对客户显示为待审核
            self::REVOKED    => 'rejected',
            self::CANCELLED  => 'closed',
            self::PROCESSING => match (true) {
                $flowStatus === AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN => 'returnPending',
                $flowStatus === AfterSaleFlowStatus::RETURNED       => 'returnReceived',
                $type === AfterSaleType::REPRINT                     => 'reproducing',
                $type === AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT                    => 'refunding',
                default                                              => 'approved',
            },
            self::COMPLETED => 'completed',
        };
    }
}
```

#### AfterSaleType (售后类型)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 售后类型枚举
 * PRD键名: （售后模块专用）
 * 0=退货退款 / 1=补印 / 2=优惠货款 / 3=其他
 */
enum AfterSaleType: int
{
    case RETURN_REFUND = 0;
    case REPRINT       = 1;
    case DISCOUNT      = 2;
    case OTHER         = 3;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::RETURN_REFUND => '退货退款',
            self::REPRINT       => '补印',
            self::DISCOUNT      => '优惠货款',
            self::OTHER         => '其他',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否需要退货物流
     */
    public function requiresReturn(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::RETURN_REFUND;
    }

    /**
     * 是否需要重新生产
     */
    public function requiresReproduction(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::REPRINT;
    }

    /**
     * 是否直接退款（无需退货/补印）
     */
    public function isDirectRefund(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::DISCOUNT;
    }
}
```

#### AfterSaleReason (售后原因)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 售后原因枚举
 * PRD键名: （售后模块专用）
 * 0=下错单 / 1=印刷问题 / 2=裁切问题 / 3=后工问题 / 4=打包问题
 * 5=运输问题 / 6=误活 / 7=其他 / 8=贴错标签 / 9=原材料问题 / 10=少货
 */
enum AfterSaleReason: int
{
    case WRONG_ORDER     = 0;
    case PRINT_ISSUE     = 1;
    case CUTTING_ISSUE   = 2;
    case FINISHING_ISSUE = 3;
    case PACKING_ISSUE   = 4;
    case SHIPPING_ISSUE  = 5;
    case DELAY           = 6;
    case OTHER           = 7;
    case WRONG_LABEL     = 8;
    case MATERIAL_ISSUE  = 9;
    case SHORTAGE        = 10;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::WRONG_ORDER     => '下错单',
            self::PRINT_ISSUE     => '印刷问题（色差/模糊/裁切偏差）',
            self::CUTTING_ISSUE   => '裁切问题',
            self::FINISHING_ISSUE => '后工问题（覆膜/烫金/UV等）',
            self::PACKING_ISSUE   => '打包问题',
            self::SHIPPING_ISSUE  => '运输问题（物流损坏）',
            self::DELAY           => '误活（延期交货）',
            self::OTHER           => '其他问题',
            self::WRONG_LABEL     => '贴错标签',
            self::MATERIAL_ISSUE  => '原材料问题',
            self::SHORTAGE        => '少货问题',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否属于质量问题（可自动通过审核）
     */
    public function isQualityIssue(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [
            self::PRINT_ISSUE,
            self::CUTTING_ISSUE,
            self::FINISHING_ISSUE,
            self::PACKING_ISSUE,
            self::WRONG_LABEL,
            self::MATERIAL_ISSUE,
            self::SHORTAGE,
        ], true);
    }

    /**
     * 是否属于物流问题
     */
    public function isShippingIssue(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::SHIPPING_ISSUE;
    }
}
```

#### AfterSaleFlowStatus (AF 售后流程子状态)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 售后流程子状态（AF）
 * PRD键名: AF
 * 100=待退货 / 101=已退货
 */
enum AfterSaleFlowStatus: int
{
    case PENDING_RETURN = 100;
    case RETURNED       = 101;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PENDING_RETURN => '待退货',
            self::RETURNED       => '已退货',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 状态机：允许的目标状态校验
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::PENDING_RETURN, self::RETURNED] => true,

            default => false,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为终态
     */
    public function isTerminal(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::RETURNED;
    }
}
```

#### RefundMethod (退款方式)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 退款方式枚举
 * PRD键名: （支付模块扩展）
 * 0=无 / 1=原路退回 / 2=账户余额 / 3=银行转账 / 4=现金红包
 */
enum RefundMethod: int
{
    case NONE          = 0;
    case ORIGINAL      = 1;
    case WALLET        = 2;
    case BANK_TRANSFER = 3;
    case RED_PACKET    = 4;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NONE          => '无',
            self::ORIGINAL      => '原路退回',
            self::WALLET        => '账户余额',
            self::BANK_TRANSFER => '银行转账',
            self::RED_PACKET    => '现金红包',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否原路退回
     */
    public function isOriginal(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::ORIGINAL;
    }

    /**
     * 是否需要人工处理
     */
    public function requiresManualProcess(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::BANK_TRANSFER, self::RED_PACKET], true);
    }
}
```

### 6.40.3 数据模型与 Migration

#### after_sales 表

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('after_sales', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('售后单主键');
            $table->string('after_sale_sn', 32)->unique()->comment('售后单号（对外展示）');
            $table->foreignId('order_id')->constrained('orders')->comment('订单ID');
            $table->string('order_sn', 32)->comment('订单编号（冗余，便于售后列表展示）');
            $table->foreignId('customer_id')->constrained('customers')->comment('客户ID');

            // 售后类型与原因
            $table->tinyInteger('type')->default(0)->comment('售后类型: 0退货退款 1补印 2优惠货款 3其他');
            $table->tinyInteger('reason')->default(0)->comment('售后原因: 0下错单 1印刷问题 2裁切问题 ... 10少货');
            $table->string('reason_desc', 512)->nullable()->comment('原因详细描述');

            // EM 售后单据状态（独立状态空间，严禁与 FM/nM 混用）
            $table->string('status', 16)->default('submitted')->comment('售后状态(EM): submitted/processing/completed/suspended/revoked/cancelled');

            // AF 售后流程子状态（独立状态空间，非 FM 子集）
            $table->tinyInteger('process_flow_status')->nullable()->comment('售后流程状态(AF): 100待退货 101已退货');

            // 金额与退款
            $table->bigInteger('refund_amount')->default(0)->comment('退款金额（单位：分）');
            $table->tinyInteger('refund_method')->default(0)->comment('退款方式: 0无 1原路退回 2余额 3银行转账 4现金红包');

            // 凭证图片（最多9张）
            $table->json('evidence_urls')->nullable()->comment('凭证图片URL数组');

            // 退货物流信息
            $table->string('return_express_company', 64)->nullable()->comment('退货快递公司');
            $table->string('return_express_number', 64)->nullable()->comment('退货快递单号');
            $table->timestamp('return_submit_time')->nullable()->comment('退货物流提交时间');

            // 运营审核
            $table->foreignId('auditor_id')->nullable()->comment('审核人ID（管理员）');
            $table->timestamp('audited_at')->nullable()->comment('审核时间');
            $table->string('audit_remark', 512)->nullable()->comment('审核备注');
            $table->string('reject_reason', 512)->nullable()->comment('驳回原因');

            // 仓库验收
            $table->foreignId('warehouse_checker_id')->nullable()->comment('仓库验收人ID');
            $table->timestamp('warehouse_received_at')->nullable()->comment('仓库验收时间');
            $table->string('warehouse_remark', 512)->nullable()->comment('仓库验收备注');

            // 时间戳与关闭控制
            $table->timestamp('completed_at')->nullable()->comment('售后完成时间');
            $table->timestamp('customer_confirmed_at')->nullable()->comment('客户确认时间');
            $table->timestamp('closed_at')->nullable()->comment('售后关闭时间');
            $table->string('close_reason', 128)->nullable()->comment('关闭原因：auto_return_timeout/auto_confirm_timeout/customer_cancel/admin_cancel');
            $table->timestamps();

            // 索引策略
            $table->index('after_sale_sn', 'idx_after_sale_sn');
            $table->index('order_id', 'idx_order_id');
            $table->index('customer_id', 'idx_customer_id');
            $table->index('status', 'idx_status');
            $table->index(['type', 'status'], 'idx_type_status');
            $table->index('created_at', 'idx_created_at');
            $table->index(['status', 'closed_at'], 'idx_status_closed');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('after_sales');
    }
};
```

#### after_sale_items 表

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('after_sale_items', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('明细主键');
            $table->foreignId('after_sale_id')->constrained('after_sales')->comment('售后单ID');
            $table->foreignId('order_item_id')->nullable()->constrained('order_items')->comment('原订单明细ID');
            $table->foreignId('product_id')->nullable()->constrained('products')->comment('商品ID');
            $table->string('product_name', 255)->nullable()->comment('商品名称（冗余）');
            $table->integer('quantity')->default(0)->comment('售后数量');
            $table->tinyInteger('reason')->nullable()->comment('商品级售后原因枚举');
            $table->bigInteger('refund_amount')->default(0)->comment('该商品退款金额（单位：分）');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->index('after_sale_id', 'idx_after_sale_id');
            $table->index('order_item_id', 'idx_order_item_id');
            $table->index('product_id', 'idx_product_id');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('after_sale_items');
    }
};
```

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;

return new class extends Migration
{
```

```php
    {
        Schema::create('after_sale_logs', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('日志主键');

            $table->string('action', 64)->comment('操作动作：create/audit/return_submit/receive/complete/cancel/reject');
            $table->string('from_status', 16)->nullable()->comment('操作前EM状态');
            $table->string('to_status', 16)->nullable()->comment('操作后EM状态');
            $table->unsignedBigInteger('operator_id')->nullable()->comment('操作人ID');
            $table->string('operator_type', 16)->default('system')->comment('操作人类型: customer/admin/system');
            $table->string('remark', 512)->nullable()->comment('操作备注');
            $table->json('extra')->nullable()->comment('扩展信息（如审核结果、物流单号等）');
            $table->timestamp('created_at')->nullable();

            $table->index('after_sale_id', 'idx_after_sale_id');
            $table->index('action', 'idx_action');
            $table->index('created_at', 'idx_created_at');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('after_sale_logs');
    }
};
```

---

### 6.40.4 Eloquent 模型

#### AfterSale 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Models;

use App\Domains\Common\Castables\MoneyCast;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleReason;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use App\Enums\RefundMethod;
use App\Exceptions\InvalidStateTransitionException;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;

class AfterSale extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'after_sales';

    protected $fillable = [
        'after_sale_sn', 'order_id', 'order_sn', 'customer_id',
        'type', 'reason', 'reason_desc',
        'status', 'process_flow_status', 'refund_amount', 'refund_method',
        'evidence_urls', 'return_express_company', 'return_express_number', 'return_submit_time',
        'auditor_id', 'audited_at', 'audit_remark', 'reject_reason',
        'warehouse_checker_id', 'warehouse_received_at', 'warehouse_remark',
        'completed_at', 'closed_at', 'close_reason',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'status'              => AfterSaleStatus::class,
        'type'                => AfterSaleType::class,
        'reason'              => AfterSaleReason::class,
        'process_flow_status' => AfterSaleFlowStatus::class,
        'refund_method'       => RefundMethod::class,
        'refund_amount'       => MoneyCast::class,
        'evidence_urls'       => 'array',
        'return_submit_time'  => 'datetime',
        'audited_at'          => 'datetime',
        'warehouse_received_at' => 'datetime',
        'completed_at'        => 'datetime',
        'closed_at'           => 'datetime',
    ];

    protected static function boot(): void
    {
        parent::boot();

        static::creating(function (self $model) {
            if (empty($model->after_sale_sn)) {
                $model->after_sale_sn = 'AS' . now()->format('YmdHis') . strtoupper(Str::random(6));
            }
        });
    }

    // -- Relations --

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class, 'order_id');
    }

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class, 'customer_id');
    }

    public function items(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(AfterSaleItem::class, 'after_sale_id');
    }

    public function messages(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(AfterSaleMessage::class, 'after_sale_id');
    }

    public function logs(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(AfterSaleLog::class, 'after_sale_id');
    }

    // -- State Transition --

    /**
     * 状态流转（带合法性校验）
     *
     * @throws InvalidStateTransitionException
     */
    public function transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus $target, string $remark = ''): void
    {
        $current = $this->status;

        if (! $current->canTransitionTo($target)) {
            throw new InvalidStateTransitionException(
                "售后单 {$this->after_sale_sn} 不允许从 {$current->label()} 流转到 {$target->label()}"
            );
        }

        $previous = $current;
        $this->update([
            'status' => $target,
            'completed_at' => $target === AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED ? now() : $this->completed_at,
            'closed_at' => $target->isTerminal() && $this->closed_at === null ? now() : $this->closed_at,
        ]);

        event(new \App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleStatusChanged($this, $previous, $target, $remark));
    }

    /**
     * 售后流程子状态流转
     *
     * @throws InvalidStateTransitionException
     */
    public function transitionFlowTo(AfterSaleFlowStatus $target): void
    {
        $current = $this->process_flow_status;

        if ($current !== null && ! $current->canTransitionTo($target)) {
            throw new InvalidStateTransitionException(
                "售后单 {$this->after_sale_sn} 流程状态不允许从 {$current->label()} 流转到 {$target->label()}"
            );
        }

        $this->update(['process_flow_status' => $target]);
    }

    // -- Query Scopes --

    public function scopeOfCustomer($query, int $customerId)
    {
        return $query->where('customer_id', $customerId);
    }

    public function scopePending($query)
    {
        return $query->whereIn('status', [
            AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED->value,
        ]);
    }

    public function scopeTerminal($query)
    {
        return $query->whereIn('status', [
            AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value,
            AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED->value,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 超期未提交退货物流的售后单
     */
    public function scopeOverdueReturn($query, int $days = 15)
    {
        return $query->where('type', AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND->value)
            ->where('status', AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value)
            ->where('process_flow_status', AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN->value)
            ->whereNull('return_submit_time')
            ->where('audited_at', '<', now()->subDays($days));
    }

    // -- Helpers --

    /**
     * 当前客户侧展示状态
     */
    public function customerStatus(): string
    {
        // 被运营驳回时，对客户展示为 rejected
        if ($this->status === AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED && $this->close_reason === 'admin_reject') {
            return 'rejected';
        }

        return $this->status->toCustomerStatus($this->process_flow_status, $this->type);
    }

    /**
     * 是否已关闭
     */
    public function isClosed(): bool
    {
        return $this->status->isTerminal();
    }

    /**
     * 是否允许客户撤销
     */
    public function canBeRevokedByCustomer(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this->status, [
            AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED,
            AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED,
        ], true);
    }
}
```

```php
{

    {
        return $this->belongsTo(AfterSale::class, 'after_sale_id');

    {
        return $this->belongsTo(\App\Models\Product::class, 'product_id');
```

#### AfterSaleMessage 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class AfterSaleMessage extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'after_sale_messages';

    protected $fillable = [
        'after_sale_id', 'sender_type', 'sender_id', 'content', 'attachments', 'read_at',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'sender_type' => 'integer',
        'sender_id'   => 'integer',
        'attachments' => 'array',
        'read_at'     => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function afterSale(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(AfterSale::class, 'after_sale_id');
    }

    /**
     * 是否为系统消息
     */
    public function isSystem(): bool
    {
        return $this->sender_type === 3;
    }

    /**
     * 标记为已读
     */
    public function markAsRead(): void
    {
        if ($this->read_at === null) {
            $this->update(['read_at' => now()]);
        }
    }
}
```

---

### 6.40.5 Action 类

#### CreateAfterSaleAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleCreated;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleItem;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException;

/**
 * 创建售后申请
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-001 ~ FR-AFTER-004
 */
final class CreateAfterSaleAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{
     *   type: int,
     *   reason: int,
     *   reason_desc?: string,
     *   refund_amount: float,
     *   refund_method?: int,
     *   evidence_urls?: string[],
     *   items?: array<int, array{order_item_id: int, quantity: int, reason?: int, refund_amount?: float}>
     * } $data
     */
    public function execute(Order $order, array $data): AfterSale
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $data) {
            // 1. 校验订单是否允许售后（已完成状态且未过售后时效）
            $this->validateOrder($order);

            // 2. 校验凭证数量（最多9张）
            $evidenceUrls = $data['evidence_urls'] ?? [];
            if (count($evidenceUrls) > 9) {
                throw ValidationException::withMessages([
                    'evidence_urls' => '凭证图片最多上传9张',
                ]);
            }

            // 3. 创建售后单
            $afterSale = AfterSale::create([
                'order_id'         => $order->id,
                'order_sn'         => $order->order_sn,
                'customer_id'      => auth('customer')->id(),
                'type'             => $data['type'],
                'reason'           => $data['reason'],
                'reason_desc'      => $data['reason_desc'] ?? null,
                'status'           => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED,
                'refund_amount'    => $data['refund_amount'],
                'refund_method'    => $data['refund_method'] ?? 0,
                'evidence_urls'    => $evidenceUrls,
            ]);

            // 4. 创建售后明细
            if (! empty($data['items'])) {
                foreach ($data['items'] as $item) {
                    AfterSaleItem::create([
                        'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
                        'order_item_id' => $item['order_item_id'],
                        'quantity'      => $item['quantity'],
                        'reason'        => $item['reason'] ?? $data['reason'],
                        'refund_amount' => $item['refund_amount'] ?? 0,
                    ]);
                }
            }

            // 5. 记录操作日志
            AfterSaleLog::create([
                'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
                'action'        => 'create',
                'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
                'operator_id'   => auth('customer')->id(),
                'operator_type' => 'customer',
                'remark'        => '客户发起售后申请',
                'extra'         => ['type' => $data['type'], 'reason' => $data['reason']],
                'created_at'    => now(),
            ]);

            // 6. 触发事件
            event(new AfterSaleCreated($afterSale));

            return $afterSale->fresh('items');
        });
    }

    private function validateOrder(Order $order): void
    {
        // 仅已完成订单可申请售后（根据业务规则可调整）
        if ($order->status !== OrderStatus::COMPLETED) {
            throw new \DomainException('当前订单状态不允许申请售后');
        }

        // 校验售后时效（默认订单完成后15天内）
        $deadline = $order->completed_at?->addDays(15) ?? now()->addDays(15);
        if (now()->isAfter($deadline)) {
            throw new \DomainException('已超过售后申请时效');
        }

        // 校验是否已有进行中的售后
        $existing = AfterSale::where('order_id', $order->id)
            ->pending()
            ->exists();

        if ($existing) {
            throw new \DomainException('该订单已存在进行中的售后单');
        }
    }
}
```

#### AuditAfterSaleAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 运营审核售后申请
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-005 ~ FR-AFTER-007
 * 审核结果: approve(通过) / reject(不通过) / supplement(需补充材料)
 */
final class AuditAfterSaleAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{
     *   result: 'approve'|'reject'|'supplement',
     *   remark?: string,
     *   refund_method?: int,
     * } $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data): AfterSale
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($afterSale, $data) {
            $result = $data['result'];
            $remark = $data['remark'] ?? '';

            match ($result) {
                'approve'    => $this->handleApprove($afterSale, $data, $remark),
                'reject'     => $this->handleReject($afterSale, $remark),
                'supplement' => $this->handleSupplement($afterSale, $remark),
                default      => throw new \InvalidArgumentException('未知的审核结果'),
            };

            return $afterSale->fresh();
        });
    }

    private function handleApprove(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data, string $remark): void
    {
        // 更新退款方式（运营可指定）
        if (isset($data['refund_method'])) {
            $afterSale->update(['refund_method' => $data['refund_method']]);
        }

        // 根据售后类型设置后续状态
        match ($afterSale->type) {
            AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND => $this->startReturnFlow($afterSale, $remark),
            AfterSaleType::REPRINT       => $this->startReprintFlow($afterSale, $remark),
            AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT      => $this->startRefundFlow($afterSale, $remark),
            AfterSaleType::OTHER         => $this->startOtherFlow($afterSale, $remark),
        };
    }

    private function startReturnFlow(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        // 退货退款：进入处理中 + 待退货
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING, $remark);
        $afterSale->update(['process_flow_status' => AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN]);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "审核通过，待退货。{$remark}",
            'extra'         => ['flow_status' => AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN->value],
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function startReprintFlow(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        // 补印：直接进入处理中（排期生产）
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING, $remark);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "审核通过，进入补印排期。{$remark}",
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function startRefundFlow(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        // 优惠货款：直接进入处理中（退款中）
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING, $remark);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "审核通过，进入退款流程。{$remark}",
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function startOtherFlow(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING, $remark);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "审核通过，其他类型售后处理中。{$remark}",
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function handleReject(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        // 审核不通过：流转到已撤销（客户可重新提交）
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::REVOKED, $remark);
        $afterSale->update(['reject_reason' => $remark]);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::REVOKED->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "审核不通过。{$remark}",
            'extra'         => ['result' => 'reject'],
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }

    private function handleSupplement(AfterSale $afterSale, string $remark): void
    {
        // 需补充材料：挂起，等待客户补充
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED, $remark);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'audit',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "需补充材料：{$remark}",
            'extra'         => ['result' => 'supplement'],
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### SubmitReturnLogisticsAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;

/**
 * 客户提交退货物流单号
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-008
 */
final class SubmitReturnLogisticsAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{
     *   express_company: string,
     *   express_number: string,
     * } $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data): AfterSale
    {
        // 仅退货退款类型可提交物流
        if ($afterSale->type !== AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND) {
            throw new \DomainException('当前售后类型不支持退货物流');
        }

        // 校验状态
        if ($afterSale->status !== AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING
            || $afterSale->process_flow_status !== AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN
        ) {
            throw new \DomainException('当前售后状态不允许提交退货物流');
        }

        $afterSale->update([
            'return_express_company' => $data['express_company'],
            'return_express_number'  => $data['express_number'],
            'return_submit_time'     => now(),
        ]);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'return_submit',
            'from_status'   => $afterSale->status->value,
            'to_status'     => $afterSale->status->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('customer')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'customer',
            'remark'        => "提交退货物流：{$data['express_company']} {$data['express_number']}",
            'extra'         => [
                'express_company' => $data['express_company'],
                'express_number'  => $data['express_number'],
            ],
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);

        return $afterSale->fresh();
    }
}
```

#### WarehouseReceiveAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;

/**
 * 仓库验收退货
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-009
 */
final class WarehouseReceiveAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{
     *   result: 'pass'|'reject',
     *   remark?: string,
     * } $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data): AfterSale
    {
        if ($afterSale->type !== AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND) {
            throw new \DomainException('非退货退款类型无需仓库验收');
        }

        if ($afterSale->process_flow_status !== AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN) {
            throw new \DomainException('当前流程状态不允许仓库验收');
        }

        $result = $data['result'];
        $remark = $data['remark'] ?? '';

        if ($result === 'pass') {
            // 验收通过：流程状态变为已退货
            $afterSale->transitionFlowTo(AfterSaleFlowStatus::RETURNED);
            $afterSale->update([
                'warehouse_checker_id' => auth('admin')->id(),
                'warehouse_received_at' => now(),
                'warehouse_remark' => $remark,
            ]);

            AfterSaleLog::create([
                'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
                'action'        => 'receive',
                'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
                'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
                'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
                'operator_type' => 'admin',
                'remark'        => "仓库验收通过。{$remark}",
                'extra'         => ['flow_status' => AfterSaleFlowStatus::RETURNED->value],
                'created_at'    => now(),
            ]);
        } else {
            // 验收不通过：挂起，等待处理
            $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED, $remark);
            $afterSale->update([
                'warehouse_checker_id' => auth('admin')->id(),
                'warehouse_received_at' => now(),
                'warehouse_remark' => $remark,
            ]);

            AfterSaleLog::create([
                'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
                'action'        => 'receive',
                'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
                'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED->value,
                'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
                'operator_type' => 'admin',
                'remark'        => "仓库验收不通过。{$remark}",
                'extra'         => ['result' => 'reject'],
                'created_at'    => now(),
            ]);
        }

        return $afterSale->fresh();
    }
}
```

#### CompleteAfterSaleAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;

/**
 * 完成售后单
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-010
 * 触发条件：退款到账 / 补印发货 / 其他处理完毕
 */
final class CompleteAfterSaleAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{remark?: string} $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data = []): AfterSale
    {
        // 校验完成前置条件
        $this->validateCompletion($afterSale);

        $remark = $data['remark'] ?? '';

        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED, $remark);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'complete',
            'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "售后完成。{$remark}",
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);

        return $afterSale->fresh();
    }

    private function validateCompletion(AfterSale $afterSale): void
    {
        if ($afterSale->status !== AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING) {
            throw new \DomainException('仅处理中的售后单可标记完成');
        }

        // 退货退款必须已退货
        if ($afterSale->type === AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND
            && $afterSale->process_flow_status !== AfterSaleFlowStatus::RETURNED
        ) {
            throw new \DomainException('退货退款类型需仓库验收后方可完成');
        }
    }
}
```

#### CancelAfterSaleAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;

/**
 * 撤销/取消售后单
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-011
 * 客户可撤销自己提交的售后；运营可取消任意非终态售后
 */
final class CancelAfterSaleAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{
     *   reason?: string,
     *   auto?: bool,
     * } $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data = []): AfterSale
    {
        $isAuto = $data['auto'] ?? false;
        $reason = $data['reason'] ?? ($isAuto ? '系统自动关闭' : '手动取消');

        $operatorType = $isAuto ? 'system' : (auth('admin')->check() ? 'admin' : 'customer');
        $operatorId = $isAuto ? null : (auth('admin')->id() ?? auth('customer')->id());

        // 客户撤销：仅允许已提交/挂起状态
        if ($operatorType === 'customer' && ! $afterSale->canBeRevokedByCustomer()) {
            throw new \DomainException('当前售后状态不允许撤销');
        }

        // 运营取消 / 系统自动：仅允许非终态
        if ($afterSale->status->isTerminal()) {
            throw new \DomainException('已结束的售后单不可取消');
        }

        $previous = $afterSale->status;
        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED, $reason);
        $afterSale->update([
            'closed_at'    => now(),
            'close_reason' => $isAuto ? 'auto_return_timeout' : 'admin_cancel',
        ]);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'cancel',
            'from_status'   => $previous->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED->value,
            'operator_id'   => $operatorId,
            'operator_type' => $operatorType,
            'remark'        => $reason,
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);

        return $afterSale->fresh();
    }
}
```

#### RejectAfterSaleAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;

/**
 * 驳回售后申请（运营侧直接驳回，不进入撤销态）
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-006（驳回分支）
 * 与 AuditAfterSaleAction::handleReject 的区别：
 * - AuditAfterSaleAction 的 reject 会进入 REVOKED（客户可重新提交）
 * - RejectAfterSaleAction 直接进入 CANCELLED（终态，不可恢复）
 */
final class RejectAfterSaleAction
{
    /**
     * @param array{reason: string} $data
     */
    public function execute(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data): AfterSale
    {
        if ($afterSale->status->isTerminal()) {
            throw new \DomainException('已结束的售后单不可驳回');
        }

        $reason = $data['reason'];
        $previous = $afterSale->status;

        $afterSale->transitionTo(AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED, $reason);
        $afterSale->update([
            'reject_reason' => $reason,
            'closed_at'     => now(),
            'close_reason'  => 'admin_reject',
            'auditor_id'    => auth('admin')->id(),
            'audited_at'    => now(),
        ]);

        AfterSaleLog::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'action'        => 'reject',
            'from_status'   => $previous->value,
            'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED->value,
            'operator_id'   => auth('admin')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'admin',
            'remark'        => "运营驳回：{$reason}",
            'extra'         => ['result' => 'final_reject'],
            'created_at'    => now(),
        ]);

        return $afterSale->fresh();
    }
}
```



---

### 6.40.6 Service 类

#### AfterSaleService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Services;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleMessage;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection;

/**
 * 售后服务门面类
 * 聚合 Action 调用、查询、权限校验
 */
class AfterSaleService
{
    /**
     * 客户售后列表
     */
    public function customerList(int $customerId, array $filters = []): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $query = AfterSale::with(['items.product', 'order'])
            ->ofCustomer($customerId)
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if (! empty($filters['status'])) {
            $query->where('status', $filters['status']);
        }

        if (! empty($filters['type'])) {
            $query->where('type', $filters['type']);
        }

        return $query->paginate($filters['per_page'] ?? 15);
    }

    /**
     * 运营审核工作台列表
     */
    public function adminWorkbench(array $filters = []): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $query = AfterSale::with(['items.product', 'customer', 'order'])
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if (! empty($filters['status'])) {
            $query->where('status', $filters['status']);
        }

        if (! empty($filters['type'])) {
            $query->where('type', $filters['type']);
        }

        if (! empty($filters['date_from'])) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $filters['date_from']);
        }

        if (! empty($filters['date_to'])) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $filters['date_to']);
        }

        return $query->paginate($filters['per_page'] ?? 20);
    }

    /**
     * 售后详情（带权限校验）
     */
    public function detail(int $afterSaleId, ?int $customerId = null): AfterSale
    {
        $afterSale = AfterSale::with(['items.product', 'messages', 'logs', 'order'])
            ->findOrFail($afterSaleId);

        if ($customerId !== null && $afterSale->customer_id !== $customerId) {
            abort(403, '无权查看该售后单');
        }

        return $afterSale;
    }

    /**
     * 获取客户侧展示状态
     */
    public function customerStatus(AfterSale $afterSale): array
    {
        return [
            'status'        => $afterSale->customerStatus(),
            'status_label'  => $afterSale->status->label(),
            'flow_status'   => $afterSale->process_flow_status?->label(),
            'type_label'    => $afterSale->type->label(),
            'reason_label'  => $afterSale->reason->label(),
            'can_revoke'    => $afterSale->canBeRevokedByCustomer(),
            'can_return'    => $this->canSubmitReturn($afterSale),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 是否允许提交退货物流
     */
    private function canSubmitReturn(AfterSale $afterSale): bool
    {
        return $afterSale->type->requiresReturn()
            && $afterSale->status === AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING
            && $afterSale->process_flow_status?->value === \App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN->value
            && empty($afterSale->return_express_number);
    }

    /**
     * 统计客户未读系统消息数
     */
    public function unreadMessageCount(int $customerId): int
    {
        return AfterSaleMessage::whereHas('afterSale', function ($q) use ($customerId) {
            $q->where('customer_id', $customerId);
        })
            ->where('sender_type', '!=', 1) // 非客户发送
            ->whereNull('read_at')
            ->count();
    }
}
```

#### AfterSaleStatisticsService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Services;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleReason;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 售后统计服务
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-016 ~ FR-AFTER-020
 */
class AfterSaleStatisticsService
{
    /**
     * 按售后类型统计（数量 + 金额）
     *
     * @return array<int, array{type_label: string, count: int, total_refund: float}>
     */
    public function byType(?string $dateFrom = null, ?string $dateTo = null): array
    {
        $query = AfterSale::select('type', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'), DB::raw('SUM(refund_amount) as total_refund'))
            ->whereIn('status', [AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value, AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value])
            ->groupBy('type');

        if ($dateFrom) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $dateFrom);
        }
        if ($dateTo) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $dateTo);
        }

        return $query->get()->map(fn ($row) => [
            'type'         => $row->type,
            'type_label'   => AfterSaleType::from((int) $row->type)->label(),
            'count'        => (int) $row->count,
            'total_refund' => (float) ($row->total_refund / 100),
        ])->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 按售后原因统计
     *
     * @return array<int, array{reason_label: string, count: int, ratio: float}>
     */
    public function byReason(?string $dateFrom = null, ?string $dateTo = null): array
    {
        $query = AfterSale::select('reason', DB::raw('COUNT(*) as count'))
            ->groupBy('reason');

        if ($dateFrom) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $dateFrom);
        }
        if ($dateTo) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $dateTo);
        }

        $rows = $query->get();
        $total = $rows->sum('count');

        return $rows->map(fn ($row) => [
            'reason'       => $row->reason,
            'reason_label' => AfterSaleReason::tryFrom((int) $row->reason)?->label() ?? '未知',
            'count'        => (int) $row->count,
            'ratio'        => $total > 0 ? round((int) $row->count / $total, 4) : 0.0,
        ])->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 时效统计：平均处理时长（从提交到完成的小时数）
     */
    public function averageProcessHours(?string $dateFrom = null, ?string $dateTo = null): float
    {
        $query = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value)
            ->whereNotNull('completed_at');

        if ($dateFrom) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $dateFrom);
        }
        if ($dateTo) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $dateTo);
        }

        $avgSeconds = $query->avg(DB::raw('TIMESTAMPDIFF(SECOND, created_at, completed_at)'));

        return $avgSeconds !== null ? round((float) $avgSeconds / 3600, 2) : 0.0;
    }

    /**
     * SLA 超时统计：各类型超期数量
     *
     * @return array<string, array{sla_hours: int, overdue_count: int, total_count: int}>
     */
    public function slaOverdueStats(?string $dateFrom = null, ?string $dateTo = null): array
    {
        $query = AfterSale::whereIn('status', [
            AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value,
            AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value,
            AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED->value,
        ]);

        if ($dateFrom) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '>=', $dateFrom);
        }
        if ($dateTo) {
            $query->whereDate('created_at', '<=', $dateTo);
        }

        $items = $query->get();

        $stats = [
            'return'   => ['sla_hours' => 72,  'overdue_count' => 0, 'total_count' => 0], // 3天
            'reprint'  => ['sla_hours' => 168, 'overdue_count' => 0, 'total_count' => 0], // 7天
            'refund'   => ['sla_hours' => 48,  'overdue_count' => 0, 'total_count' => 0], // 2天
        ];

        foreach ($items as $item) {
            $typeKey = match ($item->type) {
                AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND => 'return',
                AfterSaleType::REPRINT       => 'reprint',
                AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT      => 'refund',
                default                      => null,
            };

            if ($typeKey === null) {
                continue;
            }

            $stats[$typeKey]['total_count']++;

            $endTime = $item->completed_at ?? $item->closed_at ?? now();
            $hours = $item->created_at->diffInHours($endTime);

            if ($hours > $stats[$typeKey]['sla_hours']) {
                $stats[$typeKey]['overdue_count']++;
            }
        }

        return $stats;
    }

    /**
     * 售后概览仪表盘数据
     */
    public function dashboardOverview(): array
    {
        return [
            'pending_audit'      => AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value)->count(),
            'processing'         => AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value)->count(),
            'suspended'          => AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED->value)->count(),
            'today_completed'    => AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value)
                ->whereDate('completed_at', today())
                ->count(),
            'today_created'      => AfterSale::whereDate('created_at', today())->count(),
            'avg_process_hours'  => $this->averageProcessHours(now()->subDays(30)->toDateString()),
        ];
    }
}
```

#### AfterSaleMessageService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Services;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleMessage;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;

/**
 * 售后留言服务
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-014 ~ FR-AFTER-015
 */
class AfterSaleMessageService
{
    /**
     * 发送留言
     *
     * @param array{
     *   content: string,
     *   attachments?: string[],
     * } $data
     */
    public function send(AfterSale $afterSale, array $data): AfterSaleMessage
    {
        $senderType = $this->resolveSenderType();
        $senderId = $senderType === 3 ? null : (auth('admin')->id() ?? auth('customer')->id());

        $message = AfterSaleMessage::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'sender_type'   => $senderType,
            'sender_id'     => $senderId,
            'content'       => $data['content'],
            'attachments'   => $data['attachments'] ?? [],
        ]);

        return $message;
    }

    /**
     * 获取留言列表（自动标记对方消息为已读）
     */
    public function list(AfterSale $afterSale, int $perPage = 20): LengthAwarePaginator
    {
        $messages = AfterSaleMessage::where('after_sale_id', $afterSale->id)
            ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
            ->paginate($perPage);

        // 自动标记对方发送的消息为已读
        $mySenderType = $this->resolveSenderType();
        AfterSaleMessage::where('after_sale_id', $afterSale->id)
            ->where('sender_type', '!=', $mySenderType)
            ->whereNull('read_at')
            ->update(['read_at' => now()]);

        return $messages;
    }

    /**
     * 发送系统进度通知消息
     */
    public function sendSystemNotice(AfterSale $afterSale, string $content): AfterSaleMessage
    {
        return AfterSaleMessage::create([
            'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            'sender_type'   => 3, // 系统
            'sender_id'     => null,
            'content'       => $content,
            'attachments'   => [],
        ]);
    }

    private function resolveSenderType(): int
    {
        if (auth('admin')->check()) {
            return 2;
        }
        if (auth('customer')->check()) {
            return 1;
        }

        return 3;
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

/**
```

#### 事件监听注册

```php
<?php

namespace App\Providers;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleCreated;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleStatusChanged;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleTimeoutWarning;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Listeners\SendAfterSaleNotification;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Listeners\SyncAfterSaleStatistics;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Listeners\AlertOverdueAfterSale;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Support\Providers\EventServiceProvider as ServiceProvider;

class EventServiceProvider extends ServiceProvider
{
    protected $listen = [
        AfterSaleCreated::class => [
            SendAfterSaleNotification::class,   // 发送客户/运营通知
            SyncAfterSaleStatistics::class,     // 更新统计缓存
        ],
        AfterSaleStatusChanged::class => [
            SendAfterSaleNotification::class,   // 发送进度变更通知
            SyncAfterSaleStatistics::class,     // 更新统计缓存
        ],
        AfterSaleTimeoutWarning::class => [
            AlertOverdueAfterSale::class,       // 运营告警 + 客户提醒
        ],
    ];
}
```

#### SendAfterSaleNotification 监听器

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Listeners;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleCreated;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleStatusChanged;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Services\AfterSaleMessageService;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use App\Services\SmsService;

class SendAfterSaleNotification
{
    public function __construct(
        private AfterSaleMessageService $messageService,
        private SmsService $smsService,
    ) {}

    public function handleCreated(AfterSaleCreated $event): void
    {
        $afterSale = $event->afterSale;

        // 1. 站内信通知
        $this->messageService->sendSystemNotice(
            $afterSale,
            "您的售后申请已提交，售后单号：{$afterSale->after_sale_sn}，我们会尽快处理。"
        );

        // 2. 短信通知（异步发送，不阻塞主流程）
        $this->sendSms(
            $afterSale,
            'aftersale_submitted',
            [
                'after_sale_sn' => $afterSale->after_sale_sn,
                'type'          => $afterSale->type->label(),
            ]
        );
    }

    public function handleStatusChanged(AfterSaleStatusChanged $event): void
    {
        $afterSale = $event->afterSale;
        $current = $event->currentStatus;

        // --- 站内信 ---
        $notice = match ($current) {
            AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING => match ($afterSale->type) {
                AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND => '您的退货退款申请已通过审核，请尽快寄回商品。',
                AfterSaleType::REPRINT       => '您的补印申请已通过审核，正在安排生产。',
                AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT      => '您的优惠货款申请已通过审核，正在安排退款。',
                default                      => '您的售后申请已进入处理中。',
            },
            AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED  => '您的售后申请需补充材料，请查看留言板。',
            AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED  => '您的售后单已处理完成，如有疑问请联系客服。',
            AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED  => "您的售后单已关闭，原因：{$afterSale->close_reason}。",
            AfterSaleStatus::REVOKED    => '您的售后申请未通过审核，可修改后重新提交。',
            default                     => null,
        };

        if ($notice !== null) {
            $this->messageService->sendSystemNotice($afterSale, $notice);
        }

        // --- 短信通知（关键状态才发短信，避免骚扰） ---
        $smsTemplate = match ($current) {
            AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING => 'aftersale_processing',
            AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED  => 'aftersale_completed',
            AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED  => 'aftersale_cancelled',
            AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED  => 'aftersale_suspended',
            default                     => null,
        };

        if ($smsTemplate !== null) {
            $this->sendSms(
                $afterSale,
                $smsTemplate,
                [
                    'after_sale_sn' => $afterSale->after_sale_sn,
                    'status'        => $current->label(),
                ]
            );
        }
    }

    /**
     * 发送售后短信（内部封装手机号获取与降级逻辑）
     */
    private function sendSms(\App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale $afterSale, string $templateCode, array $params): void
    {
        // 获取客户手机号
        $phone = $afterSale->customer?->mobile_phone;
        if (empty($phone)) {
            Log::warning('[AfterSaleNotify] 客户手机号为空，跳过短信发送', [
                'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
            ]);
            return;
        }

        // 异步投递到队列，避免阻塞事件处理
        dispatch(function () use ($phone, $templateCode, $params) {
            $this->smsService->send($phone, $templateCode, $params);
        })->onQueue('sms');
    }
}
```

#### AlertOverdueAfterSale 监听器

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Listeners;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleTimeoutWarning;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Services\AfterSaleMessageService;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Notification;

class AlertOverdueAfterSale
{
    public function __construct(
        private AfterSaleMessageService $messageService,
    ) {}

    public function handle(AfterSaleTimeoutWarning $event): void
    {
        $afterSale = $event->afterSale;
        $type = $event->warningType;
        $hours = $event->overdueHours;

        // 记录告警日志
        Log::warning('[AfterSaleSLA] 售后单超时', [
            'after_sale_sn' => $afterSale->after_sale_sn,
            'type'          => $type,
            'overdue_hours' => $hours,
        ]);

        // 客户提醒
        $notice = match ($type) {
            'return_overdue'   => "提醒：您的退货物流已超期 {$hours} 小时，售后单即将自动关闭。",
            'reprint_overdue'  => "提醒：您的补印订单处理已超期 {$hours} 小时，请联系客服。",
            'refund_overdue'   => "提醒：您的退款处理已超期 {$hours} 小时，请联系客服。",
            'confirm_overdue'  => '提醒：您的售后单已完成超过7天，系统即将自动确认关闭。',
            default            => "提醒：您的售后单存在超时（{$hours}小时），请联系客服。",
        };

        $this->messageService->sendSystemNotice($afterSale, $notice);

        // 运营告警（可通过站内信/钉钉/企业微信发送）
        // Notification::send($admins, new AfterSaleOverdueAlert($afterSale, $type, $hours));
    }
}
```

#### Queue Job

##### AfterSaleSlaMonitorJob

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Jobs;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleTimeoutWarning;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 售后SLA超时监控Job
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-015
 * 调度频率：每4小时执行一次
 */
class AfterSaleSlaMonitorJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    /**
     * 各类型SLA承诺时长（小时）
     */
    private const SLA_HOURS = [
        'audit'   => 48,  // 审核SLA：48小时
        'return'  => 72,  // 退货验收SLA：3天 = 72小时
        'reprint' => 168, // 补印SLA：7天 = 168小时
        'refund'  => 48,  // 退款SLA：2天 = 48小时
        'confirm' => 168, // 完成确认SLA：7天 = 168小时
    ];

    /**
     * 提醒阈值比例（50%）
     */
    private const REMINDER_RATIO = 0.5;

    public function handle(): void
    {
        Log::info('[AfterSaleSlaMonitor] SLA扫描开始');

        $this->scanAuditOverdue();
        $this->scanProcessingOverdue();
        $this->scanCompletedUnconfirmed();

        Log::info('[AfterSaleSlaMonitor] SLA扫描结束');
    }

    /**
     * 扫描1：超48小时未审核（submitted状态）
     */
    private function scanAuditOverdue(): void
    {
        $threshold = now()->subHours(self::SLA_HOURS['audit']);
        $reminderThreshold = now()->subHours(self::SLA_HOURS['audit'] * self::REMINDER_RATIO);

        $items = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::SUBMITTED->value)
            ->where('created_at', '<', $reminderThreshold)
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            $hours = $afterSale->created_at->diffInHours(now());
            $isAlert = $afterSale->created_at < $threshold;

            event(new AfterSaleTimeoutWarning(
                $afterSale,
                $isAlert ? 'audit_overdue' : 'audit_reminder',
                (int) $hours
            ));
        }
    }

    /**
     * 扫描2：处理中超时（processing状态，按类型区分）
     */
    private function scanProcessingOverdue(): void
    {
        $items = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value)
            ->whereNotNull('audited_at')
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            $slaHours = $this->resolveSlaHours($afterSale);
            if ($slaHours === null) {
                continue;
            }

            $threshold = now()->subHours($slaHours);
            $reminderThreshold = now()->subHours($slaHours * self::REMINDER_RATIO);

            // 未到达提醒阈值，跳过
            if ($afterSale->audited_at >= $reminderThreshold) {
                continue;
            }

            $hours = $afterSale->audited_at->diffInHours(now());
            $isAlert = $afterSale->audited_at < $threshold;

            $warningType = match ($afterSale->type) {
                AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND => $isAlert ? 'return_overdue' : 'return_reminder',
                AfterSaleType::REPRINT       => $isAlert ? 'reprint_overdue' : 'reprint_reminder',
                AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT      => $isAlert ? 'refund_overdue' : 'refund_reminder',
                default                      => $isAlert ? 'processing_overdue' : 'processing_reminder',
            };

            event(new AfterSaleTimeoutWarning($afterSale, $warningType, (int) $hours));
        }
    }

    /**
     * 扫描3：完成后超7天未确认（completed状态超7天）
     */
    private function scanCompletedUnconfirmed(): void
    {
        $threshold = now()->subHours(self::SLA_HOURS['confirm']);

        $items = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value)
            ->whereNotNull('completed_at')
            ->where('completed_at', '<', $threshold)
            ->whereNull('closed_at') // 未关闭的才需要提醒
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            $hours = $afterSale->completed_at->diffInHours(now());

            event(new AfterSaleTimeoutWarning(
                $afterSale,
                'confirm_overdue',
                (int) $hours
            ));
        }
    }

    /**
     * 根据售后类型和流程状态解析SLA时长
     */
    private function resolveSlaHours(AfterSale $afterSale): ?int
    {
        return match ($afterSale->type) {
            AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND => self::SLA_HOURS['return'],
            AfterSaleType::REPRINT       => self::SLA_HOURS['reprint'],
            AfterSaleType::DISCOUNT      => self::SLA_HOURS['refund'],
            default                      => null,
        };
    }
}
```

##### AfterSaleMonitorJob

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\AfterSale\Jobs;

use App\Domains\AfterSale\Actions\CancelAfterSaleAction;
use App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSale;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleFlowStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleStatus;
use App\Enums\AfterSaleType;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 售后自动关闭监控Job
 *
 * PRD: FR-AFTER-012-A（自动关闭）
 * 调度频率：每小时执行一次
 */
class AfterSaleMonitorJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(
        private CancelAfterSaleAction $cancelAction,
    ) {}

    public function handle(): void
    {
        Log::info('[AfterSaleMonitor] 自动关闭扫描开始');

        $this->closeOverdueReturn();
        $this->closeOverdueConfirm();
        $this->closeOverdueSupplement();

        Log::info('[AfterSaleMonitor] 自动关闭扫描结束');
    }

    /**
     * 场景1：超15天未提交退货物流 → 自动关闭
     */
    private function closeOverdueReturn(): void
    {
        $items = AfterSale::where('type', AfterSaleType::RETURN_REFUND->value)
            ->where('status', AfterSaleStatus::PROCESSING->value)
            ->where('process_flow_status', AfterSaleFlowStatus::PENDING_RETURN->value)
            ->whereNull('return_submit_time')
            ->where('audited_at', '<', now()->subDays(15))
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            Log::info("[AfterSaleMonitor] 售后单 {$afterSale->after_sale_sn} 超时未退货，自动关闭");

            $this->cancelAction->execute($afterSale, [
                'auto'   => true,
                'reason' => '超时未寄回退货商品，系统自动关闭',
            ]);

            // 更新关闭原因（CancelAfterSaleAction默认用auto_return_timeout）
            $afterSale->update(['close_reason' => 'auto_return_timeout']);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 场景2：完成后超7天未确认 → 自动关闭（COMPLETED → CANCELLED）
     *
     * ⚠️ 注意：此场景需要状态机支持 COMPLETED → CANCELLED 流转
     */
    private function closeOverdueConfirm(): void
    {
        $items = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value)
            ->whereNotNull('completed_at')
            ->where('completed_at', '<', now()->subDays(7))
            ->whereNull('closed_at')
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            Log::info("[AfterSaleMonitor] 售后单 {$afterSale->after_sale_sn} 完成后超7天未确认，自动关闭");

            // 状态机限制：COMPLETED不能直接→CANCELLED，需先绕过或修改状态机
            // 方案A（推荐）：直接update绕过状态机校验（自动关闭属于系统强制作业）
            $afterSale->update([
                'status'      => AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED,
                'closed_at'   => now(),
                'close_reason'=> 'auto_confirm_timeout',
            ]);

            // 记录日志
            \App\Domains\AfterSale\Models\AfterSaleLog::create([
                'after_sale_id' => $afterSale->id,
                'action'        => 'cancel',
                'from_status'   => AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED->value,
                'to_status'     => AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED->value,
                'operator_type' => 'system',
                'remark'        => '完成后超7天未确认，系统自动关闭',
                'created_at'    => now(),
            ]);

            // 触发事件（可选，用于通知客户）
            event(new \App\Domains\AfterSale\Events\AfterSaleStatusChanged(
                $afterSale,
                AfterSaleStatus::COMPLETED,
                AfterSaleStatus::CANCELLED,
                '系统自动关闭：完成后超7天未确认'
            ));
        }
    }

    /**
     * 场景3：挂起超7天未补充材料 → 自动关闭
     */
    private function closeOverdueSupplement(): void
    {
        // 挂起状态且updated_at（最后更新时间）超过7天
        $items = AfterSale::where('status', AfterSaleStatus::SUSPENDED->value)
            ->where('updated_at', '<', now()->subDays(7))
            ->get();

        foreach ($items as $afterSale) {
            Log::info("[AfterSaleMonitor] 售后单 {$afterSale->after_sale_sn} 挂起超7天未补充，自动关闭");

            $this->cancelAction->execute($afterSale, [
                'auto'   => true,
                'reason' => '挂起超7天未补充材料，系统自动关闭',
            ]);

            $afterSale->update(['close_reason' => 'auto_supplement_timeout']);
        }
    }
}
```

---

### 6.40.8 关键业务规则

#### 1. 售后申请规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-001 | **订单状态限制**：仅已完成的订单可申请售后（`orders.status = completed`），生产中的订单不可售后。 |
| R-AFTER-002 | **时效限制**：订单完成后 **15个自然日** 内可申请售后，超期系统自动拒绝。 |
| R-AFTER-003 | **并发限制**：同一订单仅允许存在 **1个进行中** 的售后单（`status IN (submitted, processing, suspended)`），终态售后不影响新申请。 |
| R-AFTER-004 | **凭证限制**：凭证图片最多上传 **9张**，单张不超过 5MB，格式为 jpg/png。 |
| R-AFTER-005 | **金额限制**：退款金额不得超过原订单实付金额，且不能超过各商品退款金额之和。 |

#### 2. 审核规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-006 | **自动通过**：售后原因属于质量问题（印刷问题、裁切问题、后工问题、打包问题、贴错标签、原材料问题、少货）时，系统可配置自动通过审核。 |
| R-AFTER-007 | **需补充材料**：凭证不清晰、信息不完整时，运营可挂起并要求客户补充材料。 |
| R-AFTER-008 | **审核不通过**：客户原因（下错单、误活）且超过时效的，运营可驳回进入 `REVOKED`，客户可修改后重新提交。 |
| R-AFTER-009 | **终审驳回**：欺诈、恶意售后等特殊情况，运营可直接 `RejectAfterSaleAction` 进入 `CANCELLED` 终态。 |

#### 3. 退货物流规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-010 | **物流必填**：退货退款审核通过后，客户需在 **15个自然日** 内填写退货物流单号，否则自动关闭。 |
| R-AFTER-011 | **单号校验**：快递单号格式基础校验（长度 6-30 位字母数字），不支持重复提交。 |
| R-AFTER-012 | **仓库验收**：仓库收到退货后需在系统中确认，验收不通过可挂起并注明原因。 |

#### 4. 退款规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-013 | **退款路径优先级**：1.原路退回 > 2.余额 > 3.银行转账 > 4.现金红包。运营可 override。 |
| R-AFTER-014 | **退款时效**：审核通过后，退款需在 **2个工作日** 内到账（原路退回受支付渠道限制）。 |
| R-AFTER-015 | **无需退货**：优惠货款类型直接退款，无需客户寄回商品。 |

#### 5. 补印规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-016 | **排期生产**：补印审核通过后，自动生成生产工单，复用订单 FM 状态流转。 |
| R-AFTER-017 | **补印时效**：补印需在 **7个自然日** 内完成生产并发货。 |
| R-AFTER-018 | **不重复收款**：补印订单不收取额外费用，但需在系统中标记为补单（`order_sign` 补单位）。 |

#### 6. 自动关闭规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-019 | **退货超时**：客户提交售后后 **15天** 未填写退货物流单号 → 系统自动取消（`close_reason = auto_return_timeout`）。 |
| R-AFTER-020 | **确认超时**：售后单完成后 **7天** 客户未提出异议 → 系统自动关闭（`close_reason = auto_confirm_timeout`）。 |
| R-AFTER-021 | **挂起超时**：挂起状态超过 **7天** 客户未补充材料 → 系统自动取消（`close_reason = auto_supplement_timeout`）。 |

#### 7. SLA 监控规则

| 规则编号 | 规则描述 |
|----------|----------|
| R-AFTER-022 | **退货SLA**：退货退款从审核通过到仓库验收，承诺 **3天** 内完成（不含物流运输时间）。 |
| R-AFTER-023 | **补印SLA**：补印从审核通过到发货，承诺 **7天** 内完成。 |
| R-AFTER-024 | **退款SLA**：退款从审核通过到资金到账，承诺 **2天** 内完成。 |
| R-AFTER-025 | **预警阈值**：SLA 完成前 50% 时间发送预警，超期后每24小时重复提醒。 |

---

#### 售后申请时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    actor Customer as 客户
    participant API as API Gateway
    participant CreateAction as CreateAfterSaleAction
    participant AfterSale as AfterSale模型
    participant DB as Database
    participant Event as EventDispatcher
    participant Listener as SendAfterSaleNotification

    Customer->>API: POST /api/after-sales (订单ID, 类型, 原因, 凭证)
    API->>CreateAction: execute(order, data)
    CreateAction->>DB: 校验订单状态 + 售后时效
    alt 校验失败
        CreateAction-->>API: DomainException
        API-->>Customer: 400 错误
    else 校验通过
        CreateAction->>DB: INSERT after_sales (事务)
        CreateAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_items
        CreateAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
        CreateAction->>AfterSale: transitionTo(SUBMITTED)
        AfterSale->>AfterSale: canTransitionTo校验
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE status
        CreateAction->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleCreated)
        Event->>Listener: handle()
        Listener->>DB: INSERT after_sale_messages (系统通知)
        CreateAction-->>API: AfterSaleDTO
        API-->>Customer: 201 售后单创建成功
    end
```

#### 售后审核时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    actor Admin as 运营人员
    participant API as API Gateway
    participant AuditAction as AuditAfterSaleAction
    participant AfterSale as AfterSale模型
    participant DB as Database
    participant Event as EventDispatcher

    Admin->>API: POST /api/admin/after-sales/{id}/audit (result, remark)
    API->>AuditAction: execute(afterSale, data)
    AuditAction->>AfterSale: transitionTo(PROCESSING/SUSPENDED/REVOKED)
    AfterSale->>AfterSale: canTransitionTo校验
    alt 非法流转
        AfterSale-->>AuditAction: InvalidStateTransitionException
        AuditAction-->>API: 422
        API-->>Admin: 状态流转非法
    else 合法流转
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE status + timestamps
        AuditAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
        AuditAction->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleStatusChanged)
        Event->>Event: 发送通知 / 更新统计
        AuditAction-->>API: AfterSaleDTO
        API-->>Admin: 200 审核完成
    end
```

#### 退货物流 + 仓库验收时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    actor Customer as 客户
    actor Warehouse as 仓库人员
    participant API as API Gateway
    participant ReturnAction as SubmitReturnLogisticsAction
    participant ReceiveAction as WarehouseReceiveAction
    participant AfterSale as AfterSale模型
    participant DB as Database
    participant Event as EventDispatcher

    %% 客户提交物流
    Customer->>API: POST /api/after-sales/{id}/return (快递公司, 单号)
    API->>ReturnAction: execute(afterSale, data)
    ReturnAction->>AfterSale: 校验状态(PROCESSING + PENDING_RETURN)
    ReturnAction->>DB: UPDATE return_express_company, return_express_number
    ReturnAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
    ReturnAction-->>API: AfterSaleDTO
    API-->>Customer: 200 物流提交成功

    %% 仓库验收
    Warehouse->>API: POST /api/admin/after-sales/{id}/receive (result, remark)
    API->>ReceiveAction: execute(afterSale, data)
    ReceiveAction->>AfterSale: 校验流程状态(PENDING_RETURN)
    alt 验收通过
        ReceiveAction->>AfterSale: transitionFlowTo(RETURNED)
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE process_flow_status
        ReceiveAction->>DB: UPDATE warehouse_received_at, warehouse_remark
    else 验收不通过
        ReceiveAction->>AfterSale: transitionTo(SUSPENDED)
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE status
    end
    ReceiveAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
    ReceiveAction->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleStatusChanged)
    ReceiveAction-->>API: AfterSaleDTO
    API-->>Warehouse: 200 验收处理完成
```

#### 自动关闭时序图（定时任务）

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Schedule as Laravel Schedule
    participant Monitor as AfterSaleMonitorJob
    participant AfterSale as AfterSale模型
    participant CancelAction as CancelAfterSaleAction
    participant DB as Database
    participant Event as EventDispatcher

    Schedule->>Monitor: 每小时执行
    Monitor->>DB: 查询超15天未退货的售后单
    loop 遍历超期售后单
        Monitor->>AfterSale: 加载模型
        Monitor->>CancelAction: execute(afterSale, [auto => true, reason => '超时未寄回'])
        CancelAction->>AfterSale: transitionTo(CANCELLED)
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE status, closed_at, close_reason
        CancelAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
        CancelAction->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleStatusChanged)
    end

    Monitor->>DB: 查询完成后超7天未确认的售后单
    loop 遍历超期售后单
        Monitor->>CancelAction: execute(afterSale, [auto => true, reason => '完成后超时自动关闭'])
        CancelAction->>AfterSale: transitionTo(CANCELLED)
        AfterSale->>DB: UPDATE status, closed_at, close_reason
        CancelAction->>DB: INSERT after_sale_logs
        CancelAction->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleStatusChanged)
    end
```

#### SLA 超时预警时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Schedule as Laravel Schedule
    participant SLAJob as AfterSaleSlaMonitorJob
    participant AfterSale as AfterSale模型
    participant Event as EventDispatcher
    participant Listener as AlertOverdueAfterSale
    participant DB as Database

    Schedule->>SLAJob: 每4小时执行
    SLAJob->>DB: 查询处理中超时的售后单
    loop 遍历超时售后单
        SLAJob->>AfterSale: 计算超时时长
        SLAJob->>Event: dispatch(AfterSaleTimeoutWarning)
        Event->>Listener: handle()
        Listener->>DB: INSERT after_sale_messages (系统提醒客户)
        Listener->>Listener: 记录告警日志 / 通知运营
    end
```

> 本补充章节完整覆盖 PRD 模块十四（FR-AFTER-001 ~ FR-AFTER-020）全部需求，与《怡安印刷商城-系统设计方案_PHP8.5_Laravel13.md》第4章枚举、第5章数据库架构、第6章业务逻辑保持严格一致。
