## 6.41 物流与配送子系统设计 (LogisticsService)

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：第三方快递/专线物流为核心，多地址运费折扣，轨迹同步异步化，配送区域围栏化管理。
> **边界说明**：门店自营配送已在 6.14/6.39 中覆盖，本节聚焦第三方快递/专线物流。

---

### 6.41.1 设计概述

物流与配送子系统承担订单出仓后的全链路物流管理能力，核心设计原则如下：

1. **多地址运费折扣**：首地址按标准运费计算，附加地址享折扣（如 7 折），公式为 `totalFee = 首地址标准运费 + Σ(附加地址标准运费 × 折扣率)`。
2. **物流状态机内聚**：`DeliveryStatus` Backed Enum 提供 `canTransitionTo()` 与 `isTerminal()` 方法，禁止在 Service / Controller 中分散判断。
3. **轨迹同步异步化**：对接快递鸟/快递100/各家官方 API，通过 `SyncExpressTracksJob` 定时拉取，缓存 24 小时，超 48 小时无更新自动标记异常。
4. **配送区域围栏化**：大区+小区+多边形围栏（经纬度数组），支持地理编码与配送限制检查。
5. **专线与快递双轨**：`DeliveryType` 区分专线（自有物流）、快递（第三方）、云仓、门店自提，专线轨迹通过自有系统同步。
6. **金额统一 MoneyCast**：所有运费、费用字段使用 `MoneyCast`（分↔元），与订单系统保持一致。

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph 客户端
        C1[下单选择配送] --> C2[多地址设置]
        C2 --> C3[运费计算]
        C3 --> C4[物流轨迹查询]
    end

    subgraph 运营端
        O1[快递公司管理] --> O2[配送区域配置]
        O2 --> O3[异常预警处理]
    end

    subgraph 领域层
        A1[CalculateShippingFeeAction] --> S1[ShippingFeeCalculator]
        A2[CreateDeliveryAction] --> S2[LogisticsService]
        A3[SyncExpressTracksAction] --> S3[ExpressTrackSyncService]
        S3 --> J1[SyncExpressTracksJob]
        S4[DeliveryAreaService] --> O2
    end

    C1 --> S1
    C2 --> A2
    C4 --> S3
    O1 --> S2
```

---

### 6.41.2 枚举定义

#### DeliveryStatus (物流状态)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 物流状态枚举
 * PRD键名: order_deliveries.status
 * 0=待揽收 / 1=已揽收 / 2=运输中 / 3=派送中 / 4=已签收 / 5=异常 / 6=已退回
 */
enum DeliveryStatus: int
{
    case PENDING_PICKUP = 0;   // 待揽收
    case PICKED_UP      = 1;   // 已揽收
    case IN_TRANSIT     = 2;   // 运输中
    case OUT_FOR_DELIVERY = 3; // 派送中
    case DELIVERED      = 4;   // 已签收
    case EXCEPTION      = 5;   // 异常
    case RETURNED       = 6;   // 已退回

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PENDING_PICKUP   => '待揽收',
            self::PICKED_UP        => '已揽收',
            self::IN_TRANSIT       => '运输中',
            self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY => '派送中',
            self::DELIVERED        => '已签收',
            self::EXCEPTION        => '异常',
            self::RETURNED         => '已退回',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否允许状态流转到目标状态
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            // 待揽收 -> 已揽收 / 异常
            [self::PENDING_PICKUP, self::PICKED_UP],
            [self::PENDING_PICKUP, self::EXCEPTION] => true,

            // 已揽收 -> 运输中 / 异常
            [self::PICKED_UP, self::IN_TRANSIT],
            [self::PICKED_UP, self::EXCEPTION] => true,

            // 运输中 -> 派送中 / 异常 / 已退回
            [self::IN_TRANSIT, self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY],
            [self::IN_TRANSIT, self::EXCEPTION],
            [self::IN_TRANSIT, self::RETURNED] => true,

            // 派送中 -> 已签收 / 异常 / 已退回
            [self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY, self::DELIVERED],
            [self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY, self::EXCEPTION],
            [self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY, self::RETURNED] => true,

            // 异常 -> 运输中 / 已退回（恢复或退回）
            [self::EXCEPTION, self::IN_TRANSIT],
            [self::EXCEPTION, self::RETURNED] => true,

            // 已退回为终态
            default => false,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为终态
     */
    public function isTerminal(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::DELIVERED, self::RETURNED], true);
    }

    /**
     * 映射为客户侧展示状态（对应 orders.out_status_name）
     */
    public function toCustomerOutStatus(): int
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PENDING_PICKUP   => 4, // 已发货
            self::PICKED_UP        => 4, // 已发货
            self::IN_TRANSIT       => 8, // 配送中
            self::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY => 8, // 配送中
            self::DELIVERED        => 9, // 已完成
            self::EXCEPTION        => 8, // 配送中（异常保持配送中，客服跟进）
            self::RETURNED         => 5, // 已取消（退回视同取消）
        };
    }
}
```

#### DeliveryType (配送方式)

> **注意**：本枚举已在 SDD 第 4.3 节（ch01）定义，此处完整复现以确保一致性。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 配送方式枚举
 * PRD键名: iM / deliveryType
 * 0=专线 / 1=快递 / 2=云仓 / 3=门店自提
 */
enum DeliveryType: int
{
    case SPECIAL_LINE    = 0; // 专线物流
    case EXPRESS         = 1; // 快递
    case CLOUD_WAREHOUSE = 2; // 云仓
    case SELF_PICKUP     = 3; // 门店自提

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SPECIAL_LINE    => '专线物流',
            self::EXPRESS         => '快递',
            self::CLOUD_WAREHOUSE => '云仓配送',
            self::SELF_PICKUP     => '门店自提',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为第三方快递（需要对接快递鸟/快递100）
     */
    public function isThirdPartyExpress(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::EXPRESS;
    }

    /**
     * 是否需要物流轨迹同步
     */
    public function requiresTrackSync(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::SPECIAL_LINE, self::EXPRESS, self::CLOUD_WAREHOUSE], true);
    }
}
```

#### ExpressCompany (快递公司)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 快递公司枚举
 * PRD: 支持顺丰、圆通、中通等多家快递
 */
enum ExpressCompany: string
{
    case SF         = 'shunfeng';    // 顺丰速运
    case YTO        = 'yuantong';    // 圆通速递
    case ZTO        = 'zhongtong';   // 中通快递
    case STO        = 'shentong';    // 申通快递
    case EMS        = 'ems';         // EMS
    case YUNDA      = 'yunda';       // 韵达速递
    case JD         = 'jd';          // 京东物流
    case DEBANG     = 'debang';      // 德邦快递
    case JT         = 'jitu';        // 极兔速递
    case SPECIAL    = 'zhuanxian';   // 怡安专线（自有）

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SF      => '顺丰速运',
            self::YTO     => '圆通速递',
            self::ZTO     => '中通快递',
            self::STO     => '申通快递',
            self::EMS     => 'EMS',
            self::YUNDA   => '韵达速递',
            self::JD      => '京东物流',
            self::DEBANG  => '德邦快递',
            self::JT      => '极兔速递',
            self::SPECIAL => '怡安专线',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 快递鸟/快递100 对应的查询编码
     */
    public function queryCode(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SF      => 'SF',
            self::YTO     => 'YTO',
            self::ZTO     => 'ZTO',
            self::STO     => 'STO',
            self::EMS     => 'EMS',
            self::YUNDA   => 'YD',
            self::JD      => 'JD',
            self::DEBANG  => 'DBK',
            self::JT      => 'JT',
            self::SPECIAL => 'YIAN',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否支持电子面单
     */
    public function supportsElectronicWaybill(): bool
    {
        return $this !== self::SPECIAL;
    }
}
```

#### DeliveryTimeliness (配送时效)

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 配送时效枚举（位掩码）
 * PRD键名: GM / deliveryTimeliness
 * 1=当日发 / 2=同城快递 / 4=半日达
 */
enum DeliveryTimeliness: int
{
    case SAME_DAY_SHIP  = 1; // 当日发
    case SAME_CITY      = 2; // 同城快递
    case HALF_DAY       = 4; // 半日达

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SAME_DAY_SHIP => '当日发',
            self::SAME_CITY     => '同城快递',
            self::HALF_DAY      => '半日达',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 解码位掩码为枚举数组
     */
    public static function decode(int $mask): array
    {
        $result = [];
        foreach (self::cases() as $case) {
            if ($mask & $case->value) {
                $result[] = $case;
            }
        }
        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * 编码枚举数组为位掩码
     */
    public static function encode(array $cases): int
    {
        $mask = 0;
        foreach ($cases as $case) {
            if ($case instanceof self) {
                $mask |= $case->value;
            }
        }
        return $mask;
    }

    /**
     * 位掩码是否包含当前标志
     */
    public function inMask(int $mask): bool
    {
        return (bool) ($mask & $this->value);
    }
}
```

```php
        return match ($this) {
            self::DELIVERY => '收货地址',
            self::INVOICE  => '发票地址',
            self::RETURN   => '退货地址',

```

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('order_deliveries', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('物流主键');
            $table->foreignId('order_id')->constrained('orders')->comment('订单ID');
            $table->string('express_company', 64)->nullable()->comment('快递公司');
            $table->string('tracking_no', 64)->nullable()->comment('快递单号/物流单号');
            $table->tinyInteger('delivery_type')->default(1)->comment('配送方式: 0专线 1快递 2云仓 3门店自提');
            $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(0)->comment('物流状态: 0待揽收 1已揽收 2运输中 3派送中 4已签收 5异常 6已退回');
            $table->tinyInteger('factory_code')->nullable()->comment('发货工厂代码(dM)');
            $table->timestamp('delivery_time')->nullable()->comment('预计配送时间');
            $table->timestamp('signed_at')->nullable()->comment('签收时间');
            $table->string('sign_image', 500)->nullable()->comment('电子签名图片URL');
            $table->tinyInteger('sign_type')->default(0)->comment('签收方式: 0本人签收 1代收 2电子签名');
            $table->string('signer_name', 50)->nullable()->comment('签收人姓名');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->index('order_id', 'idx_order_id');
            $table->index('tracking_no', 'idx_tracking_no');
            $table->index('status', 'idx_status');
            $table->index('factory_code', 'idx_factory_code');
            $table->index('delivery_type', 'idx_delivery_type');
            $table->index(['order_id', 'delivery_type'], 'idx_order_delivery_type');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('order_deliveries');
    }
};
```

#### delivery_areas 表（配送区域管理）

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('delivery_areas', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('区域主键');
            $table->string('big_area_name', 64)->comment('配送大区名称（如淮安淮安）');
            $table->string('special_line', 128)->nullable()->comment('专线名称（如永城-淮安专线）');
            $table->string('sorting_area', 32)->nullable()->comment('分拣区编号（如A66）');
            $table->tinyInteger('delivery_level')->default(1)->comment('配送等级');
            $table->string('small_area_name', 64)->comment('小区名称');
            $table->json('polygon')->nullable()->comment('多边形围栏坐标（经纬度数组）');
            $table->decimal('min_lng', 10, 6)->nullable()->comment('围栏最小经度（包围盒预过滤）');
            $table->decimal('max_lng', 10, 6)->nullable()->comment('围栏最大经度');
            $table->decimal('min_lat', 10, 6)->nullable()->comment('围栏最小纬度');
            $table->decimal('max_lat', 10, 6)->nullable()->comment('围栏最大纬度');
            $table->integer('delivery_days')->default(1)->comment('预计配送天数');
            $table->tinyInteger('factory_code')->nullable()->comment('关联工厂代码(dM)');
            $table->boolean('is_enabled')->default(true)->comment('是否启用');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->index('big_area_name', 'idx_big_area');
            $table->index('small_area_name', 'idx_small_area');
            $table->index('factory_code', 'idx_factory_code');
            $table->index('is_enabled', 'idx_is_enabled');
            $table->index(['min_lng', 'max_lng', 'min_lat', 'max_lat'], 'idx_bbox');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('delivery_areas');
    }
};
```

### 6.41.4 Eloquent 模型

#### OrderDelivery 模型

> **说明**：本模型已在 SDD 5.2.31 节定义，此处复现完整字段与关联，新增 `transitionTo()` 状态流转方法。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Models;

use App\Domains\Common\Castables\MoneyCast;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class OrderDelivery extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'order_deliveries';

    protected $fillable = [
        'order_id', 'express_company', 'tracking_no', 'status',
        'factory_code', 'delivery_time', 'signed_at',
        'sign_image', 'sign_type', 'signer_name',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'status'        => DeliveryStatus::class,
        'factory_code'  => 'integer',
        'delivery_time' => 'datetime',
        'signed_at'     => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class, 'order_id');
    }

    public function expressTracks(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ExpressTrack::class, 'order_delivery_id');
    }

    /**
     * 状态流转（带合法性校验）
     *
     * @throws \InvalidArgumentException
     */
    public function transitionTo(DeliveryStatus $target, ?string $remark = null): void
    {
        $current = $this->status;

        if (! $current->canTransitionTo($target)) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException(
                "物流单 {$this->tracking_no} 不允许从 {$current->label()} 流转到 {$target->label()}"
            );
        }

        $this->update([
            'status'    => $target,
            'signed_at' => $target === DeliveryStatus::DELIVERED ? now() : $this->signed_at,
        ]);

        // 触发物流状态变更事件
        event(new \App\Domains\Logistics\Events\DeliveryStatusChanged($this, $current, $target, $remark));
    }

    /**
     * 查询作用域：待揽收
     */
    public function scopePendingPickup($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', DeliveryStatus::PENDING_PICKUP);
    }

    /**
     * 查询作用域：运输中（含已揽收、运输中、派送中）
     */
    public function scopeInTransit($query)
    {
        return $query->whereIn('status', [
            DeliveryStatus::PICKED_UP->value,
            DeliveryStatus::IN_TRANSIT->value,
            DeliveryStatus::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY->value,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询作用域：异常
     */
    public function scopeException($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION);
    }
}
```

#### OrderMultiDelivery 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Models;

use App\Domains\Common\Castables\MoneyCast;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class OrderMultiDelivery extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'order_multi_deliveries';

    protected $fillable = [
        'order_id', 'address_id', 'receiver_name', 'phone',
        'province_name', 'city_name', 'county_name', 'detail_address',
        'quantity', 'fee', 'discount_rate', 'express_company', 'tracking_no',
        'status', 'ship_status', 'is_primary', 'shipped_at', 'signed_at',
        'sign_image', 'sign_type', 'signer_name',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'order_id'      => 'integer',
        'address_id'    => 'integer',
        'quantity'      => 'integer',
        'fee'           => MoneyCast::class,
        'discount_rate' => MoneyCast::class,
        'status'        => DeliveryStatus::class,
        'is_primary'    => 'boolean',
        'shipped_at'    => 'datetime',
        'signed_at'     => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class, 'order_id');
    }

    /**
     * 是否为首地址
     */
    public function isPrimary(): bool
    {
        return $this->is_primary;
    }

    /**
     * 计算折扣后运费（元）
     */
    public function discountedFee(): float
    {
        return $this->fee->toFloat() * (float) $this->discount_rate;
    }
}
```

#### ExpressTrack 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Models;

use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class ExpressTrack extends Model
{
    protected $table = 'express_tracks';

    protected $fillable = [
        'order_id', 'order_delivery_id', 'express_company', 'tracking_no',
        'status', 'tracks', 'last_event_at', 'synced_at', 'cached_until',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'status'       => DeliveryStatus::class,
        'tracks'       => 'array',
        'last_event_at' => 'datetime',
        'synced_at'    => 'datetime',
        'cached_until' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function order(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class, 'order_id');
    }

    public function orderDelivery(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(OrderDelivery::class, 'order_delivery_id');
    }

    /**
     * 查询作用域：缓存已过期
     */
    public function scopeCacheExpired($query)
    {
        return $query->where(function ($q) {
            $q->whereNull('cached_until')
              ->orWhere('cached_until', '<=', now());
        });
    }

    /**
     * 查询作用域：超48小时无更新
     */
    public function scopeStale($query, int $hours = 48)
    {
        return $query->whereNotNull('last_event_at')
                     ->where('last_event_at', '<=', now()->subHours($hours))
                     ->where('status', '!=', DeliveryStatus::DELIVERED);
    }

    /**
     * 刷新缓存过期时间（默认24小时）
     */
    public function refreshCache(int $ttlHours = 24): void
    {
        $this->update(['cached_until' => now()->addHours($ttlHours)]);
    }
}
```

---

### 6.41.5 Action 类

#### CalculateShippingFeeAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Actions;

use App\Domains\Common\ValueObjects\Money;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\OrderMultiDelivery;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Services\ShippingFeeCalculator;
use App\Models\Order;

/**
 * 计算运费 Action
 * FR-LOG-002 / FR-LOG-022-A / FR-LOG-022-C
 */
class CalculateShippingFeeAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private ShippingFeeCalculator $calculator,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 执行运费计算
     *
     * @param Order $order 订单
     * @param array $addresses 地址数组，每项含 address_id, quantity, province_name, city_name...
     * @param float $additionalDiscountRate 附加地址折扣率（默认0.7即7折）
     * @return array {
     *   perAddressFee: array, // 每个地址的运费明细
     *   totalFee: Money,      // 总运费
     * }
     */
    public function execute(Order $order, array $addresses, float $additionalDiscountRate = 0.7): array
    {
        $perAddressFee = [];
        $totalFee = Money::zero();

        foreach ($addresses as $index => $address) {
            $isPrimary = $index === 0;
            $baseFee = $this->calculator->calculate(
                order: $order,
                province: $address['province_name'] ?? '',
                city: $address['city_name'] ?? '',
                county: $address['county_name'] ?? '',
                weight: $order->weight ?? 0,
                quantity: $address['quantity'] ?? 1,
            );

            $discountRate = $isPrimary ? 1.0 : $additionalDiscountRate;
            $discountedFee = $baseFee->multiply($discountRate);

            $perAddressFee[] = [
                'address_id'     => $address['address_id'] ?? null,
                'is_primary'     => $isPrimary,
                'base_fee'       => $baseFee,
                'discount_rate'  => $discountRate,
                'discounted_fee' => $discountedFee,
            ];

            $totalFee = $totalFee->add($discountedFee);
        }

        return [
            'perAddressFee' => $perAddressFee,
            'totalFee'      => $totalFee,
        ];
    }
}
```

#### CreateDeliveryAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Actions;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\OrderDelivery;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\OrderMultiDelivery;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 创建物流单 Action
 * 支持单地址与多地址配送
 */
class CreateDeliveryAction
{
    /**
     * 创建主物流单
     */
    public function execute(
        Order $order,
        string $expressCompany,
        ?string $trackingNo = null,
        ?int $factoryCode = null,
    ): OrderDelivery {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $expressCompany, $trackingNo, $factoryCode) {
            $delivery = OrderDelivery::create([
                'order_id'        => $order->id,
                'express_company' => $expressCompany,
                'tracking_no'     => $trackingNo,
                'status'          => DeliveryStatus::PENDING_PICKUP,
                'factory_code'    => $factoryCode,
                'delivery_time'   => $this->estimateDeliveryTime($order),
            ]);

            return $delivery;
        });
    }

    /**
     * 创建多地址配送记录
     *
     * @param Order $order
     * @param array $addresses 地址明细数组
     */
    public function executeMulti(Order $order, array $addresses): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $addresses) {
            OrderMultiDelivery::where('order_id', $order->id)->delete();

            foreach ($addresses as $index => $addr) {
                OrderMultiDelivery::create([
                    'order_id'        => $order->id,
                    'address_id'      => $addr['address_id'],
                    'receiver_name'   => $addr['receiver_name'],
                    'phone'           => $addr['phone'],
                    'province_name'   => $addr['province_name'],
                    'city_name'       => $addr['city_name'],
                    'county_name'     => $addr['county_name'],
                    'detail_address'  => $addr['detail_address'],
                    'quantity'        => $addr['quantity'] ?? 0,
                    'fee'             => $addr['fee'] ?? 0,
                    'discount_rate'   => $addr['discount_rate'] ?? ($index === 0 ? 1.0 : 0.7),
                    'express_company' => $addr['express_company'] ?? null,
                    'tracking_no'     => $addr['tracking_no'] ?? null,
                    'status'          => DeliveryStatus::PENDING_PICKUP,
                    'is_primary'      => $index === 0,
                ]);
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * 预估配送时间（根据配送区域与时效）
     */
    private function estimateDeliveryTime(Order $order): ?\Carbon\Carbon
    {
        // 从配送区域服务获取预计天数
        $days = app(\App\Domains\Logistics\Services\DeliveryAreaService::class)
            ->getDeliveryDays($order->province_name, $order->city_name);

        return $days ? now()->addDays($days) : null;
    }
}
```

#### UpdateExpressTrackAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Actions;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\ExpressTrack;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;

/**
 * 更新物流轨迹 Action
 * 由 SyncExpressTracksJob 调用
 */
class UpdateExpressTrackAction
{
    /**
     * 执行轨迹更新
     *
     * @param ExpressTrack $expressTrack
     * @param array $tracks 从第三方API拉取的轨迹数组
     * @param DeliveryStatus $latestStatus 最新状态
     */
    public function execute(
        ExpressTrack $expressTrack,
        array $tracks,
        DeliveryStatus $latestStatus,
    ): void {
        $lastEvent = $tracks[0] ?? null;

        $expressTrack->update([
            'tracks'        => $tracks,
            'status'        => $latestStatus,
            'last_event_at' => $lastEvent['time'] ?? now(),
            'synced_at'     => now(),
        ]);

        $expressTrack->refreshCache();

        // 同步更新 order_deliveries 状态
        if ($expressTrack->orderDelivery) {
            $current = $expressTrack->orderDelivery->status;
            if ($current->canTransitionTo($latestStatus)) {
                $expressTrack->orderDelivery->transitionTo($latestStatus);
            }
        }

        // 触发轨迹更新事件
        event(new \App\Domains\Logistics\Events\ExpressTrackUpdated($expressTrack, $latestStatus));
    }
}
```

#### SyncExpressTracksAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Actions;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\ExpressTrack;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Services\ExpressTrackSyncService;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;

/**
 * 批量同步物流轨迹 Action
 * 由定时任务或命令调用
 */
class SyncExpressTracksAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private ExpressTrackSyncService $syncService,
        private UpdateExpressTrackAction $updateAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 执行批量同步
     *
     * @param int $batchSize 每批处理数量
     * @return array { synced: int, failed: int }
     */
    public function execute(int $batchSize = 50): array
    {
        $tracks = ExpressTrack::cacheExpired()
            ->whereNotIn('status', [
                DeliveryStatus::DELIVERED->value,
                DeliveryStatus::RETURNED->value,
            ])
            ->limit($batchSize)
            ->get();

        $synced = 0;
        $failed = 0;

        foreach ($tracks as $expressTrack) {
            try {
                $result = $this->syncService->fetch(
                    company: $expressTrack->express_company,
                    trackingNo: $expressTrack->tracking_no,
                );

                if ($result !== null) {
                    $this->updateAction->execute(
                        $expressTrack,
                        $result['tracks'],
                        $result['status'],
                    );
                    $synced++;
                }
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log::error('物流轨迹同步失败', [
                    'tracking_no' => $expressTrack->tracking_no,
                    'error'       => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
                $failed++;
            }
        }

        return ['synced' => $synced, 'failed' => $failed];
    }
}
```

---

### 6.41.6 Service 类

#### LogisticsService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Services;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Actions\CreateDeliveryAction;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\ExpressTrack;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\OrderDelivery;
use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\OrderMultiDelivery;
use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use App\Enums\ExpressCompany;
use App\Models\Order;

/**
 * 物流服务入口
 * 封装物流查询、创建、轨迹获取等高层能力
 */
class LogisticsService
{
    public function __construct(
        private ShippingFeeCalculator $feeCalculator,
        private DeliveryAreaService $areaService,
        private ExpressTrackSyncService $trackSyncService,
        private CreateDeliveryAction $createDeliveryAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 最优物流推荐
     * FR-LOG-001
     */
    public function recommendBestDelivery(Order $order, array $addresses): ?array
    {
        $candidates = [];
        $enabledCompanies = \Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB::table('express_companies')
            ->where('is_enabled', true)
            ->pluck('code')
            ->toArray();

        foreach (ExpressCompany::cases() as $company) {
            if (! in_array($company->value, $enabledCompanies, true)) {
                continue;
            }

            $feeResult = $this->feeCalculator->calculateForAddresses($order, $addresses, $company);
            $days = $this->areaService->getDeliveryDays(
                $addresses[0]['province_name'] ?? '',
                $addresses[0]['city_name'] ?? ''
            );

            $candidates[] = [
                'company'       => $company->value,
                'company_name'  => $company->label(),
                'fee'           => $feeResult['totalFee'],
                'estimated_days'=> $days,
                'score'         => $this->scoreDelivery($feeResult['totalFee']->toFloat(), $days),
            ];
        }

        // 按综合评分排序（费用低、时效快得分高）
        usort($candidates, fn ($a, $b) => $b['score'] <=> $a['score']);

        return $candidates[0] ?? null;
    }

    /**
     * 获取物流轨迹（优先缓存，缓存失效则触发异步同步）
     * FR-LOG-008
     */
    public function getExpressTracks(string $orderSn): ?ExpressTrack
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_no', $orderSn)->first();
        if (! $order) {
            return null;
        }

        $track = ExpressTrack::where('order_id', $order->id)->first();

        if (! $track || $track->cacheExpired()->exists()) {
            // 触发异步同步
            \App\Jobs\Logistics\SyncExpressTracksJob::dispatch($order->id);
        }

        return $track;
    }

    /**
     * 获取快递信息列表
     * FR-LOG-009 / FR-LOG-038
     */
    public function getExpressInfos(): array
    {
        return array_map(fn (ExpressCompany $c) => [
            'code'        => $c->value,
            'name'        => $c->label(),
            'query_code'  => $c->queryCode(),
            'supports_electronic_waybill' => $c->supportsElectronicWaybill(),
        ], ExpressCompany::cases());
    }

    /**
     * 获取仅快递列表（排除专线和自提）
     * FR-LOG-039
     */
    public function getOnlyExpresses(): array
    {
        return array_filter($this->getExpressInfos(), fn ($c) => $c['code'] !== 'zhuanxian');
    }

    /**
     * 获取快递员信息
     * FR-LOG-005
     */
    public function getDeliveryMan(int $orderId): ?array
    {
        $delivery = OrderDelivery::where('order_id', $orderId)
            ->where('status', DeliveryStatus::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY)
            ->first();

        if (! $delivery) {
            return null;
        }

        // 从第三方API或自有系统获取快递员信息
        return $this->trackSyncService->getDeliveryManInfo(
            $delivery->express_company,
            $delivery->tracking_no
        );
    }

    /**
     * 获取工厂信息
     * FR-LOG-006
     */
    public function getFactories(): array
    {
        return \App\Models\Factory::all()
            ->map(fn ($f) => [
                'code' => $f->code,
                'name' => $f->name,
                'address' => $f->address,
                'lnglat' => $f->lnglat,
            ])
            ->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 获取专属客户经理
     * FR-LOG-007
     */
    public function getCustomerManager(int $customerId): ?array
    {
        $customer = \App\Models\Customer::find($customerId);
        if (! $customer || ! $customer->manager_id) {
            return null;
        }

        $manager = \App\Models\AdminUser::find($customer->manager_id);
        return $manager ? [
            'id'       => $manager->id,
            'name'     => $manager->name,
            'phone'    => $manager->phone,
            'avatar'   => $manager->avatar,
        ] : null;
    }

    /**
     * 配送限制检查
     * FR-LOG-036
     */
    public function checkDeliveryLimit(string $province, string $city, string $county = ''): array
    {
        $area = $this->areaService->findArea($province, $city, $county);

        if (! $area || ! $area->is_enabled) {
            return [
                'allow'   => false,
                'message' => '当前地址超出配送范围',
            ];
        }

        return [
            'allow'         => true,
            'delivery_days' => $area->delivery_days,
            'factory_code'  => $area->factory_code,
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 根据交易ID查询物流
     * FR-LOG-040
     */
    public function getTradeByTid(string $platformOrderId): ?array
    {
        $platformOrder = \App\Models\PlatformOrder::where('platform_order_id', $platformOrderId)->first();
        if (! $platformOrder) {
            return null;
        }

        $order = Order::find($platformOrder->order_id);
        if (! $order) {
            return null;
        }

        return [
            'order'     => $order->toArray(),
            'delivery'  => OrderDelivery::where('order_id', $order->id)->get()->toArray(),
            'tracks'    => ExpressTrack::where('order_id', $order->id)->get()->toArray(),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 综合评分算法（费用权重60%，时效权重40%）
     */
    private function scoreDelivery(float $fee, ?int $days): float
    {
        $feeScore = max(0, 100 - $fee); // 费用越低得分越高
        $daysScore = $days ? max(0, 100 - $days * 20) : 50; // 天数越少得分越高

        return $feeScore * 0.6 + $daysScore * 0.4;
    }
}
```

#### ShippingFeeCalculator

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Services;

use App\Domains\Common\ValueObjects\Money;
use App\Enums\ExpressCompany;
use App\Models\Order;

/**
 * 运费计算服务
 * FR-LOG-002 / FR-LOG-022-A / FR-LOG-022-C
 */
class ShippingFeeCalculator
{
    /**
     * 基础运费计算（单地址）
     *
     * @param Order $order
     * @param string $province
     * @param string $city
     * @param string $county
     * @param float $weight 重量(kg)
     * @param int $quantity 数量
     * @param ExpressCompany|null $company 指定快递公司
     * @return Money 运费（分）
     */
    public function calculate(
        Order $order,
        string $province,
        string $city,
        string $county = '',
        float $weight = 0,
        ?float $volume = null,
        int $quantity = 1,
        ?ExpressCompany $company = null,
        ?int $expressCompanyId = null,
    ): Money {
        // 1. 从配送区域获取基础运费系数
        $area = app(DeliveryAreaService::class)->findArea($province, $city, $county);
        $baseRate = $area ? $area->delivery_level * 100 : 1000; // 默认10元

        // 2. 体积重量换算（印刷品体积大但重量轻的场景）
        $chargeableWeight = $weight;
        if ($volume !== null && $volume > 0) {
            $ratio = 6000; // 默认抛比系数
            if ($expressCompanyId !== null) {
                $cfg = \Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB::table('express_companies')
                    ->where('id', $expressCompanyId)
                    ->value('volumetric_ratio');
                $ratio = $cfg ?? 6000;
            }
            $volumetricWeight = $this->getVolumetricWeight($volume, $ratio);
            $chargeableWeight = max($weight, $volumetricWeight);
        }

        // 3. 重量加价（每公斤加2元，按计费重量）
        $weightFee = (int) ($chargeableWeight * 200);

        // 4. 数量系数（每增加1件加基础系数20%）
        $quantityFee = (int) ($baseRate * ($quantity - 1) * 0.2);

        // 5. 快递公司系数
        $companyRate = $this->getCompanyRate($company);

        $total = (int) (($baseRate + $weightFee + $quantityFee) * $companyRate);

        return new Money($total);
    }

    /**
     * 体积重量计算
     *
     * @param float $volume 体积(cm³)
     * @param int $volumetricRatio 抛比系数（默认6000）
     * @return float 体积重量(kg)
     */
    public function getVolumetricWeight(float $volume, int $volumetricRatio): float
    {
        return round($volume / $volumetricRatio, 2);
    }

    /**
     * 多地址运费计算
     *
     * @param Order $order
     * @param array $addresses
     * @param ExpressCompany|null $company
     * @param float $additionalDiscountRate 附加地址折扣率
     * @return array { perAddressFee: array, totalFee: Money }
     */
    public function calculateForAddresses(
        Order $order,
        array $addresses,
        ?ExpressCompany $company = null,
        float $additionalDiscountRate = 0.7,
    ): array {
        $perAddressFee = [];
        $totalFee = Money::zero();

        foreach ($addresses as $index => $addr) {
            $baseFee = $this->calculate(
                order: $order,
                province: $addr['province_name'] ?? '',
                city: $addr['city_name'] ?? '',
                county: $addr['county_name'] ?? '',
                weight: $order->weight ?? 0,
                volume: $order->total_volume ?? null,
                quantity: $addr['quantity'] ?? 1,
                company: $company,
            );

            $rate = $index === 0 ? 1.0 : $additionalDiscountRate;
            $discounted = $baseFee->multiply($rate);

            $perAddressFee[] = [
                'address_id'      => $addr['address_id'] ?? null,
                'base_fee'        => $baseFee,
                'discount_rate'   => $rate,
                'discounted_fee'  => $discounted,
            ];

            $totalFee = $totalFee->add($discounted);
        }

        return [
            'perAddressFee' => $perAddressFee,
            'totalFee'      => $totalFee,
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 快递公司费率系数
     */
    private function getCompanyRate(?ExpressCompany $company): float
    {
        return match ($company) {
            ExpressCompany::SF      => 1.5, // 顺丰最贵
            ExpressCompany::JD      => 1.3,
            ExpressCompany::EMS     => 1.2,
            ExpressCompany::DEBANG  => 1.15,
            ExpressCompany::SPECIAL => 0.8, // 自有专线优惠
            default                 => 1.0,
        };
    }
}
```

#### ExpressTrackSyncService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Services;

use App\Enums\DeliveryStatus;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Http;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 物流轨迹同步服务
 * 对接快递鸟/快递100/各家官方API
 * FR-LOG-030 / FR-LOG-032 / FR-LOG-033
 */
class ExpressTrackSyncService
{
    private const CACHE_TTL_HOURS = 24;
    private const STALE_THRESHOLD_HOURS = 48;
    private const DEVIATION_THRESHOLD_KM = 5.0; // 偏离阈值：5公里

    /**
     * 从第三方平台拉取轨迹
     *
     * @param string $company 快递公司编码
     * @param string $trackingNo 快递单号
     * @return array|null { tracks: array, status: DeliveryStatus }
     */
    public function fetch(string $company, string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        $cacheKey = "express_track:{$company}:{$trackingNo}";

        // 优先读缓存
        if ($cached = Cache::get($cacheKey)) {
            return $cached;
        }

        // 三级降级策略：快递鸟 → 快递100 → 缓存兜底
        // 一级：快递鸟
        try {
            $result = $this->fetchFromKdniao($company, $trackingNo);
            if ($result && ! empty($result['traces'])) {
                Cache::put($cacheKey, $result, now()->addHours(self::CACHE_TTL_HOURS));
                return $result;
            }
        } catch (ExternalApiException $e) {
            Log::warning("快递鸟轨迹查询失败: {$trackingNo}, 尝试降级到快递100");
        }

        // 二级：快递100
        try {
            $result = $this->fetchFromKuaidi100($company, $trackingNo);
            if ($result && ! empty($result['traces'])) {
                Cache::put($cacheKey, $result, now()->addHours(self::CACHE_TTL_HOURS));
                return $result;
            }
        } catch (ExternalApiException $e) {
            Log::warning("快递100轨迹查询失败: {$trackingNo}, 尝试降级到缓存");
        }

        // 三级：缓存兜底（读取可能已过期的历史缓存）
        $cached = $this->getCachedTracks($trackingNo);
        if ($cached && $cached['cached_until'] > now()) {
            return $cached;
        }

        // 最终：返回空轨迹并标记异常
        return ['traces' => [], 'exception' => 'ALL_PROVIDERS_FAILED'];
    }

    /**
     * 检测异常轨迹（超48小时无更新 + 偏离配送路线）
     * FR-LOG-033 / FR-LOG-041
     */
    public function detectExceptions(): array
    {
        $exceptions = [];

        // 1. 超48小时无更新（原有逻辑保留）
        $staleTracks = \App\Domains\Logistics\Models\ExpressTrack::stale(self::STALE_THRESHOLD_HOURS)
            ->get();
        foreach ($staleTracks as $track) {
            $track->update(['status' => DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION]);

            // 同步更新 order_deliveries
            if ($track->orderDelivery) {
                $track->orderDelivery->transitionTo(DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION, '超48小时无轨迹更新');
            }

            $exceptions[] = [
                'order_id'     => $track->order_id,
                'tracking_no'  => $track->tracking_no,
                'last_event_at'=> $track->last_event_at,
            ];

            // 触发异常预警事件
            event(new \App\Domains\Logistics\Events\DeliveryExceptionWarning($track));
        }

        // 2. 偏离配送路线检测（新增）
        $deviatedTracks = $this->detectRouteDeviations();
        foreach ($deviatedTracks as $item) {
            $track = $item['track'];
            $track->update(['status' => DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION]);

            if ($track->orderDelivery) {
                $track->orderDelivery->transitionTo(DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION, $item['reason']);
            }

            $exceptions[] = [
                'order_id'     => $track->order_id,
                'tracking_no'  => $track->tracking_no,
                'last_event_at'=> $track->last_event_at,
            ];

            event(new \App\Domains\Logistics\Events\DeliveryExceptionWarning($track));
        }

        return $exceptions;
    }

    /**
     * 偏离配送路线检测
     *
     * 算法逻辑：
     * 1. 获取订单关联的 delivery_routes（通过 from_city/to_city 匹配）
     * 2. 获取该订单最近 3 个 GPS 轨迹点（internal_logistics_tracks.latitude/longitude）
     * 3. 计算每个轨迹点到路线 polyline 上各线段的最短距离（Haversine + 点到线段投影）
     * 4. 若最短距离 > DEVIATION_THRESHOLD_KM，则判定为偏离路线
     */
    private function detectRouteDeviations(): array
    {
        $deviations = [];

        // 仅检测专线物流且运输中的轨迹
        $tracks = \App\Domains\Logistics\Models\ExpressTrack::where('source', 'private')
            ->whereIn('status', [
                DeliveryStatus::IN_TRANSIT->value,
                DeliveryStatus::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY->value,
            ])
            ->get();

        foreach ($tracks as $track) {
            $order = $track->order;
            if (! $order) {
                continue;
            }

            // 匹配配送路线（通过订单发货地与收货地）
            $route = \App\Domains\Logistics\Models\DeliveryRoute::where([
                ['from_city', 'like', "%{$order->ship_city}%"],
                ['to_city', 'like', "%{$order->receiver_city}%"],
                ['is_enabled', true],
            ])->first();

            if (! $route || empty($route->polyline)) {
                continue;
            }

            // 取最近 3 个 GPS 点
            $recentPoints = \App\Domains\Logistics\Models\InternalLogisticsTrack::where('tracking_no', $track->tracking_no)
                ->whereNotNull('latitude')
                ->whereNotNull('longitude')
                ->orderByDesc('event_time')
                ->limit(3)
                ->get(['latitude', 'longitude']);

            if ($recentPoints->isEmpty()) {
                continue;
            }

            $polyline = $route->polyline; // [[lng, lat], [lng, lat], ...]
            $maxDeviation = 0.0;

            foreach ($recentPoints as $point) {
                $minDist = $this->pointToPolylineMinDistance(
                    (float) $point->latitude,
                    (float) $point->longitude,
                    $polyline,
                );
                $maxDeviation = max($maxDeviation, $minDist);
            }

            if ($maxDeviation > self::DEVIATION_THRESHOLD_KM) {
                $deviations[] = [
                    'track'  => $track,
                    'reason' => "偏离规划路线 {$maxDeviation}km（阈值 " . self::DEVIATION_THRESHOLD_KM . "km）",
                ];
            }
        }

        return $deviations;
    }

    /**
     * 计算点到 polyline 的最短距离（公里，Haversine）
     *
     * @param float $lat 点纬度
     * @param float $lng 点经度
     * @param array $polyline [[lng, lat], ...]
     */
    private function pointToPolylineMinDistance(float $lat, float $lng, array $polyline): float
    {
        $minDist = PHP_FLOAT_MAX;
        $count = count($polyline);

        for ($i = 0; $i < $count - 1; $i++) {
            $dist = $this->pointToSegmentDistance(
                $lat, $lng,
                (float) $polyline[$i][1], (float) $polyline[$i][0],
                (float) $polyline[$i + 1][1], (float) $polyline[$i + 1][0],
            );
            $minDist = min($minDist, $dist);
        }

        return $minDist;
    }

    /**
     * 点到线段的最短距离（Haversine，单位：公里）
     */
    private function pointToSegmentDistance(
        float $lat, float $lng,
        float $lat1, float $lng1,
        float $lat2, float $lng2,
    ): float {
        // 使用 DeliveryAreaService 的 Haversine 公式
        $areaService = app(DeliveryAreaService::class);

        // 向量投影判断垂足是否在线段内
        $dx = $lng2 - $lng1;
        $dy = $lat2 - $lat1;
        $len2 = $dx * $dx + $dy * $dy;

        if ($len2 == 0) {
            return $areaService->getDeliveryDistance($lng1, $lat1, $lng, $lat);
        }

        $t = max(0, min(1, (($lng - $lng1) * $dx + ($lat - $lat1) * $dy) / $len2));
        $projLng = $lng1 + $t * $dx;
        $projLat = $lat1 + $t * $dy;

        return $areaService->getDeliveryDistance($projLng, $projLat, $lng, $lat);
    }

    /**
     * 获取快递员信息
     */
    public function getDeliveryManInfo(string $company, string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        // 实际对接快递鸟/快递100的快递员查询接口
        // 以下为示例结构
        return [
            'name'   => '张师傅',
            'phone'  => '138****1234',
            'avatar' => null,
        ];
    }

    // -- 私有适配器方法 --

    private function fetchFromKdniao(string $company, string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        $config = config('services.kdniao');
        $requestData = json_encode(['OrderCode' => '', 'ShipperCode' => strtoupper($company), 'LogisticCode' => $trackingNo]);

        $response = Http::asForm()->post($config['api_url'], [
            'RequestData' => $requestData,
            'EBusinessID' => $config['ebusiness_id'],
            'RequestType' => '1002',
            'DataSign'    => base64_encode(md5($requestData . $config['api_key'])),
            'DataType'    => '2',
        ]);

        if (! $response->successful()) {
            Log::warning('快递鸟查询失败', ['tracking_no' => $trackingNo, 'response' => $response->body()]);
            return null;
        }

        $data = $response->json();
        if (! ($data['Success'] ?? false)) {
            return null;
        }

        return $this->normalizeTracks($data['Traces'] ?? [], $company);
    }

    private function fetchFromKuaidi100(string $company, string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        $config = config('services.kuaidi100');

        $response = Http::get($config['api_url'] . '/query', [
            'type'   => $company,
            'postid' => $trackingNo,
            'temp'   => time(),
        ]);

        if (! $response->successful()) {
            return null;
        }

        $data = $response->json();
        if ($data['status'] !== '200') {
            return null;
        }

        return $this->normalizeTracks($data['data'] ?? [], $company);
    }

    private function fetchFromJD(string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        // 京东物流官方API对接
        Log::info('京东物流轨迹拉取', ['tracking_no' => $trackingNo]);
        return null; // 占位实现
    }

    private function fetchFromInternal(string $trackingNo): ?array
    {
        // 自有专线系统对接
        $tracks = \App\Models\InternalLogisticsTrack::where('tracking_no', $trackingNo)
            ->orderByDesc('event_time')
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($t) => [
                'time'    => $t->event_time->format('Y-m-d H:i:s'),
                'location'=> $t->location,
                'status'  => $t->status,
                'operator'=> $t->operator_name,
            ])
            ->toArray();

        return $this->normalizeTracks($tracks, 'zhuanxian');
    }

    /**
     * 标准化轨迹数据并推断状态
     */
    private function normalizeTracks(array $rawTracks, string $company): array
    {
        $tracks = array_map(fn ($t) => [
            'time'     => $t['time'] ?? ($t['AcceptTime'] ?? ''),
            'location' => $t['location'] ?? ($t['AcceptStation'] ?? ''),
            'status'   => $t['status'] ?? ($t['ActionCode'] ?? ''),
            'operator' => $t['operator'] ?? '',
        ], $rawTracks);

        $latestStatus = $this->inferStatus($tracks[0]['status'] ?? '');

        return [
            'tracks' => $tracks,
            'status' => $latestStatus,
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 从轨迹文本推断 DeliveryStatus
     */
    private function inferStatus(string $statusText): DeliveryStatus
    {
        $text = mb_strtolower($statusText);

        return match (true) {
            str_contains($text, '签收') || str_contains($text, 'signed') => DeliveryStatus::DELIVERED,
            str_contains($text, '派送') || str_contains($text, 'out for delivery') => DeliveryStatus::OUT_FOR_DELIVERY,
            str_contains($text, '揽收') || str_contains($text, 'picked') => DeliveryStatus::PICKED_UP,
            str_contains($text, '退回') || str_contains($text, 'return') => DeliveryStatus::RETURNED,
            str_contains($text, '异常') || str_contains($text, 'exception') => DeliveryStatus::EXCEPTION,
            default => DeliveryStatus::IN_TRANSIT,
        };
    }
}
```

#### DeliveryAreaService

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Logistics\Services;

use App\Domains\Logistics\Models\DeliveryArea;

/**
 * 配送区域服务
 * FR-LOG-023 ~ FR-LOG-029
 */
class DeliveryAreaService
{
    /**
     * 根据省市区查找配送区域
     */
    public function findArea(string $province, string $city, string $county = ''): ?DeliveryArea
    {
        // 优先精确匹配
        $area = DeliveryArea::where('big_area_name', 'like', "%{$province}%")
            ->where('small_area_name', 'like', "%{$city}%")
            ->where('is_enabled', true)
            ->first();

        if (! $area && $county) {
            $area = DeliveryArea::where('small_area_name', 'like', "%{$county}%")
                ->where('is_enabled', true)
                ->first();
        }

        return $area;
    }

    /**
     * 获取配送天数
     */
    public function getDeliveryDays(string $province, string $city, string $county = ''): ?int
    {
        $area = $this->findArea($province, $city, $county);
        return $area?->delivery_days;
    }

    /**
     * 地理编码：地址转经纬度
     * FR-LOG-024
     */
    public function geoEncode(string $address): ?array
    {
        $cacheKey = 'geo:' . md5($address);

        if ($cached = \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache::get($cacheKey)) {
            return $cached;
        }

        $response = \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Http::get(config('services.amap.geo_url'), [
            'address' => $address,
            'key'     => config('services.amap.key'),
        ]);

        if (! $response->successful()) {
            return null;
        }

        $data = $response->json();
        if ($data['status'] !== '1' || empty($data['geocodes'])) {
            return null;
        }

        $location = $data['geocodes'][0]['location'];
        [$lng, $lat] = explode(',', $location);

        $result = ['lng' => (float) $lng, 'lat' => (float) $lat];
        \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache::put($cacheKey, $result, now()->addDays(30));

        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * 判断坐标是否在多边形围栏内
     *
     * @param float $lng 经度
     * @param float $lat 纬度
     * @param array $polygon 多边形顶点数组 [[lng, lat], ...]
     */
    public function isPointInPolygon(
        float $lng, float $lat, array $polygon,
        ?float $minLng = null, ?float $maxLng = null,
        ?float $minLat = null, ?float $maxLat = null,
    ): bool {
        // 1. 包围盒快速预过滤（如有提供，可过滤掉 90% 以上无关区域）
        if ($minLng !== null && $maxLng !== null && $minLat !== null && $maxLat !== null) {
            if ($lng < $minLng || $lng > $maxLng || $lat < $minLat || $lat > $maxLat) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        // 2. PHP 射线法精确判定
        $inside = false;
        $count = count($polygon);

        for ($i = 0, $j = $count - 1; $i < $count; $j = $i++) {
            $xi = $polygon[$i][0];
            $yi = $polygon[$i][1];
            $xj = $polygon[$j][0];
            $yj = $polygon[$j][1];

            $intersect = (($yi > $lat) !== ($yj > $lat))
                && ($lng < ($xj - $xi) * ($lat - $yi) / ($yj - $yi) + $xi);

            if ($intersect) {
                $inside = ! $inside;
            }
        }

        return $inside;
    }

    /**
     * 配送计划查询
     * FR-LOG-004
     */
    public function getDeliveryPlan(string $province, string $city): array
    {
        $area = $this->findArea($province, $city);
        if (! $area) {
            return ['available' => false, 'message' => '该区域暂不支持配送'];
        }

        return [
            'available'      => true,
            'big_area'       => $area->big_area_name,
            'small_area'     => $area->small_area_name,
            'special_line'   => $area->special_line,
            'sorting_area'   => $area->sorting_area,
            'delivery_days'  => $area->delivery_days,
            'factory_code'   => $area->factory_code,
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 计算配送距离（基于经纬度）
     * FR-LOG-003
     */
    public function getDeliveryDistance(float $fromLng, float $fromLat, float $toLng, float $toLat): float
    {
        // 哈弗辛公式（Haversine）
        $earthRadius = 6371; // 地球半径(km)

        $dLat = deg2rad($toLat - $fromLat);
        $dLng = deg2rad($toLng - $fromLng);

        $a = sin($dLat / 2) * sin($dLat / 2)
            + cos(deg2rad($fromLat)) * cos(deg2rad($toLat))
            * sin($dLng / 2) * sin($dLng / 2);

        $c = 2 * atan2(sqrt($a), sqrt(1 - $a));

        return round($earthRadius * $c, 2);
    }
}
```

---

### 6.41.7 关键业务规则

| 规则项 | 说明 | 实现位置 |
|--------|------|----------|
| **多地址运费公式** | `totalFee = 首地址标准运费 + Σ(附加地址标准运费 × 折扣率)` | `ShippingFeeCalculator::calculateForAddresses()` |
| **附加地址默认折扣** | 默认 7 折（`discount_rate = 0.70`），可通过配置调整 | `CalculateShippingFeeAction` / `CreateDeliveryAction` |
| **物流状态机** | 待揽收→已揽收→运输中→派送中→已签收；异常可恢复或退回 | `DeliveryStatus::canTransitionTo()` |
| **轨迹缓存** | 缓存 24 小时，减少 API 调用频率 | `ExpressTrackSyncService::fetch()` |
| **异常预警** | 超 48 小时无更新自动标记"物流异常"，通知客服 | `ExpressTrackSyncService::detectExceptions()` |
| **自动签收** | 7 天无异常自动确认收货 | `OrderDeliveryObserver`（定时任务） |
| **配送区域围栏** | 多边形围栏判定地址是否在配送范围内 | `DeliveryAreaService::isPointInPolygon()` |
| **专线自有轨迹** | 通过 `internal_logistics_tracks` 表同步自有系统轨迹 | `ExpressTrackSyncService::fetchFromInternal()` |
| **位掩码时效** | `deliveryTimeliness` 使用位掩码：`1=当日发, 2=同城快递, 4=半日达` | `DeliveryTimeliness::decode()/encode()` |
| **地址类型** | `0=收货地址, 1=发票地址, 2=退货地址` | `AddressType` |
| **快递公司费率** | 顺丰1.5x、京东1.3x、EMS1.2x、自有专线0.8x | `ShippingFeeCalculator::getCompanyRate()` |
| **VIP 运费权益** | Lv1~Lv8 均享"代送货免费、指定快递包邮" | `ShippingFeeCalculator`（结合 VIP 服务） |

#### 运费计算详细示例

```php
// 场景：1个订单配送至3个地址，基础运费各20元
$addresses = [
    ['address_id' => 1, 'quantity' => 100], // 首地址
    ['address_id' => 2, 'quantity' => 50],  // 附加地址1
    ['address_id' => 3, 'quantity' => 50],  // 附加地址2
];

// 计算结果：
// 首地址：20元 × 1.0 = 20元
// 附加地址1：20元 × 0.7 = 14元
// 附加地址2：20元 × 0.7 = 14元
// totalFee = 20 + 14 + 14 = 48元
```

#### 物流状态映射

| `order_deliveries.status` | `DeliveryStatus` | 客户侧 `out_status_name` | 说明 |
|---------------------------|------------------|--------------------------|------|
| 0 | 待揽收 | 4（已发货） | 订单已发货，等待揽收 |
| 1 | 已揽收 | 4（已发货） | 快递公司已揽收 |
| 2 | 运输中 | 8（配送中） | 包裹在运输途中 |
| 3 | 派送中 | 8（配送中） | 快递员正在派送 |
| 4 | 已签收 | 9（已完成） | 客户确认收货 |
| 5 | 异常 | 8（配送中） | 客服跟进中 |
| 6 | 已退回 | 5（已取消） | 退回视同取消 |

#### 运费计算时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client as 客户端
    participant Controller as DeliveryController
    participant Action as CalculateShippingFeeAction
    participant Calculator as ShippingFeeCalculator
    participant AreaService as DeliveryAreaService
    participant DB as 数据库

    Client->>Controller: POST /api/Delivery/CalcExpressSum
    Controller->>Action: execute(order, addresses, discountRate)
    Action->>Calculator: calculateForAddresses(order, addresses, company, rate)
    loop 每个地址
        Calculator->>AreaService: findArea(province, city)
        AreaService->>DB: SELECT * FROM delivery_areas
        DB-->>AreaService: 区域记录
        AreaService-->>Calculator: delivery_level / days
        Calculator->>Calculator: baseFee + weightFee + quantityFee
        Calculator->>Calculator: * discountRate
    end
    Calculator-->>Action: {perAddressFee, totalFee}
    Action-->>Controller: 运费明细
    Controller-->>Client: {code: 200, data: {...}}
```

#### 物流轨迹同步时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Schedule as 定时任务
    participant Job as SyncExpressTracksJob
    participant Action as SyncExpressTracksAction
    participant Service as ExpressTrackSyncService
    participant Kdniao as 快递鸟/快递100
    participant UpdateAction as UpdateExpressTrackAction
    participant DB as 数据库
    participant Event as DeliveryStatusChanged

    Schedule->>Job: dispatch()
    Job->>Action: execute(batchSize)
    Action->>DB: SELECT * FROM express_tracks WHERE cached_until <= NOW()
    DB-->>Action: 待同步轨迹列表
    loop 每条轨迹
        Action->>Service: fetch(company, trackingNo)
        Service->>Kdniao: HTTP API 查询
        Kdniao-->>Service: 轨迹JSON
        Service-->>Action: {tracks, status}
        Action->>UpdateAction: execute(track, tracks, status)
        UpdateAction->>DB: UPDATE express_tracks
        UpdateAction->>DB: UPDATE order_deliveries (状态流转)
        UpdateAction->>Event: dispatch()
    end
    Action-->>Job: {synced: N, failed: M}
    Job-->>Schedule: 完成
```

#### 多地址配送创建时序图

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram

    loop 每个地址
        Action->>DB: INSERT INTO order_multi_deliveries
    end
    DB-->>Action: 插入完成
    Action-->>Controller: void
    Controller->>DB: UPDATE orders SET express_sum = totalFee
    Controller-->>Client: {code: 200, data: {totalFee}}
```

---

### 补充说明

1. **Queue Job 定义**：`SyncExpressTracksJob` 实现 `ShouldQueue` 接口，使用 `database` 或 `redis` 队列驱动，在 `app/Jobs/Logistics/SyncExpressTracksJob.php` 中定义。
2. **定时任务配置**：在 `app/Console/Kernel.php` 中注册 `logistics:sync` 命令，每 15 分钟执行一次轨迹同步；每日凌晨执行一次异常检测。
3. **配置项**：`config/services.php` 中新增 `kdniao` 和 `kuaidi100` 配置节点，含 `api_url`、`ebusiness_id`、`api_key` 等字段。
4. **与现有表兼容**：`order_deliveries` 表保持与 SDD 5.2.31 完全一致，本章新增的 `order_multi_deliveries.status` 字段使用 `DeliveryStatus` 枚举的简化视图（0待发货/1已发货/2已签收），实际存储为 `tinyint`。
5. **异常预警通知**：`DeliveryExceptionWarning` 事件由 `App\Listeners\Logistics\NotifyCustomerService` 监听，发送企业微信/钉钉通知给客服团队。

---

## 6.42 商品管理子系统设计 (ProductManagementService)

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：品类参数模板化、SKU 动态生成、cpSummary 规格摘要标准化、联动规则引擎化、设计规范自动校验。
> **一致性声明**：本章与 SDD 第 5.2.19 ~ 5.2.21 节及 supplement_tables.md 中已定义的 `products`、`product_categories`、`param_templates`、`product_param_options`、`product_param_rules`、`product_design_specs` 保持完全兼容，在此基础上进行子系统级能力扩展。

---

### 6.42.1 设计概述

商品管理子系统是怡安印刷商城的核心品类中枢，承载从分类树维护、参数模板配置、规格摘要（cpSummary）生成、设计文件校验到实时计价的完整链路。核心设计原则如下：

1. **品类参数模板化**：每个一级品类（名片/单张/标签/画册/广告物料/包装/办公/家居/文创/季节/现货样品）拥有独立的参数模板集，支持版本管理与分组参数，历史订单引用下单时的模板版本，避免模板变更影响已成交订单的计价回溯。

2. **联动规则引擎化**：参数间依赖关系（如尺寸影响材质、装订影响页数）通过离散化的 `param_template_rules` 表存储，由 `ParamTemplateService` 在前端渲染时实时计算可用选项，确保用户只能提交合法的参数组合。

3. **cpSummary 标准化**：所有商品规格统一编码为 `productType:size:style:binding:reprint:designOrder:groupParams:pageCount:totalPages:quantity:skuCount` 格式，支持正向生成与反向解析回填，是购物车、订单、收藏、再下单全链路的规格唯一标识。

4. **设计规范自动校验**：按品类维护印刷设计规范（出血、格式、分辨率、色彩模式），文件上传时通过 `DesignSpecValidationService` 自动校验，前端即时反馈不符合规范的文件。

5. **搜索与缓存分离**：商品搜索采用 Laravel Scout + Meilisearch 实现全文检索与热度排序；分类树、参数模板等低频变更数据使用 Redis 缓存，实时计价结果使用短期缓存（5 分钟）。

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph 数据层
        P[products] --> PC[product_categories]
        P --> PI[product_images]
        P --> PS[product_skus]
        PC --> PT[param_templates]
        PT --> PTO[param_template_options]
        PT --> PTR[param_template_rules]
        PC --> PDS[product_design_specs]
    end

    subgraph 领域层
        A1[CreateProductAction] --> P
        A2[UpdateProductParamsAction] --> PT
        A3[GenerateCpSummaryAction] --> CS[CpSummaryService]
        A4[ParseCpSummaryAction] --> CS
        A5[ValidateDesignFileAction] --> DSV[DesignSpecValidationService]
    end

    subgraph 服务层
        PSS[ProductSearchService] --> MEI[Meilisearch]
        PTS[ParamTemplateService] --> PTR
        FME[FileMetadataExtractorService] --> MIN[MinIO]
    end

    subgraph 前端
        F1[商品列表] --> PSS
        F2[参数选择] --> PTS
        F3[文件上传] --> A5
        F4[实时计价] --> A3
    end
```

---

### 6.42.2 枚举定义

#### ProductStatus

商品生命周期状态机，覆盖从草稿到上架到归档的完整流程。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 商品状态
 */
enum ProductStatus: int
{
    case DRAFT     = 0;  // 草稿
    case PENDING   = 1;  // 待审核
    case ACTIVE    = 2;  // 上架中
    case INACTIVE  = 3;  // 已下架
    case ARCHIVED  = 4;  // 已归档

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::DRAFT    => '草稿',
            self::PENDING  => '待审核',
            self::ACTIVE   => '上架中',
            self::INACTIVE => '已下架',
            self::ARCHIVED => '已归档',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否前端可见
     */
    public function isVisible(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::ACTIVE;
    }

    /**
     * 状态机：允许的目标状态校验
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::DRAFT, self::PENDING],
            [self::PENDING, self::ACTIVE],
            [self::PENDING, self::DRAFT],
            [self::ACTIVE, self::INACTIVE],
            [self::INACTIVE, self::ACTIVE],
            [self::INACTIVE, self::ARCHIVED],
            [self::ACTIVE, self::ARCHIVED] => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }
}
```

#### ParamType

参数模板中控件类型定义，决定前端渲染组件与校验逻辑。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 参数模板控件类型
 */
enum ParamType: string
{
    case SELECT      = 'SELECT';      // 下拉选择
    case RADIO       = 'RADIO';       // 单选
    case CHECKBOX    = 'CHECKBOX';    // 多选
    case NUMBER      = 'NUMBER';      // 数字输入
    case TEXT        = 'TEXT';        // 文本输入
    case IMAGE_UPLOAD = 'IMAGE_UPLOAD'; // 图片上传
    case FILE_UPLOAD  = 'FILE_UPLOAD';  // 文件上传
    case COLOR       = 'COLOR';       // 颜色选择

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::SELECT       => '下拉选择',
            self::RADIO        => '单选',
            self::CHECKBOX     => '多选',
            self::NUMBER       => '数字输入',
            self::TEXT         => '文本输入',
            self::IMAGE_UPLOAD => '图片上传',
            self::FILE_UPLOAD  => '文件上传',
            self::COLOR        => '颜色选择',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为选项型控件（需要 options 配置）
     */
    public function isOptionBased(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::SELECT, self::RADIO, self::CHECKBOX], true);
    }

    /**
     * 是否支持多值
     */
    public function allowsMultiple(): bool
    {
        return $this === self::CHECKBOX;
    }
}
```

#### FileFormat

上传文件格式枚举，用于设计文件校验与缩略图生成策略选择。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 设计文件格式
 */
enum FileFormat: int
{
    case PDF  = 1;
    case AI   = 2;
    case PSD  = 3;
    case CDR  = 4;
    case JPG  = 5;
    case PNG  = 6;
    case TIFF = 7;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PDF  => 'PDF',
            self::AI   => 'AI',
            self::PSD  => 'PSD',
            self::CDR  => 'CDR',
            self::JPG  => 'JPG',
            self::PNG  => 'PNG',
            self::TIFF => 'TIFF',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为矢量格式
     */
    public function isVector(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::PDF, self::AI, self::CDR], true);
    }

    /**
     * 是否为位图格式
     */
    public function isRaster(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::JPG, self::PNG, self::TIFF, self::PSD], true);
    }

    /**
     * 文件扩展名
     */
    public function extension(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PDF  => 'pdf',
            self::AI   => 'ai',
            self::PSD  => 'psd',
            self::CDR  => 'cdr',
            self::JPG  => 'jpg',
            self::PNG  => 'png',
            self::TIFF => 'tiff',
        };
    }

    /**
     * MIME 类型
     */
    public function mimeType(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PDF  => 'application/pdf',
            self::AI   => 'application/postscript',
            self::PSD  => 'image/vnd.adobe.photoshop',
            self::CDR  => 'application/coreldraw',
            self::JPG  => 'image/jpeg',
            self::PNG  => 'image/png',
            self::TIFF => 'image/tiff',
        };
    }
}
```

#### ColorMode

印刷色彩模式枚举，用于设计规范校验与印前检测配置。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 印刷色彩模式
 */
enum ColorMode: int
{
    case CMYK      = 1;
    case RGB       = 2;
    case GRAYSCALE = 3;
    case SPOT      = 4;

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::CMYK      => 'CMYK',
            self::RGB       => 'RGB',
            self::GRAYSCALE => '灰度',
            self::SPOT      => '专色',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否适合印刷输出
     */
    public function isPrintReady(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::CMYK, self::GRAYSCALE, self::SPOT], true);
    }
}
```

---

### 6.42.3 Migration

> **兼容性说明**：`products`、`product_categories`、`param_templates` 已在 SDD 5.2.19 ~ 5.2.21 节定义基础结构；本节在其基础上扩展字段并补充关联表。`product_design_specs` 与 supplement_tables.md 5.2.A3 完全一致，此处完整复现以保持子系统闭环。

#### products 表（扩展）

在既有 `products` 表基础上扩展商品卡片字段（labels、is_new、heat_value、score），并统一金额 Cast。

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('products', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id()->comment('商品主键');
            $table->foreignId('category_id')->constrained('product_categories')->comment('品类ID');
            $table->string('name', 128)->comment('商品名称');
            $table->string('product_type', 16)->nullable()->comment('商品类型编码，如 MP=名片');
            $table->decimal('base_price', 12, 2)->default(0)->comment('基础价格');
            $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(1)->comment('ProductStatus: 0草稿 1待审核 2上架 3下架 4归档');
            $table->text('description')->nullable()->comment('商品描述');
            $table->string('thumbnail', 500)->nullable()->comment('缩略图URL');
            $table->boolean('is_sample')->default(false)->comment('是否样品商品');
            $table->boolean('is_new')->default(false)->comment('是否新品');
            $table->json('labels')->nullable()->comment('卖点标签，如 ["高清印刷","免费设计"]');
            $table->unsignedInteger('heat_value')->default(0)->comment('热度值');
            $table->decimal('score', 3, 1)->default(5.0)->comment('评分 0.0~5.0');
            $table->timestamps();
            $table->softDeletes();

            $table->index('category_id', 'idx_category_id');
            $table->index('status', 'idx_status');
            $table->index(['category_id', 'status'], 'idx_category_status');
            $table->index('heat_value', 'idx_heat_value');
            $table->index('product_type', 'idx_product_type');
            $table->fullText('name', 'idx_name_fulltext');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('products');
    }
};
```

---

### 6.42.4 Eloquent 模型

#### Product 模型

集成 Scout 搜索、支持商品卡片全字段、关联图集与 SKU。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Product\Models;

use App\Domains\Common\Castables\MoneyCast;
use App\Enums\ProductStatus;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\SoftDeletes;
use Laravel\Scout\Searchable;

class Product extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;
    use Searchable;
    use SoftDeletes;

    protected $table = 'products';

    protected $fillable = [
        'category_id', 'name', 'product_type', 'base_price', 'status',
        'description', 'thumbnail', 'is_sample', 'is_new',
        'labels', 'heat_value', 'score',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'category_id' => 'integer',
        'base_price' => MoneyCast::class,
        'status' => ProductStatus::class,
        'is_sample' => 'boolean',
        'is_new' => 'boolean',
        'labels' => 'array',
        'heat_value' => 'integer',
        'score' => 'decimal:1',
    ];

    // -- Scout 搜索索引 --

    public function toSearchableArray(): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'name' => $this->name,
            'product_type' => $this->product_type,
            'category_id' => $this->category_id,
            'status' => $this->status?->value,
            'is_new' => $this->is_new,
            'labels' => $this->labels,
            'heat_value' => $this->heat_value,
            'score' => $this->score,
            'description' => $this->description,
        ];
    }

    // -- Relations --

    public function category(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(ProductCategory::class, 'category_id');
    }

    public function images(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ProductImage::class, 'product_id');
    }

    public function primaryImage(): ?ProductImage
    {
        return $this->images()->where('is_primary', true)->first()
            ?? $this->images()->orderBy('sort_order')->first();
    }

    public function skus(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ProductSku::class, 'product_id');
    }

    public function paramTemplates(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ParamTemplate::class, 'category_id', 'category_id');
    }

    // -- Query Scopes --

    public function scopeActive($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', ProductStatus::ACTIVE);
    }

    public function scopeVisible($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', ProductStatus::ACTIVE)
                     ->whereHas('category', fn ($q) => $q->where('is_show', true));
    }

    public function scopeOfCategory($query, int $categoryId)
    {
        return $query->where('category_id', $categoryId);
    }

    public function scopeNewArrivals($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_new', true)->orderByDesc('created_at');
    }

    public function scopeHot($query)
    {
        return $query->orderByDesc('heat_value')->orderByDesc('score');
    }

    // -- Helpers --

    /**
     * 获取商品完整卡片数据（供前端列表/详情使用）
     */
    public function toCardArray(): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'name' => $this->name,
            'thumbnail' => $this->primaryImage()?->thumbnail_url ?? $this->thumbnail,
            'labels' => $this->labels ?? [],
            'is_new' => $this->is_new,
            'heat_value' => $this->heat_value,
            'score' => $this->score,
            'base_price' => $this->base_price,
        ];
    }
}
```

#### ProductSku 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Product\Models;

use App\Domains\Common\Castables\MoneyCast;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class ProductSku extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'product_skus';

    protected $fillable = [
        'product_id', 'sku_code', 'cp_summary', 'cp_summary_hash',
        'sale_price', 'market_price', 'stock_qty', 'locked_qty', 'status',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'product_id' => 'integer',
        'sale_price' => MoneyCast::class,
        'market_price' => MoneyCast::class,
        'stock_qty' => 'integer',
        'locked_qty' => 'integer',
        'status' => 'integer',
    ];

    public function product(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Product::class, 'product_id');
    }

    /**
     * 可用库存
     */
    public function availableStock(): int
    {
        return max(0, $this->stock_qty - $this->locked_qty);
    }

    /**
     * 锁定库存
     */
    public function lock(int $qty): void
    {
        if ($this->availableStock() < $qty) {
            throw new \App\Exceptions\ProductException('库存不足');
        }
        $this->increment('locked_qty', $qty);
    }

    /**
     * 释放库存
     */
    public function release(int $qty): void
    {
        $this->decrement('locked_qty', min($qty, $this->locked_qty));
    }
}
```

#### ProductCategory 模型

与 SDD 5.2.20 节一致，补充 `paramTemplates` 关联的返回类型声明。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Product\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class ProductCategory extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'product_categories';

    protected $fillable = [
        'cd_category_id', 'category_name', 'parent_id', 'level',
        'sort_order', 'icon', 'is_show', 'heat_value', 'score', 'labels',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'level' => 'integer',
        'sort_order' => 'integer',
        'heat_value' => 'integer',
        'score' => 'decimal:1',
        'is_show' => 'boolean',
        'labels' => 'array',
    ];

    public function parent(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(self::class, 'parent_id');
    }

    public function children(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(self::class, 'parent_id');
    }

    public function products(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(Product::class, 'category_id');
    }

    public function paramTemplates(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ParamTemplate::class, 'category_id');
    }

    public function designSpec(): ?ProductDesignSpec
    {
        return $this->hasOne(ProductDesignSpec::class, 'category_id')->first();
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：仅展示的分类
     */
    public function scopeShown($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_show', true);
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：指定层级
     */
    public function scopeAtLevel($query, int $level)
    {
        return $query->where('level', $level);
    }
}
```

#### ParamTemplate 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Product\Models;

use App\Enums\ParamType;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class ParamTemplate extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'param_templates';

    protected $fillable = [
        'category_id', 'group_name', 'param_key', 'param_type',
        'param_name', 'meta', 'version', 'sort_order', 'status',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'category_id' => 'integer',
        'param_type' => ParamType::class,
        'version' => 'integer',
        'sort_order' => 'integer',
        'status' => 'integer',
        'meta' => 'array',
    ];

    public function category(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(ProductCategory::class, 'category_id');
    }

    public function options(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ParamTemplateOption::class, 'param_id');
    }

    public function rules(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(ParamTemplateRule::class, 'param_id');
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前启用的选项列表
     */
    public function activeOptions(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->options()->where('status', 1)->orderBy('sort_order');
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前启用的联动规则
     */
    public function activeRules(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->rules()->where('status', 1)->orderByDesc('priority');
    }
}
```

#### ProductDesignSpec 模型

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Product\Models;

use App\Enums\ColorMode;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class ProductDesignSpec extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $table = 'product_design_specs';

    protected $fillable = [
        'category_id', 'design_size', 'finished_size', 'bleed',
        'allowed_formats', 'resolution', 'color_mode', 'meta',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'category_id' => 'integer',
        'color_mode' => ColorMode::class,
        'allowed_formats' => 'array',
        'meta' => 'array',
    ];

    public function category(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(ProductCategory::class, 'category_id');
    }

    /**
     * 是否允许指定文件格式
     */
    public function allowsFormat(int $formatValue): bool
    {
        return in_array($formatValue, $this->allowed_formats ?? [], true);
    }

    /**
     * 获取规范摘要文本（用于前端提示）
     */
    public function toGuidelineText(): string
    {
        $parts = [];
        if ($this->design_size) {
            $parts[] = "设计尺寸：{$this->design_size}";
        }
        if ($this->finished_size) {
            $parts[] = "成品尺寸：{$this->finished_size}";
        }
        if ($this->bleed) {
            $parts[] = "出血：{$this->bleed}";
        }
        if ($this->resolution) {
            $parts[] = "分辨率：{$this->resolution}";
        }
        if ($this->color_mode) {
            $parts[] = "色彩模式：{$this->color_mode->label()}";
        }
        return implode('；', $parts);
    }
}
```
