### 6.42.5 Action 类

#### CreateProductAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\Product;
use App\Enums\ProductStatus;
use App\Exceptions\ProductException;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 创建商品及关联图集
 * FR-PROD-001: 商品创建
 */
class CreateProductAction
{
    /**
     * @param array $data 商品基础数据
     * @param array $images 图片URL列表 [['url'=>'...','is_primary'=>true],...]
     */
    public function execute(array $data, array $images = []): Product
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($data, $images) {
            $product = Product::create([
                'category_id' => $data['category_id'],
                'name' => $data['name'],
                'product_type' => $data['product_type'] ?? null,
                'base_price' => $data['base_price'] ?? 0,
                'status' => $data['status'] ?? ProductStatus::DRAFT,
                'description' => $data['description'] ?? null,
                'thumbnail' => $images[0]['url'] ?? null,
                'is_sample' => $data['is_sample'] ?? false,
                'is_new' => $data['is_new'] ?? false,
                'labels' => $data['labels'] ?? [],
                'heat_value' => $data['heat_value'] ?? 0,
                'score' => $data['score'] ?? 5.0,
            ]);

            foreach ($images as $index => $image) {
                $product->images()->create([
                    'image_url' => $image['url'],
                    'thumbnail_url' => $image['thumbnail_url'] ?? $image['url'],
                    'sort_order' => $index,
                    'is_primary' => $image['is_primary'] ?? ($index === 0),
                ]);
            }

            Log::info('[Product] 创建商品', ['product_id' => $product->id]);

            return $product;
        });
    }
}
```

#### UpdateProductParamsAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\ParamTemplate;
use App\Domains\Product\Models\ParamTemplateOption;
use App\Domains\Product\Models\ParamTemplateRule;
use App\Enums\ParamType;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

/**
 * 更新品类参数模板、选项及联动规则
 * FR-PROD-020 ~ FR-PROD-035: 参数模板管理
 */
class UpdateProductParamsAction
{
    /**
     * @param int $categoryId 品类ID
     * @param array $params 参数模板列表
     * @param array $options 选项列表 [paramKey => [[value, label, price_delta],...],...]
     * @param array $rules 联动规则列表
     */
    public function execute(int $categoryId, array $params, array $options = [], array $rules = []): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($categoryId, $params, $options, $rules) {
            $version = ParamTemplate::where('category_id', $categoryId)->max('version') + 1;
            $paramIdMap = [];

            foreach ($params as $index => $param) {
                $template = ParamTemplate::updateOrCreate(
                    [
                        'category_id' => $categoryId,
                        'param_key' => $param['param_key'],
                    ],
                    [
                        'group_name' => $param['group_name'] ?? null,
                        'param_type' => ParamType::from($param['param_type']),
                        'param_name' => $param['param_name'],
                        'meta' => $param['meta'] ?? null,
                        'version' => $version,
                        'sort_order' => $index,
                        'status' => $param['status'] ?? 1,
                    ]
                );
                $paramIdMap[$param['param_key']] = $template->id;
            }

            foreach ($options as $paramKey => $opts) {
                if (! isset($paramIdMap[$paramKey])) {
                    continue;
                }
                $paramId = $paramIdMap[$paramKey];
                ParamTemplateOption::where('param_id', $paramId)->delete();
                foreach ($opts as $sort => $opt) {
                    ParamTemplateOption::create([
                        'param_id' => $paramId,
                        'value' => $opt['value'],
                        'label' => $opt['label'],
                        'price_delta' => $opt['price_delta'] ?? 0,
                        'sort_order' => $sort,
                        'status' => $opt['status'] ?? 1,
                    ]);
                }
            }

            foreach ($rules as $rule) {
                $paramId = $paramIdMap[$rule['param_key']] ?? null;
                if (! $paramId) {
                    continue;
                }
                ParamTemplateRule::updateOrCreate(
                    [
                        'param_id' => $paramId,
                        'condition_param' => $rule['condition_param'],
                        'condition_value' => $rule['condition_value'],
                        'action_param' => $rule['action_param'],
                    ],
                    [
                        'rule_type' => $rule['rule_type'] ?? 'DISABLE',
                        'action_value' => $rule['action_value'] ?? null,
                        'priority' => $rule['priority'] ?? 0,
                        'status' => $rule['status'] ?? 1,
                    ]
                );
            }

            Log::info('[Product] 更新参数模板', [
                'category_id' => $categoryId,
                'version' => $version,
                'param_count' => count($params),
            ]);
        });
    }
}
```

#### ValidateDesignFileAction

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\ProductCategory;
use App\Enums\FileFormat;
use App\Exceptions\ProductException;
use App\Services\Product\DesignSpecValidationService;
use App\Services\Product\FileMetadataExtractorService;
use Illuminate\Http\UploadedFile;

/**
 * 设计文件上传校验
 * FR-PROD-050 ~ FR-PROD-055: 文件格式/尺寸/分辨率/色彩模式校验
 */
class ValidateDesignFileAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private readonly DesignSpecValidationService $designSpecService,
        private readonly FileMetadataExtractorService $fileMetaService,
    ) {
    }

    /**
     * @param int $categoryId 品类ID
     * @param UploadedFile $file 上传文件
     * @return array 校验通过返回文件元数据 ['format'=>FileFormat, 'width'=>..., 'height'=>..., 'dpi'=>..., 'color_mode'=>...]
     * @throws ProductException
     */
    public function execute(int $categoryId, UploadedFile $file): array
    {
        $category = ProductCategory::findOrFail($categoryId);
        $spec = $category->designSpec();

        if (! $spec) {
            throw new ProductException('该品类尚未配置设计规范');
        }

        // 1. 格式校验
        $format = $this->fileMetaService->detectFormat($file);
        if (! $spec->allowsFormat($format->value)) {
            throw new ProductException(
                "不支持的文件格式：{$format->label()}，该品类仅支持：" .
                implode(',', array_map(
                    fn (int $v) => FileFormat::from($v)->label(),
                    $spec->allowed_formats ?? []
                ))
            );
        }

        // 2. 元数据提取与规范校验
        $meta = $this->fileMetaService->extract($file, $format);
        $violations = $this->designSpecService->validate($spec, $meta);

        if (! empty($violations)) {
            throw new ProductException('文件不符合设计规范：' . implode('；', $violations));
        }

        return array_merge($meta, ['format' => $format->value]);
    }
}
```


---

### 6.42.6 Service 类

#### ProductSearchService

基于 Laravel Scout + Meilisearch 的商品搜索服务，支持关键词全文检索、分类过滤、热度排序与新品筛选。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\Product;
use App\Enums\ProductStatus;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;
use Meilisearch\Client;

class ProductSearchService
{
    public function __construct(
        private readonly Client $meilisearch
    ) {
    }

    /**
     * 关键词搜索商品
     *
     * @param string $keyword 搜索关键词
     * @param array $filters 过滤条件 ['category_id'=>int, 'is_new'=>bool, 'min_price'=>float, 'max_price'=>float]
     * @param string $sort 排序方式: relevance/heat/price_asc/price_desc/newest
     * @param int $perPage 每页数量
     */
    public function search(
        string $keyword,
        array $filters = [],
        string $sort = 'relevance',
        int $perPage = 20
    ): LengthAwarePaginator {
        $query = Product::search($keyword, function (Client $client, string $query, array $options) use ($filters, $sort) {
            $filterExpr = ["status = " . ProductStatus::ACTIVE->value];

            if (isset($filters['category_id'])) {
                $filterExpr[] = "category_id = {$filters['category_id']}";
            }
            if (isset($filters['is_new']) && $filters['is_new']) {
                $filterExpr[] = "is_new = true";
            }
            if (isset($filters['min_price'])) {
                $filterExpr[] = "base_price >= {$filters['min_price']}";
            }
            if (isset($filters['max_price'])) {
                $filterExpr[] = "base_price <= {$filters['max_price']}";
            }

            $options['filter'] = implode(' AND ', $filterExpr);

            $options['sort'] = match ($sort) {
                'heat' => ['heat_value:desc', 'score:desc'],
                'price_asc' => ['base_price:asc'],
                'price_desc' => ['base_price:desc'],
                'newest' => ['created_at:desc'],
                default => [],
            };

            return $client->index('products')->search($query, $options);
        });

        return $query->paginate($perPage);
    }

    /**
     * 热搜商品（按热度值降序）
     */
    public function hotProducts(int $limit = 12): array
    {
        return Product::search('', function (Client $client, string $query, array $options) use ($limit) {
            $options['filter'] = "status = " . ProductStatus::ACTIVE->value;
            $options['sort'] = ['heat_value:desc', 'score:desc'];
            $options['limit'] = $limit;
            return $client->index('products')->search($query, $options);
        })->raw()['hits'] ?? [];
    }

    /**
     * 同步索引配置（建议在部署脚本或 Command 中调用）
     */
    public function configureIndex(): void
    {
        $index = $this->meilisearch->index('products');
        $index->updateFilterableAttributes(['category_id', 'status', 'is_new', 'base_price']);
        $index->updateSortableAttributes(['heat_value', 'score', 'base_price', 'created_at']);
        $index->updateSearchableAttributes(['name', 'description', 'labels', 'product_type']);
    }
}
```

#### ParamTemplateService

参数模板与联动规则引擎的核心服务，负责参数可用性计算与前端渲染数据组装。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\ParamTemplate;
use App\Domains\Product\Models\ParamTemplateRule;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class ParamTemplateService
{
    private const CACHE_TTL = 3600; // 1小时

    /**
     * 获取品类下的完整参数模板（含选项与规则），带缓存
     */
    public function getTemplatesForCategory(int $categoryId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = "param_templates:{$categoryId}";

        return Cache::remember($cacheKey, self::CACHE_TTL, function () use ($categoryId) {
            $templates = ParamTemplate::with(['options', 'rules'])
                ->where('category_id', $categoryId)
                ->where('status', 1)
                ->orderBy('sort_order')
                ->get();

            return $templates->map(fn (ParamTemplate $t) => [
                'id' => $t->id,
                'group_name' => $t->group_name,
                'param_key' => $t->param_key,
                'param_type' => $t->param_type?->value,
                'param_name' => $t->param_name,
                'meta' => $t->meta,
                'options' => $t->options->map(fn ($o) => [
                    'value' => $o->value,
                    'label' => $o->label,
                    'price_delta' => $o->price_delta,
                ])->values(),
                'rules' => $t->rules->map(fn ($r) => [
                    'rule_type' => $r->rule_type,
                    'condition_param' => $r->condition_param,
                    'condition_value' => $r->condition_value,
                    'action_param' => $r->action_param,
                    'action_value' => $r->action_value,
                    'priority' => $r->priority,
                ])->values(),
            ])->values()->all();
        });
    }

    /**
     * 根据当前选中值计算各参数可用状态
     *
     * @param int $categoryId 品类ID
     * @param array $selectedValues 当前选中值 [paramKey => value, ...]
     * @return array 各参数可用选项与禁用状态
     */
    public function computeAvailability(int $categoryId, array $selectedValues): array
    {
        $templates = $this->getTemplatesForCategory($categoryId);
        $result = [];

        foreach ($templates as $template) {
            $paramKey = $template['param_key'];
            $availableOptions = [];
            $disabledOptions = [];
            $hidden = false;

            foreach ($template['options'] as $option) {
                $isDisabled = $this->isOptionDisabled(
                    $template['rules'],
                    $selectedValues,
                    $paramKey,
                    $option['value']
                );

                if ($isDisabled) {
                    $disabledOptions[] = $option['value'];
                } else {
                    $availableOptions[] = $option;
                }
            }

            // 检查整个参数是否被隐藏
            $hidden = $this->isParamHidden($template['rules'], $selectedValues, $paramKey);

            $result[$paramKey] = [
                'param_type' => $template['param_type'],
                'available_options' => $availableOptions,
                'disabled_options' => $disabledOptions,
                'hidden' => $hidden,
            ];
        }

        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * 判断选项是否被联动规则禁用
     */
    private function isOptionDisabled(array $rules, array $selected, string $targetParam, string $targetValue): bool
    {
        foreach ($rules as $rule) {
            if ($rule['rule_type'] !== 'DISABLE') {
                continue;
            }
            if ($rule['action_param'] !== $targetParam) {
                continue;
            }
            if ($rule['action_value'] !== null && $rule['action_value'] !== $targetValue) {
                continue;
            }
            // 条件匹配：当前选中的 condition_param 值等于 condition_value
            $currentValue = $selected[$rule['condition_param']] ?? null;
            if ($currentValue !== null && $currentValue == $rule['condition_value']) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * 判断参数是否被联动规则隐藏
     */
    private function isParamHidden(array $rules, array $selected, string $targetParam): bool
    {
        foreach ($rules as $rule) {
            if ($rule['rule_type'] !== 'HIDE') {
                continue;
            }
            if ($rule['action_param'] !== $targetParam) {
                continue;
            }
            $currentValue = $selected[$rule['condition_param']] ?? null;
            if ($currentValue !== null && $currentValue == $rule['condition_value']) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * 清除品类参数模板缓存
     */
    public function clearCache(int $categoryId): void
    {
        Cache::forget("param_templates:{$categoryId}");
    }
}
```

#### CpSummaryService

cpSummary 的生成与反解析服务，是连接前端参数面板与后端计价/订单的核心纽带。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Exceptions\ProductException;

/**
 * cpSummary 格式：productType:size:style:binding:reprint:designOrder:groupParams:pageCount:totalPages:quantity:skuCount
 * 示例：MP:90x54:STANDARD::0:1:PAPER_300G,COAT_MATTE:2:4:500:1
 */
class CpSummaryService
{
    private const DELIMITER = ':';
    private const PART_COUNT = 11;

    private const FIELD_NAMES = [
        'product_type',
        'size',
        'style',
        'binding',
        'reprint',
        'design_order',
        'group_params',
        'page_count',
        'total_pages',
        'quantity',
        'sku_count',
    ];

    /**
     * 生成 cpSummary 字符串
     */
    public function generate(
        string $productType,
        array $params,
        int $quantity,
        int $skuCount = 1
    ): string {
        $parts = [
            $productType,
            $params['size'] ?? '',
            $params['style'] ?? '',
            $params['binding'] ?? '',
            $params['reprint'] ?? '0',
            $params['design_order'] ?? '0',
            $params['group_params'] ?? '',
            $params['page_count'] ?? '',
            $params['total_pages'] ?? '',
            (string) $quantity,
            (string) $skuCount,
        ];

        return implode(self::DELIMITER, $parts);
    }

    /**
     * 反解析 cpSummary 为关联数组
     */
    public function parse(string $cpSummary): array
    {
        $parts = explode(self::DELIMITER, $cpSummary);

        if (count($parts) !== self::PART_COUNT) {
            throw new ProductException("cpSummary 格式错误：期望 {self::PART_COUNT} 段，实际 " . count($parts));
        }

        $result = [];
        foreach (self::FIELD_NAMES as $index => $name) {
            $result[$name] = $parts[$index] !== '' ? $parts[$index] : null;
        }

        // group_params 反解析为数组
        if (! empty($result['group_params'])) {
            $result['group_params_array'] = explode(',', $result['group_params']);
        }

        // 数值型字段转换
        $result['reprint'] = (int) ($result['reprint'] ?? 0);
        $result['design_order'] = (int) ($result['design_order'] ?? 0);
        $result['page_count'] = $result['page_count'] !== null ? (int) $result['page_count'] : null;
        $result['total_pages'] = $result['total_pages'] !== null ? (int) $result['total_pages'] : null;
        $result['quantity'] = (int) $result['quantity'];
        $result['sku_count'] = (int) $result['sku_count'];

        return $result;
    }

    /**
     * 校验 cpSummary 合法性（不反解析，仅格式校验）
     */
    public function validate(string $cpSummary): bool
    {
        $parts = explode(self::DELIMITER, $cpSummary);
        return count($parts) === self::PART_COUNT && $parts[0] !== '';
    }

    /**
     * 计算 cpSummary 的 MD5 哈希（用于 SKU 匹配与缓存键）
     */
    public function hash(string $cpSummary): string
    {
        return md5($cpSummary);
    }

    /**
     * 判断两个 cpSummary 是否代表同一规格（忽略数量差异）
     */
    public function isSameSpec(string $a, string $b): bool
    {
        $pa = $this->parse($a);
        $pb = $this->parse($b);

        // 忽略 quantity 和 sku_count
        unset($pa['quantity'], $pa['sku_count'], $pb['quantity'], $pb['sku_count']);

        return $pa === $pb;
    }
}
```

#### DesignSpecValidationService

设计规范校验服务，将文件元数据与品类设计规范逐条比对。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Domains\Product\Models\ProductDesignSpec;
use App\Enums\ColorMode;

class DesignSpecValidationService
{
    /**
     * 校验文件元数据是否符合品类设计规范
     *
     * @return array 违规项文本列表，空数组表示全部通过
     */
    public function validate(ProductDesignSpec $spec, array $fileMeta): array
    {
        $violations = [];

        // 分辨率校验
        if (! empty($spec->resolution) && isset($fileMeta['dpi'])) {
            $requiredDpi = (int) filter_var($spec->resolution, FILTER_SANITIZE_NUMBER_INT);
            if ($fileMeta['dpi'] < $requiredDpi) {
                $violations[] = "分辨率不足：当前 {$fileMeta['dpi']}dpi，要求 ≥ {$requiredDpi}dpi";
            }
        }

        // 色彩模式校验
        if ($spec->color_mode !== null && isset($fileMeta['color_mode'])) {
            $fileColorMode = is_int($fileMeta['color_mode'])
                ? ColorMode::from($fileMeta['color_mode'])
                : null;
            if ($fileColorMode && $fileColorMode !== $spec->color_mode && ! $fileColorMode->isPrintReady()) {
                $violations[] = "色彩模式不符：当前 {$fileColorMode->label()}，建议 {$spec->color_mode->label()}";
            }
        }

        // 尺寸校验（允许 ±2mm 误差）
        if (! empty($spec->design_size) && isset($fileMeta['width_mm'], $fileMeta['height_mm'])) {
            [$reqW, $reqH] = $this->parseSize($spec->design_size);
            $tolerance = 2.0; // mm
            if (abs($fileMeta['width_mm'] - $reqW) > $tolerance || abs($fileMeta['height_mm'] - $reqH) > $tolerance) {
                $violations[] = "尺寸不符：当前 {$fileMeta['width_mm']}×{$fileMeta['height_mm']}mm，要求 {$reqW}×{$reqH}mm（±2mm）";
            }
        }

        // 扩展规范校验（最小字号等）
        if (! empty($spec->meta['min_font_size']) && isset($fileMeta['min_font_size_pt'])) {
            if ($fileMeta['min_font_size_pt'] < $spec->meta['min_font_size']) {
                $violations[] = "字号过小：最小字号 {$fileMeta['min_font_size_pt']}pt，要求 ≥ {$spec->meta['min_font_size']}pt";
            }
        }

        return $violations;
    }

    /**
     * 解析尺寸字符串 "210×285mm" 为 [210.0, 285.0]
     */
    private function parseSize(string $size): array
    {
        $clean = preg_replace('/[^0-9×xX,.]/', '', $size);
        $parts = preg_split('/[×xX]/', $clean);
        return [
            (float) str_replace(',', '.', $parts[0] ?? '0'),
            (float) str_replace(',', '.', $parts[1] ?? '0'),
        ];
    }
}
```

#### FileMetadataExtractorService

文件元数据提取服务，支持 PDF/AI/PSD/CDR/JPG/PNG/TIFF 的格式识别与关键信息提取。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\Product;

use App\Enums\FileFormat;
use Illuminate\Http\UploadedFile;
use Imagick;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class FileMetadataExtractorService
{
    /**
     * 检测文件格式
     */
    public function detectFormat(UploadedFile $file): FileFormat
    {
        $ext = strtolower($file->getClientOriginalExtension());
        $mime = $file->getMimeType();

        return match (true) {
            $ext === 'pdf' || $mime === 'application/pdf' => FileFormat::PDF,
            $ext === 'ai'  || str_contains($mime, 'postscript') => FileFormat::AI,
            $ext === 'psd' || $mime === 'image/vnd.adobe.photoshop' => FileFormat::PSD,
            $ext === 'cdr' => FileFormat::CDR,
            $ext === 'jpg' || $ext === 'jpeg' || $mime === 'image/jpeg' => FileFormat::JPG,
            $ext === 'png' || $mime === 'image/png' => FileFormat::PNG,
            $ext === 'tiff' || $ext === 'tif' || $mime === 'image/tiff' => FileFormat::TIFF,
            default => throw new \App\Exceptions\ProductException('无法识别的文件格式'),
        };
    }

    /**
     * 提取文件元数据（分辨率、尺寸、色彩模式等）
     *
     * @return array ['width_px'=>int, 'height_px'=>int, 'width_mm'=>float, 'height_mm'=>float, 'dpi'=>int, 'color_mode'=>int|ColorMode]
     */
    public function extract(UploadedFile $file, FileFormat $format): array
    {
        $meta = [
            'width_px' => null,
            'height_px' => null,
            'width_mm' => null,
            'height_mm' => null,
            'dpi' => null,
            'color_mode' => null,
        ];

        // 位图格式统一使用 Imagick 提取
        if ($format->isRaster() || $format === FileFormat::PDF) {
            $meta = array_merge($meta, $this->extractWithImagick($file));
        }

        // PDF 额外提取页数
        if ($format === FileFormat::PDF) {
            $meta['page_count'] = $this->extractPdfPageCount($file);
        }

        return $meta;
    }

    /**
     * 生成缩略图并上传至 MinIO
     */
    public function generateThumbnail(UploadedFile $file, FileFormat $format, int $maxWidth = 400): string
    {
        $imagick = new Imagick();
        $imagick->setResolution(72, 72);

        if ($format === FileFormat::PDF) {
            $imagick->readImage($file->getRealPath() . '[0]');
        } else {
            $imagick->readImage($file->getRealPath());
        }

        $imagick->setImageFormat('jpg');
        $imagick->thumbnailImage($maxWidth, $maxWidth, true, true);
        $imagick->setImageCompressionQuality(85);

        $filename = 'thumbs/' . uniqid('thumb_', true) . '.jpg';
        Storage::disk('minio')->put($filename, $imagick->getImageBlob());
        $imagick->clear();

        return Storage::disk('minio')->url($filename);
    }

    private function extractWithImagick(UploadedFile $file): array
    {
        $imagick = new Imagick();
        $imagick->setResolution(300, 300);
        $imagick->readImage($file->getRealPath() . ($file->extension() === 'pdf' ? '[0]' : ''));

        $widthPx = $imagick->getImageWidth();
        $heightPx = $imagick->getImageHeight();
        $dpiX = $imagick->getImageResolution()['x'] ?? 72;
        $colorSpace = $imagick->getImageColorspace();

        $imagick->clear();

        return [
            'width_px' => $widthPx,
            'height_px' => $heightPx,
            'width_mm' => round(($widthPx / $dpiX) * 25.4, 2),
            'height_mm' => round(($heightPx / $dpiX) * 25.4, 2),
            'dpi' => (int) $dpiX,
            'color_mode' => match ($colorSpace) {
                Imagick::COLORSPACE_CMYK => 1, // ColorMode::CMYK
                Imagick::COLORSPACE_GRAY => 3, // ColorMode::GRAYSCALE
                default => 2, // ColorMode::RGB
            },
        ];
    }

    private function extractPdfPageCount(UploadedFile $file): int
    {
        $imagick = new Imagick($file->getRealPath());
        $count = $imagick->getNumberImages();
        $imagick->clear();
        return $count;
    }
}
```

---

### 6.42.7 关键业务规则

#### 7.1 cpSummary 生成与反解析规则

**生成规则**：
1. 字段顺序严格固定：`productType` : `size` : `style` : `binding` : `reprint` : `designOrder` : `groupParams` : `pageCount` : `totalPages` : `quantity` : `skuCount`
2. 空字段使用空字符串占位，不得省略分隔符。
3. `groupParams` 为多值参数组合，使用逗号 `,` 拼接（如 `PAPER_300G,COAT_MATTE`）。
4. `productType` 为商品类型缩写，如 `MP`（名片）、`FL`（单张）、`LB`（标签）、`BK`（画册）等。
5. 生成后的 `cpSummary` 经 `CpSummaryService::hash()` 计算 MD5，用于 `product_skus.cp_summary_hash` 的匹配索引。

**反解析规则**：
1. 按 `:` 分割为 11 段，段数不符直接抛 `ProductException`。
2. `groupParams` 按 `,` 拆分为数组回填前端多选参数。
3. 数值型字段（`reprint`、`designOrder`、`pageCount`、`totalPages`、`quantity`、`skuCount`）自动转为 `int`。
4. 反解析结果可直接作为 `ParamTemplateService::computeAvailability()` 的 `selectedValues` 入参，重新计算联动规则后的可用选项。

**缓存策略**：
- `cpSummary` → 计价结果的映射缓存 5 分钟（`price:base:{productId}:{hash}`）。
- 参数模板变更时通过事件监听器清除对应品类的模板缓存与价格缓存。

#### 7.2 联动规则引擎规则

**规则类型**：
| 类型 | 说明 | 示例 |
|------|------|------|
| `DISABLE` | 条件满足时禁用目标参数的指定选项或整个参数 | 选择"铜版纸"时禁用"烫金"选项 |
| `HIDE` | 条件满足时隐藏目标参数 | 选择"单面印刷"时隐藏"反面工艺"参数组 |
| `SET_DEFAULT` | 条件满足时将目标参数设为默认值 | 选择"A4"尺寸时默认"300g铜版纸" |
| `ADJUST_PRICE` | 条件满足时对目标选项价格增量进行调整 | 选择"UV工艺"时"覆膜"选项加价 0.05 元 |

**执行优先级**：
1. 规则按 `priority` 降序执行，高优先级规则可覆盖低优先级规则的结果。
2. 同一参数同一选项被多条规则同时命中的，取优先级最高者；优先级相同时，`DISABLE` > `HIDE` > `ADJUST_PRICE` > `SET_DEFAULT`。
3. 规则计算在前端渲染时进行（`ParamTemplateService::computeAvailability()`），每次参数变更即时重新计算，确保用户始终看到合法的选项组合。

**性能优化**：
- 品类参数模板（含选项与规则）使用 Redis 缓存 1 小时。
- 后台修改参数模板后，通过 `ParamTemplateUpdated` 事件清除缓存并触发 Scout 索引更新（如影响商品基础价格展示）。

#### 7.3 设计规范校验规则

**校验流程**：
1. **格式白名单**：先比对 `product_design_specs.allowed_formats` 与上传文件的实际格式，`FileFormat::isVector()` 和 `FileFormat::isRaster()` 决定后续提取策略。
2. **分辨率下限**：PDF/AI/CDR 等矢量格式不强制分辨率；JPG/PNG/TIFF/PSD 等位图格式必须满足 `≥ 300dpi`（或品类自定义值）。
3. **尺寸容差**：设计尺寸允许 `±2mm` 误差，成品尺寸仅作展示参考，不做强制校验。
4. **色彩模式**：非 `CMYK/GRAYSCALE/SPOT` 的位图文件（如 `RGB`）发出警告但不阻断上传（部分客户设计文件为 RGB，由印前转色处理）。
5. **出血检测**：对 PDF 文件尝试解析裁切框（TrimBox）与媒体框（MediaBox），计算差值是否满足品类出血要求；无法解析时降级为人工审核。

**远程文件处理**：
- 支持远程 URL 下载（`file_get_contents` / Guzzle），下载后落地为 `UploadedFile` 代理对象，复用同一套校验逻辑。
- 远程文件下载超时 30 秒，大小限制 500MB，下载后存入 MinIO 临时桶，校验通过后移至正式桶。

---

#### 时序图：参数选择 + 实时计价

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as 用户
    participant F as 前端页面
    participant PTS as ParamTemplateService
    participant CpS as CpSummaryService
    participant PE as PricingEngine
    participant R as Redis

    U->>F: 进入商品详情页
    F->>PTS: GET /api/products/{id}/params
    PTS->>R: 读取参数模板缓存
    alt 缓存命中
        R-->>PTS: 返回模板数据
    else 缓存未命中
        PTS->>DB: 查询 param_templates + options + rules
        DB-->>PTS: 返回原始数据
        PTS->>R: 写入缓存
    end
    PTS-->>F: 返回分组参数与选项列表
    F->>U: 渲染参数选择面板

    U->>F: 选择"尺寸"=90x54
    F->>PTS: POST /api/products/{id}/param-availability<br/>{selected: {size:"90x54"}}
    PTS->>PTS: 执行联动规则引擎<br/>computeAvailability()
    PTS-->>F: 返回各参数可用/禁用状态
    F->>U: 更新面板（如禁用不支持的材质）

    U->>F: 完成全部参数选择
    F->>CpS: POST /api/cp-summary/generate<br/>{productType:"MP", params:{...}, quantity:500}
    CpS->>CpS: generate()<br/>MP:90x54:STANDARD::0:1:PAPER_300G,COAT_MATTE:2:4:500:1
    CpS-->>F: 返回 cpSummary

    F->>PE: POST /api/price/calculate<br/>{productId, cpSummary, quantity:500}
    PE->>R: 查询价格缓存 price:base:{productId}:{hash}
    alt 缓存命中
        R-->>PE: 返回缓存价格
    else 缓存未命中
        PE->>DB: 查询 price_tiers + param_template_options.price_delta
        DB-->>PE: 返回定价数据
        PE->>PE: 执行计价管线
        PE->>R: 写入价格缓存（5分钟）
    end
    PE-->>F: 返回实时计价结果
    F->>U: 展示价格与加购按钮
```

#### 时序图：文件上传校验

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as 用户
    participant F as 前端页面
    participant V as ValidateDesignFileAction
    participant FME as FileMetadataExtractorService
    participant DSV as DesignSpecValidationService
    participant MIN as MinIO

    U->>F: 上传设计文件
    F->>V: POST /api/design-files/validate<br/>{categoryId, file}
    V->>DB: 查询 product_design_specs
    DB-->>V: 返回品类规范
    V->>FME: detectFormat(file)
    FME-->>V: FileFormat::PDF
    V->>FME: extract(file, PDF)
    FME->>FME: Imagick 提取元数据
    FME-->>V: {width_mm,height_mm,dpi,color_mode,page_count}

    V->>DSV: validate(spec, fileMeta)
    DSV->>DSV: 分辨率/尺寸/色彩模式逐条比对
    alt 存在违规
        DSV-->>V: violations[]
        V-->>F: 422 Unprocessable<br/>{errors: violations}
        F->>U: 展示具体不合规项
    else 校验通过
        DSV-->>V: []
        V->>FME: generateThumbnail(file, PDF)
        FME->>MIN: 上传缩略图
        MIN-->>FME: 返回URL
        FME-->>V: thumbnailUrl
        V-->>F: 200 OK<br/>{meta, thumbnail_url}
        F->>U: 展示缩略图与校验通过提示
    end
```

---


## 6.43 优惠券与促销子系统设计 (CouponPromotionService)

### 6.43.1 设计概述

优惠券与促销子系统承担全平台营销优惠的核心能力，覆盖优惠券生命周期管理（创建→发放→领取→使用→过期）、促销活动配置（限时折扣/满赠/首单/推荐返利）以及优惠叠加规则计算。系统与计价引擎（6.1节）深度集成，在定价管线最后阶段注入优惠抵扣。

**覆盖PRD**：FR-VIP-010 ~ FR-VIP-018

**核心设计原则**：
1. **优惠可叠加但封顶**：VIP折扣与优惠券可叠加（乘法），但最低折扣封顶0.5折
2. **同类型互斥**：同类型折扣取最优惠，不叠加
3. **样品/印品折扣隔离**：VIP印品折扣与样品折扣互斥（取最优惠）
4. **时效驱动**：所有优惠券支持固定有效期或相对有效期（领取后N天）

---

### 6.43.2 枚举定义

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 优惠券类型
 */
enum CouponType: int
{
    case NEW_CUSTOMER = 1;      // 新人礼包
    case SAMPLE_DISCOUNT = 2;   // 样品折扣券
    case SAMPLE_VOUCHER = 3;    // 样品固定金额券（1599/1999/2599）
    case PRINT_DISCOUNT = 4;    // 印品折扣券
    case FULL_REDUCTION = 5;    // 满减券
    case SHIPPING = 6;          // 运费券
    case TIME_LIMIT = 7;        // 限时折扣
    case FIRST_ORDER = 8;       // 首单优惠
    case REFERRAL = 9;          // 推荐返利

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NEW_CUSTOMER => '新人礼包',
            self::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT => '样品折扣券',
            self::SAMPLE_VOUCHER => '样品金额券',
            self::PRINT_DISCOUNT => '印品折扣券',
            self::FULL_REDUCTION => '满减券',
            self::SHIPPING => '运费券',
            self::TIME_LIMIT => '限时折扣',
            self::FIRST_ORDER => '首单优惠',
            self::REFERRAL => '推荐返利',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否与VIP折扣可叠加
     */
    public function isStackableWithVip(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::FULL_REDUCTION, self::SHIPPING, self::TIME_LIMIT], true);
    }

    /**
     * 是否仅限样品订单使用
     */
    public function isSampleOnly(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT, self::SAMPLE_VOUCHER], true);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 客户优惠券状态
 */
enum CustomerCouponStatus: int
{
    case UNUSED = 0;     // 未使用
    case USED = 1;       // 已使用
    case EXPIRED = 2;    // 已过期
    case FROZEN = 3;     // 冻结中（如订单未支付）

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::UNUSED => '未使用',
            self::USED => '已使用',
            self::EXPIRED => '已过期',
            self::FROZEN => '冻结中',
        };
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 优惠券适用范围类型
 */
enum CouponScopeType: int
{
    case ALL = 0;           // 全平台
    case CATEGORY = 1;      // 指定分类
    case PRODUCT = 2;       // 指定商品
    case ORDER_TYPE = 3;    // 指定订单类型

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::ALL => '全平台',
            self::CATEGORY => '指定分类',
            self::PRODUCT => '指定商品',
            self::ORDER_TYPE => '指定订单类型',
        };
    }
}
```

---

### 6.43.3 数据模型与 Migration

#### coupons 表（优惠券模板）

```php
Schema::create('coupons', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->string('code', 32)->unique()->comment('优惠券编码');
    $table->string('name', 100)->comment('优惠券名称');
    $table->foreignId('created_by')->nullable()->constrained('admin_users')->comment('创建人');
    $table->tinyInteger('type')->comment('类型：1新人礼包 2样品折扣 3样品金额券 4印品折扣 5满减 6运费 7限时折扣 8首单 9推荐返利');
    $table->tinyInteger('discount_type')->comment('优惠方式：1百分比折扣 2固定金额抵扣 3免运费');
    $table->decimal('discount_value', 10, 2)->comment('优惠值：百分比时存0.90表示9折，固定金额时存具体金额');
    $table->decimal('min_order_amount', 10, 2)->default(0)->comment('最低订单金额要求');
    $table->decimal('max_discount_amount', 10, 2)->nullable()->comment('最高优惠金额封顶');
    $table->tinyInteger('scope_type')->default(0)->comment('适用范围：0全平台 1分类 2商品 3订单类型');
    $table->json('scope_ids')->nullable()->comment('适用范围ID列表');
    $table->unsignedInteger('total_quantity')->default(0)->comment('总发放数量，0表示不限');
    $table->unsignedInteger('claimed_quantity')->default(0)->comment('已领取数量');
    $table->unsignedInteger('used_quantity')->default(0)->comment('已使用数量');
    $table->timestamp('valid_from')->nullable()->comment('有效期开始');
    $table->timestamp('valid_until')->nullable()->comment('有效期结束');
    $table->unsignedInteger('valid_days_after_claim')->nullable()->comment('领取后N天内有效');
    $table->boolean('is_active')->default(true)->comment('是否启用');
    $table->json('meta')->nullable()->comment('扩展配置：如限时折扣的时段、满赠的赠品ID等');
    $table->timestamps();
    $table->softDeletes();

    $table->index(['type', 'is_active', 'valid_until']);
    $table->index(['scope_type', 'scope_ids'], 'idx_scope');
});
```

#### customer_coupons 表（客户已领取优惠券）

```php
Schema::create('customer_coupons', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->foreignId('customer_id')->constrained('customers')->comment('客户ID');
    $table->foreignId('coupon_id')->constrained('coupons')->comment('优惠券模板ID');
    $table->string('code', 32)->comment('券实例编码');
    $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(0)->comment('状态：0未使用 1已使用 2已过期 3冻结中');
    $table->timestamp('claimed_at')->comment('领取时间');
    $table->timestamp('used_at')->nullable()->comment('使用时间');
    $table->foreignId('used_order_id')->nullable()->constrained('orders')->comment('使用订单ID');
    $table->timestamp('valid_until')->comment('实例有效期截止');
    $table->timestamps();

    $table->unique(['customer_id', 'code']);
    $table->index(['customer_id', 'status', 'valid_until']);
    $table->index(['coupon_id', 'status']);
});
```

#### promotion_activities 表（促销活动）

```php
Schema::create('promotion_activities', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->string('name', 100)->comment('活动名称');
    $table->tinyInteger('type')->comment('活动类型：1限时折扣 2满赠 3首单优惠 4推荐返利');
    $table->json('rules')->comment('活动规则JSON');
    $table->timestamp('start_at')->comment('活动开始');
    $table->timestamp('end_at')->comment('活动结束');
    $table->boolean('is_active')->default(true);
    $table->tinyInteger('vip_min_level')->default(0)->comment('最低VIP等级可参与，0表示全员');
    $table->boolean('vip_only')->default(false)->comment('是否仅限VIP参与');
    $table->timestamps();

    $table->index(['type', 'is_active', 'start_at', 'end_at']);
    $table->index(['vip_min_level', 'vip_only', 'is_active']);
});
```

### 6.43.4 Eloquent 模型

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Marketing;

use App\Enums\CouponType;
use App\Enums\CouponScopeType;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;

class Coupon extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $casts = [
        'type' => CouponType::class,
        'scope_type' => CouponScopeType::class,
        'discount_value' => MoneyCast::class,
        'min_order_amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'max_discount_amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'valid_from' => 'datetime',
        'valid_until' => 'datetime',
        'scope_ids' => 'array',
        'meta' => 'array',
        'is_active' => 'boolean',
    ];

    protected $fillable = [
        'code', 'name', 'type', 'discount_type', 'discount_value',
        'min_order_amount', 'max_discount_amount', 'scope_type', 'scope_ids',
        'total_quantity', 'valid_from', 'valid_until', 'valid_days_after_claim',
        'is_active', 'meta',
    ];

    public function customerCoupons(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(CustomerCoupon::class);
    }

    /**
     * 是否还有库存可领取
     */
    public function hasStock(): bool
    {
        if ($this->total_quantity === 0) {
            return true; // 0表示不限量
        }
        return $this->claimed_quantity < $this->total_quantity;
    }

    /**
     * 当前是否在有效期内
     */
    public function isInValidPeriod(): bool
    {
        $now = now();
        if ($this->valid_from && $now->lt($this->valid_from)) {
            return false;
        }
        if ($this->valid_until && $now->gt($this->valid_until)) {
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Models\Marketing;

use App\Enums\CustomerCouponStatus;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Order\Order;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;

class CustomerCoupon extends Model
{
    use HasFactory;

    protected $casts = [
        'status' => CustomerCouponStatus::class,
        'claimed_at' => 'datetime',
        'used_at' => 'datetime',
        'valid_until' => 'datetime',
    ];

    protected $fillable = [
        'customer_id', 'coupon_id', 'code', 'status',
        'claimed_at', 'used_at', 'used_order_id', 'valid_until',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class);
    }

    public function coupon(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Coupon::class);
    }

    public function usedOrder(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Order::class, 'used_order_id');
    }

    /**
     * 是否可用（未使用、未过期、未冻结）
     */
    public function isUsable(): bool
    {
        return $this->status === CustomerCouponStatus::UNUSED
            && now()->lt($this->valid_until);
    }

    /**
     * 标记为已使用
     */
    public function markAsUsed(int $orderId): void
    {
        $this->update([
            'status' => CustomerCouponStatus::USED,
            'used_at' => now(),
            'used_order_id' => $orderId,
        ]);
    }
}
```

---

### 6.43.5 Action 类

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Marketing;

use App\Enums\CustomerCouponStatus;
use App\Models\Marketing\Coupon;
use App\Models\Marketing\CustomerCoupon;
use App\Exceptions\CouponException;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;

/**
 * 领取优惠券
 * FR-VIP-010: 领取
 */
class ClaimCouponAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, int $couponId): CustomerCoupon
    {
        $coupon = Coupon::findOrFail($couponId);

        throw_unless($coupon->is_active, CouponException::class, '优惠券未启用');
        throw_unless($coupon->isInValidPeriod(), CouponException::class, '优惠券不在有效期内');
        throw_unless($coupon->hasStock(), CouponException::class, '优惠券已领完');

        // 防重复领取（新人礼包等一次性券）
        $exists = CustomerCoupon::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('coupon_id', $couponId)
            ->exists();

        if ($exists && $coupon->type->isSampleOnly()) {
            throw new CouponException('您已领取过该优惠券');
        }

        // 分布式锁防超领
        $lockKey = "coupon:claim:{$couponId}";
        $lock = cache()->lock($lockKey, 10);

        throw_unless($lock->get(), CouponException::class, '领取人数过多，请稍后重试');

        try {
            $customerCoupon = CustomerCoupon::create([
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'coupon_id' => $couponId,
                'code' => strtoupper(Str::random(12)),
                'status' => CustomerCouponStatus::UNUSED,
                'claimed_at' => now(),
                'valid_until' => $this->calculateValidUntil($coupon),
            ]);

            $coupon->increment('claimed_quantity');

            return $customerCoupon;
        } finally {
            $lock->release();
        }
    }

    private function calculateValidUntil(Coupon $coupon): \DateTimeInterface
    {
        if ($coupon->valid_days_after_claim) {
            return now()->addDays($coupon->valid_days_after_claim);
        }
        return $coupon->valid_until ?? now()->addDays(30);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Marketing;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Marketing\Coupon;
use App\Models\Marketing\CustomerCoupon;
use App\Enums\CouponType;
use App\Enums\CustomerType;

/**
 * 自动发放新人礼包
 * FR-VIP-010: 新人礼包自动发放
 */
class GrantNewCustomerGiftAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);

        // 排除合伙人和内部员工
        if (in_array($customer->customer_type, [CustomerType::PARTNER, CustomerType::INTERNAL], true)) {
            return;
        }

        // 查找有效的新人礼包模板
        $newbieCoupons = Coupon::where('type', CouponType::NEW_CUSTOMER)
            ->where('is_active', true)
            ->where(function ($q) {
                $q->whereNull('valid_until')->orWhere('valid_until', '>', now());
            })
            ->get();

        foreach ($newbieCoupons as $coupon) {
            // 检查是否已领取
            $exists = CustomerCoupon::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->where('coupon_id', $coupon->id)
                ->exists();

            if (!$exists) {
                app(ClaimCouponAction::class)->execute($customerId, $coupon->id);
            }
        }

        // 标记已领取新人礼包（sign位掩码位0）
        $customer->sign |= 1;
        $customer->save();
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Actions\Marketing;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Marketing\Coupon;
use App\Models\Marketing\CustomerCoupon;
use App\Enums\CouponType;
use App\Enums\VipLevel;

/**
 * 按VIP等级自动发放等级券
 * FR-VIP-010: 样品折扣券/印品折扣券/样品券按等级自动发放
 */
class GrantVipLevelCouponsAction
{
    /**
     * VIP等级对应的自动发放券映射
     */
    private const VIP_COUPON_MAP = [
        VipLevel::LV1->value => [CouponType::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT],
        VipLevel::LV2->value => [CouponType::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT],
        VipLevel::LV3->value => [CouponType::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT],
        VipLevel::LV4->value => [], // Lv4无专属折扣券
        VipLevel::LV5->value => [CouponType::SAMPLE_DISCOUNT],
        VipLevel::LV6->value => [CouponType::PRINT_DISCOUNT, CouponType::SAMPLE_VOUCHER],
        VipLevel::LV7->value => [CouponType::PRINT_DISCOUNT, CouponType::SAMPLE_VOUCHER],
        VipLevel::LV8->value => [CouponType::PRINT_DISCOUNT, CouponType::SAMPLE_VOUCHER],
    ];

    public function execute(int $customerId, VipLevel $oldLevel, VipLevel $newLevel): void
    {
        if ($oldLevel === $newLevel) {
            return;
        }

        $couponTypes = self::VIP_COUPON_MAP[$newLevel->value] ?? [];

        foreach ($couponTypes as $type) {
            $coupons = Coupon::where('type', $type)
                ->where('is_active', true)
                ->get();

            foreach ($coupons as $coupon) {
                $exists = CustomerCoupon::where('customer_id', $customerId)
                    ->where('coupon_id', $coupon->id)
                    ->where('status', \App\Enums\CustomerCouponStatus::UNUSED)
                    ->exists();

                if (!$exists) {
                    app(ClaimCouponAction::class)->execute($customerId, $coupon->id);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

---

### 6.43.6 Service 类

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Marketing;

use App\Enums\CouponType;
use App\Enums\CustomerCouponStatus;
use App\Models\Marketing\Coupon;
use App\Models\Marketing\CustomerCoupon;
use App\Models\Order\Order;
use App\ValueObjects\Money;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection;

/**
 * 优惠券匹配与计算服务
 * FR-VIP-012: 下单时自动匹配可用优惠券
 */
class CouponMatcherService
{
    /**
     * 获取客户当前订单可用的所有优惠券
     */
    public function getAvailableCoupons(int $customerId, Order $order): Collection
    {
        return CustomerCoupon::with('coupon')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', CustomerCouponStatus::UNUSED)
            ->where('valid_until', '>', now())
            ->get()
            ->filter(function (CustomerCoupon $cc) use ($order) {
                return $this->isCouponApplicable($cc->coupon, $order);
            });
    }

    /**
     * 判断优惠券是否适用于当前订单
     */
    public function isCouponApplicable(Coupon $coupon, Order $order): bool
    {
        // 检查最低订单金额
        if ($order->total_amount->lessThan($coupon->min_order_amount)) {
            return false;
        }

        // 检查适用范围
        return match ($coupon->scope_type) {
            \App\Enums\CouponScopeType::ALL => true,
            \App\Enums\CouponScopeType::CATEGORY => $this->matchCategory($coupon, $order),
            \App\Enums\CouponScopeType::PRODUCT => $this->matchProduct($coupon, $order),
            \App\Enums\CouponScopeType::ORDER_TYPE => $this->matchOrderType($coupon, $order),
        };
    }

    /**
     * 计算优惠券抵扣金额
     */
    public function calculateDiscount(Coupon $coupon, Money $orderAmount): Money
    {
        $discount = match ($coupon->discount_type) {
            1 => $orderAmount->multiply(1 - $coupon->discount_value->toFloat()), // 百分比折扣
            2 => $coupon->discount_value, // 固定金额
            3 => Money::zero(), // 免运费，运费单独计算
        };

        // 封顶校验
        if ($coupon->max_discount_amount && $discount->greaterThan($coupon->max_discount_amount)) {
            $discount = $coupon->max_discount_amount;
        }

        // 抵扣金额不超过订单金额
        if ($discount->greaterThan($orderAmount)) {
            $discount = $orderAmount;
        }

        return $discount;
    }

    private function matchCategory(Coupon $coupon, Order $order): bool
    {
        $categoryIds = $order->items->pluck('product.category_id')->unique();
        return !empty(array_intersect($categoryIds->toArray(), $coupon->scope_ids ?? []));
    }

    private function matchProduct(Coupon $coupon, Order $order): bool
    {
        $productIds = $order->items->pluck('product_id')->unique();
        return !empty(array_intersect($productIds->toArray(), $coupon->scope_ids ?? []));
    }

    private function matchOrderType(Coupon $coupon, Order $order): bool
    {
        return in_array($order->order_type, $coupon->scope_ids ?? [], true);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Services\Marketing;

use App\ValueObjects\Money;

/**
 * 优惠叠加规则计算服务
 * FR-VIP-014: 叠加规则
 */
class DiscountStackingService
{
    /**
     * 最低折扣封顶
     */
    private const MIN_DISCOUNT_FLOOR = 0.5;

    /**
     * 计算最终折扣系数（考虑VIP折扣 + 优惠券叠加）
     *
     * 规则：
     * 1. 同类型折扣取最优惠，不叠加
     * 2. VIP印品折扣与样品折扣互斥（取最优惠）
     * 3. 优惠券可与VIP折扣叠加（乘法），最低封顶0.5折
     */
    public function calculateFinalDiscount(
        ?float $vipPrintDiscount,   // VIP印品折扣系数，如0.90
        ?float $vipSampleDiscount,  // VIP样品折扣系数，如0.50
        ?float $couponDiscount,     // 优惠券折扣系数，如0.95或固定金额抵扣后的等效系数
        bool $isSampleOrder = false
    ): float {
        // 步骤1：确定VIP折扣（印品/样品互斥取最优惠）
        $vipDiscount = $isSampleOrder
            ? ($vipSampleDiscount ?? 1.0)
            : ($vipPrintDiscount ?? 1.0);

        // 步骤2：叠加优惠券折扣（乘法）
        $finalDiscount = $vipDiscount * ($couponDiscount ?? 1.0);

        // 步骤3：最低折扣封顶0.5折
        return max($finalDiscount, self::MIN_DISCOUNT_FLOOR);
    }

    /**
     * 校验折扣组合是否合法
     */
    public function validateDiscountCombination(array $discounts): bool
    {
        // 检查是否有多个同类型折扣
        $types = array_column($discounts, 'type');
        return count($types) === count(array_unique($types));
    }
}
```

```php
namespace App\Listeners\Marketing;

use App\Events\Marketing\CouponUsed;
use App\Models\Marketing\Coupon;

class UpdateCouponUsageStats
{
    public function handle(CouponUsed $event): void
    {
        $coupon = Coupon::find($event->customerCoupon->coupon_id);
        if ($coupon) {
            $coupon->increment('used_quantity');
        }
    }
}
```

---

### 6.43.8 关键业务规则

| 规则项 | 说明 |
|--------|------|
| **同类型互斥** | 同类型折扣（如两个满减券）不可叠加，系统自动取最优惠 |
| **VIP与券叠加** | VIP折扣系数 × 优惠券折扣系数，乘法叠加 |
| **最低封顶** | 叠加后折扣系数不低于0.5（即最多5折） |
| **印品/样品互斥** | VIP印品折扣与样品折扣互斥，取当前订单类型对应的折扣 |
| **时效规则** | 固定有效期优先，无固定有效期则按领取后N天计算 |
| **样品券限制** | 样品折扣券/金额券仅限样品订单(orderType=sample)使用 |
| **运费券** | 运费券在运费计算阶段独立抵扣，不参与折扣系数叠加 |
| **新人礼包** | 注册自动发放，一次性领取，排除合伙人和内部员工 |

---

```mermaid
classDiagram

        +id
        +code

        +scope_type
        +scope_ids

    class CustomerCoupon {
        +id
        +customer_id
        +coupon_id
        +code
        +status: CustomerCouponStatus
        +claimed_at
        +used_at
        +valid_until
        +isUsable()
        +markAsUsed()

    class ClaimCouponAction {
        +execute(customerId, couponId)
    }
    class CouponMatcherService {
        +getAvailableCoupons(customerId, order)
        +isCouponApplicable(coupon, order)
        +calculateDiscount(coupon, amount)

        +validateDiscountCombination(discounts)
    }
```

## 6.44 用户标签与画像子系统设计 (CustomerTagService)

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x + MySQL 8.0 + Redis 7.x
> **设计原则**：RFM量化驱动、标签规则可配置、画像数据物化加速、Action原子化、Schedule定时更新。
> **关联章节**：6.12 积分成长值系统（grow_value、vip_level联动）、6.32 管理后台（标签管理、客户筛选）。

---

### 6.44.1 设计概述

用户标签与画像子系统承担客户精细化运营的核心数据能力，覆盖 **RFM等级计算、标签生命周期管理、自动/手动打标、客户360°画像、采购偏好分析、消费趋势统计、价值预测** 七大能力域。

**核心设计原则**：

1. **RFM量化分级**：Recency（最近下单距今天数）、Frequency（月均订单频次）、Monetary（累计消费金额）三维评分，每日凌晨通过 Schedule 任务批量重算，输出 A/B/C/D 四级客户等级。
2. **标签规则可配置**：自动打标规则存储于 `tag_rules` 表，支持运营人员热更新阈值与条件，无需发版。
3. **画像数据物化加速**：`customer_profiles` 物化视图（或缓存加速表）聚合客户基本信息、订单统计、偏好品类、消费趋势，避免每次查询进行多表 JOIN 和聚合计算。
4. **打标幂等性**：自动打标任务基于 `customer_tag_bindings` 的联合唯一索引 `(customer_id, tag_id, source)` 保证同一来源标签不重复绑定。
5. **与成长值系统联动**：RFM等级变化时，通过 Laravel Event 触发 `CustomerGradeChanged` 事件，积分成长值系统监听并调整 `grow_value` 与 `vip_level`（6.12节）。

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph 数据采集层
        O1[orders表] --> D1[订单数据]
        O2[order_items表] --> D2[品类/规格数据]
        O3[after_sales表] --> D3[退货数据]
        O4[customer_addresses表] --> D4[地域数据]
    end

    subgraph 计算引擎层
        D1 --> S1[CalculateRfmAction]
        D1 --> S2[AutoTagCustomerAction]
        D2 --> S3[GenerateCustomerProfileAction]
        D3 --> S2
        D4 --> S2
        S1 --> E1[CustomerGradeChanged Event]
    end

    subgraph 数据存储层
        S1 --> T1[customer_rfm_scores]
        S2 --> T2[customer_tag_bindings]
        S3 --> T3[customer_profiles]
        T4[customer_tags] --> S2
        T5[tag_rules] --> S2
    end

    subgraph 应用服务层
        T1 --> S4[CustomerProfileService]
        T2 --> S5[TagManagementService]
        T3 --> S4
        S6[RfmCalculatorService] --> S1
        S7[CustomerValuePredictionService] --> S4
    end

    subgraph 管理后台
        S5 --> A1[标签CRUD]
        S5 --> A2[手动打标]
        S4 --> A3[客户360°画像]
        S4 --> A4[标签组合筛选]
    end
```

---

### 6.44.2 枚举定义

#### TagType（标签类型）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 客户标签类型
 * 对应 customer_tags.tag_type 字段
 */
enum TagType: int
{
    case RFM       = 1;  // RFM等级标签
    case INDUSTRY  = 2;  // 行业标签
    case BEHAVIOR  = 3;  // 行为标签
    case VALUE     = 4;  // 价值标签
    case SERVICE   = 5;  // 服务标签
    case REGION    = 6;  // 地域标签

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::RFM      => 'RFM等级',
            self::INDUSTRY => '行业标签',
            self::BEHAVIOR => '行为标签',
            self::VALUE    => '价值标签',
            self::SERVICE  => '服务标签',
            self::REGION   => '地域标签',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为系统自动打标的类型
     */
    public function isAutoTaggable(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [
            self::RFM,
            self::BEHAVIOR,
            self::VALUE,
            self::SERVICE,
            self::REGION,
        ], true);
    }
}
```

#### RfmLevel（RFM评分等级）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * RFM模型综合评分等级
 * 对应 customer_rfm_scores.rfm_level 字段
 */
enum RfmLevel: string
{
    case A = 'A';  // 重要价值客户
    case B = 'B';  // 重要发展客户
    case C = 'C';  // 一般价值客户
    case D = 'D';  // 流失风险客户

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::A => '重要价值客户',
            self::B => '重要发展客户',
            self::C => '一般价值客户',
            self::D => '流失风险客户',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 获取等级对应的服务响应时效（小时）
     */
    public function responseSlaHours(): int
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::A => 2,
            self::B => 4,
            self::C => 8,
            self::D => 24,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 获取等级对应的账期额度（元）
     */
    public function creditLimit(): float
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::A => 500000.00,
            self::B => 100000.00,
            self::C => 10000.00,
            self::D => 0.00,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 获取等级对应的默认折扣力度（折扣系数，1.0=无折扣）
     */
    public function defaultDiscountFactor(): float
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::A => 0.88,
            self::B => 0.93,
            self::C => 0.97,
            self::D => 1.00,
        };
    }
}
```

#### CustomerGrade（客户等级）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 客户综合等级（与 RFM 解耦，供业务展示使用）
 * 对应 customers.grade 字段（扩展字段）
 */
enum CustomerGrade: string
{
    case A = 'A';
    case B = 'B';
    case C = 'C';
    case D = 'D';

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::A => 'A级客户',
            self::B => 'B级客户',
            self::C => 'C级客户',
            self::D => 'D级客户',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 从 RfmLevel 映射为客户展示等级
     */
    public static function fromRfmLevel(RfmLevel $level): self
    {
        return match ($level) {
            RfmLevel::A => self::A,
            RfmLevel::B => self::B,
            RfmLevel::C => self::C,
            RfmLevel::D => self::D,
        };
    }
}
```

```php
            $table->timestamp('calculated_at')->nullable()->comment('计算时间');

            $table->index('rfm_level', 'idx_rfm_level');
            $table->index('composite_score', 'idx_composite_score');
            $table->index('calculated_at', 'idx_calculated_at');
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('customer_rfm_scores');
```

### 6.44.4 Eloquent模型

#### CustomerTag（客户标签定义模型）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use App\Enums\TagType;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\HasMany;

class CustomerTag extends BaseModel
{
    protected $table = 'customer_tags';

    protected $fillable = [
        'name', 'tag_type', 'color', 'is_auto', 'is_enabled',
        'created_by', 'description',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'tag_type' => TagType::class,
        'is_auto' => 'boolean',
        'is_enabled' => 'boolean',
    ];

    public function bindings(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(CustomerTagBinding::class, 'tag_id');
    }

    public function rules(): HasMany
    {
        return $this->hasMany(TagRule::class, 'tag_id');
    }

    /**
     * 作用域：启用的标签
     */
    public function scopeEnabled($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_enabled', true);
    }
}
```

#### TagRule（自动打标规则模型）

```php
class TagRule extends BaseModel

    protected $fillable = [
        'tag_id', 'rule_name', 'rule_key', 'condition_type',
        'operator', 'threshold', 'priority', 'is_enabled',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'threshold' => 'array',
        'priority' => 'integer',
        'is_enabled' => 'boolean',
    ];

    public function tag(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(CustomerTag::class, 'tag_id');
    }

    public function scopeEnabled($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_enabled', true);
    }
}
```

#### CustomerProfile（客户画像物化模型）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

class CustomerProfile extends BaseModel
{
    protected $table = 'customer_profiles';

    protected $fillable = [
        'customer_id', 'total_orders', 'total_amount', 'avg_order_amount',
        'max_order_amount', 'total_items', 'first_order_at', 'last_order_at',
        'days_since_last_order', 'favorite_categories', 'favorite_specs',
        'favorite_processes', 'total_after_sales', 'return_rate',
        'service_tags', 'monthly_trends', 'predict_prob_30d',
        'predict_amount_30d', 'calculated_at',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'total_amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'avg_order_amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'max_order_amount' => MoneyCast::class,
        'return_rate' => 'decimal:4',
        'favorite_categories' => 'array',
        'favorite_specs' => 'array',
        'favorite_processes' => 'array',
        'service_tags' => 'array',
        'monthly_trends' => 'array',
        'predict_prob_30d' => 'decimal:4',
        'predict_amount_30d' => MoneyCast::class,
        'first_order_at' => 'datetime',
        'last_order_at' => 'datetime',
        'calculated_at' => 'datetime',
    ];

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class, 'customer_id');
    }

    /**
     * 画像数据是否过期（超过24小时需重算）
     */
    public function isStale(): bool
    {
        if (! $this->calculated_at) {
            return true;
        }
        return $this->calculated_at->diffInHours(now()) >= 24;
    }
}
```

```php
        'frequency_monthly' => 'float',

        'm_score' => 'integer',
        'rfm_level' => RfmLevel::class,
        'composite_score' => 'integer',
        'calculated_at' => 'datetime',

    public function customer(): BelongsTo
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class, 'customer_id');

     * 获取当前等级对应的 CustomerGrade
     */
    public function toCustomerGrade(): \App\Enums\CustomerGrade
    {
        return \App\Enums\CustomerGrade::fromRfmLevel($this->rfm_level);
    }
}
```
