### 6.44.5 Action类

#### CreateTagAction（创建/更新标签）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\CustomerTag;

use App\Enums\TagType;
use App\Models\CustomerTag;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Validator;
use Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException;

final class CreateTagAction
{
    /**
     * 创建或更新标签
     *
     * @param array $data 标签数据
     * @param int|null $tagId 为NULL时创建，否则更新
     * @param int|null $adminId 操作人ID
     */
    public function execute(array $data, ?int $tagId = null, ?int $adminId = null): CustomerTag
    {
        $validator = Validator::make($data, [
            'name' => 'required|string|max:64',
            'tag_type' => 'required|integer|in:1,2,3,4,5,6',
            'color' => 'nullable|string|max:16',
            'is_auto' => 'boolean',
            'is_enabled' => 'boolean',
            'description' => 'nullable|string|max:500',
        ]);

        if ($validator->fails()) {
            throw new ValidationException($validator);
        }

        if ($tagId) {
            $tag = CustomerTag::findOrFail($tagId);
            $tag->update($validator->validated());
            return $tag;
        }

        return CustomerTag::create([
            ...$validator->validated(),
            'created_by' => $adminId,
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### CalculateRfmAction（RFM评分计算）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\CustomerTag;

use App\Enums\RfmLevel;
use App\Events\CustomerTag\CustomerGradeChanged;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\CustomerRfmScore;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

final class CalculateRfmAction
{
    /**
     * R 评分阈值（天数越小，评分越高）
     */
    private const R_THRESHOLDS = [
        7  => 5,   // ≤7天
        30 => 4,   // ≤30天
        90 => 3,   // ≤90天
        180 => 2,  // ≤180天
    ];

    /**
     * F 评分阈值（月均频次）
     */
    private const F_THRESHOLDS = [
        5.0  => 5,
        2.0  => 4,
        1.0  => 3,
        0.5  => 2,
    ];

    /**
     * M 评分阈值（累计消费金额）
     */
    private const M_THRESHOLDS = [
        500000 => 5,
        100000 => 4,
        10000  => 3,
        1000   => 2,
    ];

    /**
     * 批量计算所有活跃客户的RFM评分
     */
    public function executeAll(): int
    {
        $count = 0;
        $batchSize = 500;

        Customer::where('status', 1)->chunkById($batchSize, function (Collection $customers) use (&$count) {
            foreach ($customers as $customer) {
                $this->executeSingle($customer);
                $count++;
            }
        });

        Log::info("[RFM] 批量计算完成，共 {$count} 个客户");
        return $count;
    }

    /**
     * 单个客户RFM计算
     */
    public function executeSingle(Customer $customer): CustomerRfmScore
    {
        $stats = $this->fetchOrderStats($customer->id);

        $rScore = $this->scoreRecency($stats['recency_days']);
        $fScore = $this->scoreFrequency($stats['frequency_monthly']);
        $mScore = $this->scoreMonetary($stats['monetary_total']);

        $level = $this->resolveLevel($rScore, $fScore, $mScore);
        $composite = $rScore * 100 + $fScore * 10 + $mScore;

        $oldLevel = null;
        $rfm = CustomerRfmScore::where('customer_id', $customer->id)->first();

        if ($rfm) {
            $oldLevel = $rfm->rfm_level;
            $rfm->update([
                'recency_days' => $stats['recency_days'],
                'r_score' => $rScore,
                'frequency_monthly' => $stats['frequency_monthly'],
                'f_score' => $fScore,
                'monetary_total' => $stats['monetary_total'],
                'm_score' => $mScore,
                'rfm_level' => $level,
                'composite_score' => $composite,
                'calculated_at' => now(),
            ]);
        } else {
            $rfm = CustomerRfmScore::create([
                'customer_id' => $customer->id,
                'recency_days' => $stats['recency_days'],
                'r_score' => $rScore,
                'frequency_monthly' => $stats['frequency_monthly'],
                'f_score' => $fScore,
                'monetary_total' => $stats['monetary_total'],
                'm_score' => $mScore,
                'rfm_level' => $level,
                'composite_score' => $composite,
                'calculated_at' => now(),
            ]);
        }

        // 等级变化时触发事件（供积分成长值系统监听）
        if ($oldLevel && $oldLevel !== $level) {
            event(new CustomerGradeChanged($customer, $oldLevel, $level));
        }

        // RFM评分更新事件（供成长值计算监听）
        event(new \App\Events\RfmScoreUpdated($customer->id, $rfm));

        return $rfm;
    }

    private function fetchOrderStats(int $customerId): array
    {
        $result = DB::table('orders')
            ->selectRaw('
                COUNT(*) as total_orders,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount), 0) as monetary_total,
                MAX(created_at) as last_order_at,
                DATEDIFF(NOW(), MAX(created_at)) as recency_days
            ')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20) // 已支付及以上状态
            ->first();

        $totalOrders = (int) ($result->total_orders ?? 0);
        $monetaryTotal = (float) ($result->monetary_total ?? 0);
        $recencyDays = (int) ($result->recency_days ?? 999);
        $lastOrderAt = $result->last_order_at;

        // 计算月均频次（以首单至今的月数为分母）
        $frequencyMonthly = 0.0;
        if ($totalOrders > 0 && $lastOrderAt) {
            $firstOrderAt = DB::table('orders')
                ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
                ->where('status', '>=', 20)
                ->min('created_at');

            if ($firstOrderAt) {
                $months = max(1, (int) ceil(
                    now()->diffInDays(\Carbon\Carbon::parse($firstOrderAt)) / 30
                ));
                $frequencyMonthly = round($totalOrders / $months, 2);
            }
        }

        return [
            'recency_days' => max(0, $recencyDays),
            'frequency_monthly' => $frequencyMonthly,
            'monetary_total' => $monetaryTotal,
        ];
    }

    private function scoreRecency(int $days): int
    {
        foreach (self::R_THRESHOLDS as $threshold => $score) {
            if ($days <= $threshold) {
                return $score;
            }
        }
        return 1;
    }

    private function scoreFrequency(float $freq): int
    {
        foreach (self::F_THRESHOLDS as $threshold => $score) {
            if ($freq >= $threshold) {
                return $score;
            }
        }
        return 1;
    }

    private function scoreMonetary(float $amount): int
    {
        foreach (self::M_THRESHOLDS as $threshold => $score) {
            if ($amount >= $threshold) {
                return $score;
            }
        }
        return 1;
    }

    /**
     * 综合等级判定：优先看M，其次F，再次R
     */
    private function resolveLevel(int $r, int $f, int $m): RfmLevel
    {
        return match (true) {
            $m >= 4 && $f >= 4 => RfmLevel::A,
            $m >= 3 && $f >= 3 => RfmLevel::B,
            $m >= 2 && $r >= 2 => RfmLevel::C,
            default => RfmLevel::D,
        };
    }
}
```

#### AutoTagCustomerAction（自动打标）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\CustomerTag;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\CustomerTag;
use App\Models\CustomerTagBinding;
use App\Models\CustomerProfile;
use App\Models\TagRule;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

final class AutoTagCustomerAction
{
    /**
     * 全量自动打标（Schedule 调用）
     */
    public function executeAll(): int
    {
        $rules = TagRule::with('tag')
            ->where('is_enabled', true)
            ->orderBy('priority')
            ->get();

        $count = 0;
        $batchSize = 500;

        Customer::where('status', 1)->chunkById($batchSize, function (Collection $customers) use ($rules, &$count) {
            foreach ($customers as $customer) {
                $profile = CustomerProfile::where('customer_id', $customer->id)->first();
                $this->evaluateRulesForCustomer($customer, $rules, $profile);
                $count++;
            }
        });

        Log::info("[AutoTag] 自动打标完成，共 {$count} 个客户");
        return $count;
    }

    /**
     * 单个客户自动打标（订单完成后触发）
     */
    public function executeForCustomer(int $customerId): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        $rules = TagRule::with('tag')
            ->where('is_enabled', true)
            ->orderBy('priority')
            ->get();
        $profile = CustomerProfile::where('customer_id', $customerId)->first();

        $this->evaluateRulesForCustomer($customer, $rules, $profile);
    }

    private function evaluateRulesForCustomer(
        Customer $customer,
        Collection $rules,
        ?CustomerProfile $profile,
    ): void {
        foreach ($rules as $rule) {
            if (! $rule->tag || ! $rule->tag->is_enabled) {
                continue;
            }

            $matched = $this->evaluateRule($customer, $rule, $profile);

            if ($matched) {
                $this->attachTag($customer->id, $rule->tag_id, 1); // source=1 系统自动
            } else {
                // 规则不再命中时，移除系统自动来源的该标签
                $this->detachTagBySource($customer->id, $rule->tag_id, 1);
            }
        }
    }

    private function evaluateRule(Customer $customer, TagRule $rule, ?CustomerProfile $profile): bool
    {
        $threshold = $rule->threshold;

        return match ((int) $rule->condition_type) {
            1 => $this->evalOrderFrequency($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            2 => $this->evalOrderAmount($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            3 => $this->evalNoOrderDays($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            4 => $this->evalReturnRate($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            5 => $this->evalMonetaryTotal($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            6 => $this->evalRegion($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            7 => $this->evalCategoryPreference($customer->id, $threshold, $rule->operator),
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalOrderFrequency(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $days = $threshold['days'] ?? 30;
        $min = $threshold['min'] ?? 0;
        $count = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subDays($days))
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->count();

        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => $count >= $min,
            '>' => $count > $min,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalOrderAmount(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $min = $threshold['min'] ?? 0;
        $max = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->max('total_amount');

        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => (float) $max >= $min,
            '>' => (float) $max > $min,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalNoOrderDays(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $days = $threshold['days'] ?? 90;
        $lastOrder = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->max('created_at');

        if (! $lastOrder) {
            return true; // 从未下单视为满足"未下单"条件
        }

        $diff = now()->diffInDays(\Carbon\Carbon::parse($lastOrder));
        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => $diff >= $days,
            '>' => $diff > $days,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalReturnRate(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $minRate = ($threshold['min'] ?? 0) / 100;
        $totalOrders = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->count();

        if ($totalOrders === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        $returnOrders = DB::table('after_sales')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->whereIn('type', [0, 2]) // 退货退款、优惠货款
            ->distinct('order_id')
            ->count('order_id');

        $rate = $returnOrders / $totalOrders;
        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => $rate >= $minRate,
            '>' => $rate > $minRate,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalMonetaryTotal(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $min = $threshold['min'] ?? 0;
        $total = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->sum('total_amount');

        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => (float) $total >= $min,
            '>' => (float) $total > $min,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalRegion(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $regions = $threshold['regions'] ?? [];
        $province = DB::table('customer_addresses')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('is_default', true)
            ->value('province');

        return match ($operator) {
            'in' => in_array($province, $regions, true),
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function evalCategoryPreference(int $customerId, array $threshold, string $operator): bool
    {
        $categoryId = $threshold['category_id'] ?? null;
        $minCount = $threshold['min_count'] ?? 3;

        if (! $categoryId) {
            return false;
        }

        $count = DB::table('order_items')
            ->join('orders', 'order_items.order_id', '=', 'orders.id')
            ->join('products', 'order_items.product_id', '=', 'products.id')
            ->where('orders.customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('products.category_id', $categoryId)
            ->where('orders.status', '>=', 20)
            ->count();

        return match ($operator) {
            '>=' => $count >= $minCount,
            '>' => $count > $minCount,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    private function attachTag(int $customerId, int $tagId, int $source): void
    {
        CustomerTagBinding::firstOrCreate(
            ['customer_id' => $customerId, 'tag_id' => $tagId, 'source' => $source],
            ['created_at' => now()]
        );
    }

    private function detachTagBySource(int $customerId, int $tagId, int $source): void
    {
        CustomerTagBinding::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('tag_id', $tagId)
            ->where('source', $source)
            ->delete();
    }
}
```

#### ManualTagAction（手动打标）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\CustomerTag;

use App\Models\CustomerTag;
use App\Models\CustomerTagBinding;

final class ManualTagAction
{
    /**
     * 手动为客户添加标签
     */
    public function attach(int $customerId, int $tagId, int $adminId): CustomerTagBinding
    {
        $tag = CustomerTag::findOrFail($tagId);
        throw_unless($tag->is_enabled, \DomainException::class, '标签未启用');

        return CustomerTagBinding::firstOrCreate(
            ['customer_id' => $customerId, 'tag_id' => $tagId, 'source' => 2],
            ['created_by' => $adminId, 'created_at' => now()]
        );
    }

    /**
     * 手动移除客户标签
     */
    public function detach(int $customerId, int $tagId, int $adminId): void
    {
        $binding = CustomerTagBinding::where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('tag_id', $tagId)
            ->where('source', 2) // 仅允许移除手动打标的标签
            ->first();

        if ($binding) {
            $binding->delete();
        }
    }

    /**
     * 批量为客户打标
     *
     * @param int[] $customerIds
     * @param int[] $tagIds
     */
    public function batchAttach(array $customerIds, array $tagIds, int $adminId): int
    {
        $count = 0;
        foreach ($customerIds as $customerId) {
            foreach ($tagIds as $tagId) {
                $this->attach($customerId, $tagId, $adminId);
                $count++;
            }
        }
        return $count;
    }
}
```

#### GenerateCustomerProfileAction（生成客户360°画像）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\CustomerTag;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\CustomerProfile;
use App\Services\CustomerTag\CustomerValuePredictionService;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

final class GenerateCustomerProfileAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private CustomerValuePredictionService $predictionService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 批量生成画像（Schedule 调用）
     */
    public function executeAll(): int
    {
        $count = 0;
        Customer::where('status', 1)->chunkById(500, function (Collection $customers) use (&$count) {
            foreach ($customers as $customer) {
                $this->executeSingle($customer);
                $count++;
            }
        });

        Log::info("[Profile] 画像生成完成，共 {$count} 个客户");
        return $count;
    }

    /**
     * 单个客户画像生成
     */
    public function executeSingle(Customer $customer): CustomerProfile
    {
        $customerId = $customer->id;

        $orderStats = $this->fetchOrderStats($customerId);
        $favorites = $this->fetchFavorites($customerId);
        $afterSaleStats = $this->fetchAfterSaleStats($customerId);
        $trends = $this->fetchMonthlyTrends($customerId);
        $serviceTags = $this->fetchServiceTags($customerId);

        $recencyDays = $orderStats['last_order_at']
            ? now()->diffInDays($orderStats['last_order_at'])
            : 0;

        $returnRate = $orderStats['total_orders'] > 0
            ? round($afterSaleStats['return_orders'] / $orderStats['total_orders'], 4)
            : 0.0;

        $prediction = $this->predictionService->predict($customerId);

        $profile = CustomerProfile::updateOrCreate(
            ['customer_id' => $customerId],
            [
                'total_orders' => $orderStats['total_orders'],
                'total_amount' => $orderStats['total_amount'],
                'avg_order_amount' => $orderStats['avg_order_amount'],
                'max_order_amount' => $orderStats['max_order_amount'],
                'total_items' => $orderStats['total_items'],
                'first_order_at' => $orderStats['first_order_at'],
                'last_order_at' => $orderStats['last_order_at'],
                'days_since_last_order' => $recencyDays,
                'favorite_categories' => $favorites['categories'],
                'favorite_specs' => $favorites['specs'],
                'favorite_processes' => $favorites['processes'],
                'total_after_sales' => $afterSaleStats['total_after_sales'],
                'return_rate' => $returnRate,
                'service_tags' => $serviceTags,
                'monthly_trends' => $trends,
                'predict_prob_30d' => $prediction['probability'],
                'predict_amount_30d' => $prediction['amount'],
                'calculated_at' => now(),
            ]
        );

        return $profile;
    }

    private function fetchOrderStats(int $customerId): array
    {
        $result = DB::table('orders')
            ->selectRaw('
                COUNT(*) as total_orders,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount), 0) as total_amount,
                COALESCE(AVG(total_amount), 0) as avg_order_amount,
                COALESCE(MAX(total_amount), 0) as max_order_amount,
                MIN(created_at) as first_order_at,
                MAX(created_at) as last_order_at
            ')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->first();

        $totalItems = DB::table('order_items')
            ->join('orders', 'order_items.order_id', '=', 'orders.id')
            ->where('orders.customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('orders.status', '>=', 20)
            ->sum('order_items.quantity');

        return [
            'total_orders' => (int) ($result->total_orders ?? 0),
            'total_amount' => (float) ($result->total_amount ?? 0),
            'avg_order_amount' => (float) ($result->avg_order_amount ?? 0),
            'max_order_amount' => (float) ($result->max_order_amount ?? 0),
            'total_items' => (int) $totalItems,
            'first_order_at' => $result->first_order_at ? \Carbon\Carbon::parse($result->first_order_at) : null,
            'last_order_at' => $result->last_order_at ? \Carbon\Carbon::parse($result->last_order_at) : null,
        ];
    }

    private function fetchFavorites(int $customerId): array
    {
        // 偏好品类TOP5
        $categories = DB::table('order_items')
            ->selectRaw('products.category_id, COUNT(*) as count, SUM(order_items.amount) as amount')
            ->join('orders', 'order_items.order_id', '=', 'orders.id')
            ->join('products', 'order_items.product_id', '=', 'products.id')
            ->where('orders.customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('orders.status', '>=', 20)
            ->groupBy('products.category_id')
            ->orderByDesc('count')
            ->limit(5)
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($row) => [
                'category_id' => $row->category_id,
                'count' => (int) $row->count,
                'amount' => (float) $row->amount,
            ])
            ->toArray();

        // 偏好规格TOP5（从 product_params JSON 中提取）
        $specs = DB::table('order_items')
            ->selectRaw('JSON_UNQUOTE(JSON_EXTRACT(product_params, "$[0].value")) as spec_value, COUNT(*) as count')
            ->join('orders', 'order_items.order_id', '=', 'orders.id')
            ->where('orders.customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('orders.status', '>=', 20)
            ->whereNotNull('product_params')
            ->groupBy('spec_value')
            ->orderByDesc('count')
            ->limit(5)
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($row) => [
                'spec_name' => $row->spec_value ?? '未知',
                'count' => (int) $row->count,
            ])
            ->toArray();

        // 偏好工艺TOP5（从 product_params 中提取工艺相关字段）
        $processes = DB::table('order_items')
            ->selectRaw('JSON_UNQUOTE(JSON_EXTRACT(product_params, "$[1].value")) as process_value, COUNT(*) as count')
            ->join('orders', 'order_items.order_id', '=', 'orders.id')
            ->where('orders.customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('orders.status', '>=', 20)
            ->whereNotNull('product_params')
            ->groupBy('process_value')
            ->orderByDesc('count')
            ->limit(5)
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($row) => [
                'process_name' => $row->process_value ?? '未知',
                'count' => (int) $row->count,
            ])
            ->toArray();

        return compact('categories', 'specs', 'processes');
    }

    private function fetchAfterSaleStats(int $customerId): array
    {
        $totalAfterSales = DB::table('after_sales')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->count();

        $returnOrders = DB::table('after_sales')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->whereIn('type', [0, 2])
            ->distinct('order_id')
            ->count('order_id');

        return [
            'total_after_sales' => $totalAfterSales,
            'return_orders' => $returnOrders,
        ];
    }

    private function fetchMonthlyTrends(int $customerId): array
    {
        $rows = DB::table('orders')
            ->selectRaw('
                DATE_FORMAT(created_at, "%Y-%m") as month,
                COUNT(*) as order_count,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount), 0) as amount
            ')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subMonths(12))
            ->groupBy('month')
            ->orderBy('month')
            ->get();

        return $rows->map(fn ($row) => [
            'month' => $row->month,
            'order_count' => (int) $row->order_count,
            'amount' => (float) $row->amount,
        ])->toArray();
    }

    private function fetchServiceTags(int $customerId): array
    {
        $tags = [];

        // 是否要求对账（存在发票申请记录）
        $invoiceCount = DB::table('invoices')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->count();
        if ($invoiceCount > 0) {
            $tags[] = '需要发票';
        }

        // 是否急单多（备注含"急"字且订单完成时间<48小时）
        $urgentCount = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->where('remark', 'like', '%急%')
            ->whereRaw('TIMESTAMPDIFF(HOUR, created_at, completed_at) < 48')
            ->count();
        if ($urgentCount >= 2) {
            $tags[] = '急单多';
        }

        // 是否指定物流（存在物流备注）
        $logisticsCount = DB::table('orders')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->whereNotNull('logistics_remark')
            ->count();
        if ($logisticsCount > 0) {
            $tags[] = '指定物流';
        }

        return $tags;
    }
}
```

---

### 6.44.6 Service类

#### TagManagementService（标签管理服务）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\CustomerTag;

use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\CustomerTag;
use App\Models\CustomerTagBinding;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection;
use Illuminate\Pagination\LengthAwarePaginator;

final class TagManagementService
{
    /**
     * 标签组合筛选客户列表
     * FR-TAG-007
     */
    public function filterCustomersByTags(
        array $tagIds,
        ?string $rfmLevel = null,
        int $perPage = 20,
    ): LengthAwarePaginator {
        $query = Customer::query()
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->with(['tags', 'rfmScore', 'profile']);

        if (! empty($tagIds)) {
            $query->whereHas('tagBindings', function ($q) use ($tagIds) {
                $q->whereIn('tag_id', $tagIds);
            });

            // AND 逻辑：客户必须同时拥有所有指定标签
            foreach ($tagIds as $tagId) {
                $query->whereHas('tagBindings', function ($q) use ($tagId) {
                    $q->where('tag_id', $tagId);
                });
            }
        }

        if ($rfmLevel) {
            $query->whereHas('rfmScore', function ($q) use ($rfmLevel) {
                $q->where('rfm_level', $rfmLevel);
            });
        }

        return $query->paginate($perPage);
    }

    /**
     * 获取客户的全部标签（含来源信息）
     */
    public function getCustomerTags(int $customerId): Collection
    {
        return CustomerTagBinding::with('tag')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->get();
    }

    /**
     * 删除标签（级联删除绑定关系）
     */
    public function deleteTag(int $tagId): void
    {
        $tag = CustomerTag::findOrFail($tagId);

        DB::transaction(function () use ($tag) {
            CustomerTagBinding::where('tag_id', $tag->id)->delete();
            $tag->delete();
        });
    }
}
```

#### RfmCalculatorService（RFM计算服务）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\CustomerTag;

use App\Actions\CustomerTag\CalculateRfmAction;
use App\Enums\RfmLevel;
use App\Models\CustomerRfmScore;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;

final class RfmCalculatorService
{
    public function __construct(
        private CalculateRfmAction $calculateRfmAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 全量重算RFM
     */
    public function recalculateAll(): int
    {
        return $this->calculateRfmAction->executeAll();
    }

    /**
     * 单个客户重算
     */
    public function recalculateForCustomer(int $customerId): CustomerRfmScore
    {
        $customer = \App\Models\Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        return $this->calculateRfmAction->executeSingle($customer);
    }

    /**
     * 获取等级分布统计
     */
    public function getDistributionStats(): array
    {
        return CustomerRfmScore::selectRaw('rfm_level, COUNT(*) as count')
            ->groupBy('rfm_level')
            ->pluck('count', 'rfm_level')
            ->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 获取指定等级客户列表
     */
    public function getCustomersByLevel(RfmLevel $level, int $limit = 100): Collection
    {
        return CustomerRfmScore::with('customer')
            ->where('rfm_level', $level)
            ->orderByDesc('composite_score')
            ->limit($limit)
            ->get();
    }
}
```

#### CustomerProfileService（客户画像查询服务）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\CustomerTag;

use App\Models\CustomerProfile;
use App\Models\CustomerRfmScore;
use App\Models\CustomerTagBinding;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

final class CustomerProfileService
{
    private const CACHE_TTL = 3600; // 1小时
    private const CACHE_PREFIX = 'customer_profile:';

    /**
     * 获取客户360°画像（优先缓存）
     * FR-TAG-008
     */
    public function getProfile(int $customerId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = self::CACHE_PREFIX . $customerId;

        return Cache::remember($cacheKey, self::CACHE_TTL, function () use ($customerId) {
            return $this->buildProfile($customerId);
        });
    }

    /**
     * 刷新客户画像缓存
     */
    public function refreshProfile(int $customerId): array
    {
        $cacheKey = self::CACHE_PREFIX . $customerId;
        Cache::forget($cacheKey);
        return $this->getProfile($customerId);
    }

    private function buildProfile(int $customerId): array
    {
        $profile = CustomerProfile::where('customer_id', $customerId)->first();
        $rfm = CustomerRfmScore::where('customer_id', $customerId)->first();
        $tags = CustomerTagBinding::with('tag')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($b) => [
                'id' => $b->tag_id,
                'name' => $b->tag->name,
                'type' => $b->tag->tag_type->label(),
                'color' => $b->tag->color,
                'source' => $b->source === 1 ? '系统自动' : ($b->source === 2 ? '手动' : 'RFM'),
            ])
            ->toArray();

        if (! $profile) {
            return [
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'tags' => $tags,
                'rfm' => $rfm?->toArray(),
                'stats' => null,
                'favorites' => null,
                'trends' => null,
                'prediction' => null,
            ];
        }

        return [
            'customer_id' => $customerId,
            'tags' => $tags,
            'rfm' => $rfm?->toArray(),
            'stats' => [
                'total_orders' => $profile->total_orders,
                'total_amount' => $profile->total_amount,
                'avg_order_amount' => $profile->avg_order_amount,
                'max_order_amount' => $profile->max_order_amount,
                'total_items' => $profile->total_items,
                'first_order_at' => $profile->first_order_at?->toDateTimeString(),
                'last_order_at' => $profile->last_order_at?->toDateTimeString(),
                'days_since_last_order' => $profile->days_since_last_order,
                'return_rate' => $profile->return_rate,
                'total_after_sales' => $profile->total_after_sales,
            ],
            'favorites' => [
                'categories' => $profile->favorite_categories ?? [],
                'specs' => $profile->favorite_specs ?? [],
                'processes' => $profile->favorite_processes ?? [],
            ],
            'trends' => $profile->monthly_trends ?? [],
            'prediction' => [
                'probability_30d' => $profile->predict_prob_30d,
                'amount_30d' => $profile->predict_amount_30d,
            ],
            'calculated_at' => $profile->calculated_at?->toDateTimeString(),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 消费趋势图数据（FR-TAG-010）
     */
    public function getConsumptionTrend(int $customerId): array
    {
        $profile = CustomerProfile::where('customer_id', $customerId)->first();

        if (! $profile || empty($profile->monthly_trends)) {
            return [];
        }

        return [
            'months' => array_column($profile->monthly_trends, 'month'),
            'order_counts' => array_column($profile->monthly_trends, 'order_count'),
            'amounts' => array_column($profile->monthly_trends, 'amount'),
        ];
    }
}
```

#### CustomerValuePredictionService（客户价值预测服务）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services\CustomerTag;

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

final class CustomerValuePredictionService
{
    /**
     * 基于历史数据预测未来30天消费概率和金额
     * FR-TAG-011
     *
     * 采用简单加权滑动平均模型（SMA + 趋势系数）
     * 生产环境可替换为 ML 模型（如 Prophet / XGBoost）
     */
    public function predict(int $customerId): array
    {
        // 近6个月月度消费金额
        $monthlyData = DB::table('orders')
            ->selectRaw('
                DATE_FORMAT(created_at, "%Y-%m") as month,
                COALESCE(SUM(total_amount), 0) as amount,
                COUNT(*) as order_count
            ')
            ->where('customer_id', $customerId)
            ->where('status', '>=', 20)
            ->where('created_at', '>=', now()->subMonths(6))
            ->groupBy('month')
            ->orderBy('month')
            ->get()
            ->keyBy('month');

        // 无历史数据
        if ($monthlyData->isEmpty()) {
            return [
                'probability' => 0.0,
                'amount' => 0.0,
            ];
        }

        // 计算近3个月平均消费金额（加权：最近月权重最高）
        $recentMonths = $monthlyData->slice(-3)->values();
        $weights = [0.5, 0.3, 0.2]; // 最近3个月权重
        $weightedAmount = 0.0;
        $weightedOrders = 0.0;
        $weightSum = 0.0;

        foreach ($recentMonths as $index => $month) {
            $w = $weights[$index] ?? 0.0;
            $weightedAmount += (float) $month->amount * $w;
            $weightedOrders += (int) $month->order_count * $w;
            $weightSum += $w;
        }

        $avgMonthlyAmount = $weightSum > 0 ? $weightedAmount / $weightSum : 0;
        $avgMonthlyOrders = $weightSum > 0 ? $weightedOrders / $weightSum : 0;

        // 消费概率：基于月均订单数（>1笔/月 视为高概率）
        $probability = min(1.0, $avgMonthlyOrders * 0.8);

        // 预测金额：月均值按30天比例折算，并加入衰减/增长系数
        $trendFactor = $this->calculateTrendFactor($monthlyData);
        $predictAmount = $avgMonthlyAmount * $trendFactor;

        return [
            'probability' => round($probability, 4),
            'amount' => round(max(0, $predictAmount), 2),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 计算趋势系数（基于近3个月vs前3个月）
     */
    private function calculateTrendFactor(\Illuminate\Support\Collection $monthlyData): float
    {
        if ($monthlyData->count() < 4) {
            return 1.0;
        }

        $firstHalf = $monthlyData->slice(0, (int) ceil($monthlyData->count() / 2))->sum('amount');
        $secondHalf = $monthlyData->slice((int) floor($monthlyData->count() / 2))->sum('amount');

        if ($firstHalf <= 0) {
            return 1.2; // 增长趋势
        }

        $ratio = $secondHalf / $firstHalf;
        // 限制趋势系数在 0.5 ~ 1.5 之间
        return max(0.5, min(1.5, $ratio));
    }
}
```

---

### 6.44.7 Schedule任务

#### DailyRfmRecalculation（每日RFM重算）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Services\CustomerTag\RfmCalculatorService;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class DailyRfmRecalculation extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'customer:rfm-recalculate {--customer_id= : 指定客户ID重算}';
    protected $description = '每日RFM客户等级重算（FR-TAG-001）';

    public function handle(RfmCalculatorService $rfmService): int
    {
        $customerId = $this->option('customer_id');

        if ($customerId) {
            $this->info("开始重算客户 #{$customerId} 的RFM评分...");
            $score = $rfmService->recalculateForCustomer((int) $customerId);
            $this->info("客户 #{$customerId} RFM等级更新为：{$score->rfm_level->value}");
            return self::SUCCESS;
        }

        $this->info('开始执行全量RFM重算...');
        $count = $rfmService->recalculateAll();
        $this->info("RFM重算完成，共 {$count} 个客户");
        Log::info("[Schedule] 每日RFM重算完成，共{$count}个客户");

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

#### WeeklyTagSync（每周标签同步与画像生成）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Actions\CustomerTag\AutoTagCustomerAction;
use App\Actions\CustomerTag\GenerateCustomerProfileAction;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class WeeklyTagSync extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'customer:weekly-sync';
    protected $description = '每周标签同步与客户画像全量更新（FR-TAG-005 / FR-TAG-008）';

    public function handle(
        AutoTagCustomerAction $autoTagAction,
        GenerateCustomerProfileAction $profileAction,
    ): int {
        $this->info('开始执行每周客户标签同步...');

        // 步骤1：自动打标
        $tagCount = $autoTagAction->executeAll();
        $this->info("自动打标完成，共处理 {$tagCount} 个客户");

        // 步骤2：生成/更新客户画像
        $profileCount = $profileAction->executeAll();
        $this->info("画像生成完成，共处理 {$profileCount} 个客户");

        Log::info("[Schedule] 每周标签同步完成，打标{$tagCount}个，画像{$profileCount}个");

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

#### Schedule注册（routes/console.php）

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schedule;

// ─── 客户标签与画像子系统 ───
Schedule::command('customer:rfm-recalculate')->dailyAt('01:00');
Schedule::command('customer:weekly-sync')->weeklyOn(1, '02:00'); // 每周一凌晨2点
```

### 6.44.8 关键业务规则

| 规则编号 | 规则项 | 说明 |
|:--------:|--------|------|
| **TAG-R01** | RFM计算周期 | 每日凌晨01:00执行全量重算，单客户触发时实时计算 |
| **TAG-R02** | R评分阈值 | ≤7天=5分 / ≤30天=4分 / ≤90天=3分 / ≤180天=2分 / >180天=1分 |
| **TAG-R03** | F评分阈值 | 月均≥5单=5分 / ≥2单=4分 / ≥1单=3分 / ≥0.5单=2分 / <0.5单=1分 |
| **TAG-R04** | M评分阈值 | ≥50万=5分 / ≥10万=4分 / ≥1万=3分 / ≥1千=2分 / <1千=1分 |
| **TAG-R05** | 综合等级判定 | M≥4且F≥4→A / M≥3且F≥3→B / M≥2且R≥2→C / 其他→D |
| **TAG-R06** | 等级权益差异 | A级：2小时响应+50万账期+8.8折 / B级：4小时+10万+9.3折 / C级：8小时+1万+9.7折 / D级：24小时+无账期+无折扣 |
| **TAG-R07** | 自动打标幂等 | `(customer_id, tag_id, source)` 联合唯一，同一来源不重复绑定 |
| **TAG-R08** | 手动标签保护 | 手动打标的标签（source=2）不会被自动打标任务移除 |
| **TAG-R09** | 标签筛选逻辑 | 多标签筛选为 AND 关系，客户必须同时满足所有指定标签 |
| **TAG-R10** | 画像缓存策略 | `customer_profiles` 物化表每日更新，查询层加Redis缓存1小时 |
| **TAG-R11** | 价值预测模型 | 默认采用加权滑动平均（近3月权重5:3:2），可热替换为ML模型 |
| **TAG-R12** | 等级变化联动 | RFM等级变化触发 `CustomerGradeChanged` 事件，积分系统监听并调整成长值 |
| **TAG-R13** | 首单保护期 | 注册7天内未下单的新客户不参与RFM D级判定，避免误判 |
| **TAG-R14** | 退货率计算 | 退货率 = 有售后记录的订单数 / 已完成订单总数，≥20%触发高风险标签 |

---

```mermaid
classDiagram

        +newLevel: RfmLevel
```

#### 时序图：每日RFM计算与自动打标流程

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Schedule as Laravel Schedule
    participant DailyCmd as DailyRfmRecalculation
    participant RfmSvc as RfmCalculatorService
    participant CalcAct as CalculateRfmAction
    participant DB as MySQL
    participant Event as Event Bus
    participant PointSys as 积分成长值系统

    Schedule->>DailyCmd: 每日01:00执行
    DailyCmd->>RfmSvc: recalculateAll()
    RfmSvc->>CalcAct: executeAll()
    loop chunk 500 customers
        CalcAct->>DB: SELECT order stats
        DB-->>CalcAct: stats
        CalcAct->>CalcAct: scoreRecency/Frequency/Monetary
        CalcAct->>CalcAct: resolveLevel(A/B/C/D)
        alt 等级变化
            CalcAct->>Event: dispatch CustomerGradeChanged
            Event->>PointSys: 监听：调整grow_value/vip_level
        end
        CalcAct->>DB: UPDATE/INSERT customer_rfm_scores
    end
    CalcAct-->>RfmSvc: count
    RfmSvc-->>DailyCmd: count
    DailyCmd-->>Schedule: SUCCESS
```

#### 时序图：客户360°画像查询

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Admin as 管理后台
    participant ProfileSvc as CustomerProfileService
    participant Cache as Redis
    participant Profile as CustomerProfile
    participant TagBind as CustomerTagBinding
    participant Rfm as CustomerRfmScore

    Admin->>ProfileSvc: getProfile(customerId)
    ProfileSvc->>Cache: get("customer_profile:{id}")
    alt 缓存命中
        Cache-->>ProfileSvc: cached profile
    else 缓存未命中
        ProfileSvc->>Profile: SELECT * WHERE customer_id=?
        ProfileSvc->>TagBind: SELECT with tags WHERE customer_id=?
        ProfileSvc->>Rfm: SELECT WHERE customer_id=?
        Profile-->>ProfileSvc: profile data
        TagBind-->>ProfileSvc: tags data
        Rfm-->>ProfileSvc: rfm data
        ProfileSvc->>ProfileSvc: buildProfile()
        ProfileSvc->>Cache: setex 3600s
    end
    ProfileSvc-->>Admin: 360°画像JSON
```

#### 时序图：手动打标与标签筛选

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Admin as 管理员
    participant ManualAct as ManualTagAction
    participant TagSvc as TagManagementService
    participant Tag as CustomerTag
    participant Bind as CustomerTagBinding
    participant DB as MySQL

    Admin->>ManualAct: attach(customerId, tagId, adminId)
    ManualAct->>Tag: findOrFail(tagId)
    ManualAct->>Bind: firstOrCreate (customer_id, tag_id, source=2)
    Bind->>DB: INSERT/IGNORE
    DB-->>Bind: binding record
    Bind-->>ManualAct: CustomerTagBinding
    ManualAct-->>Admin: success

    Admin->>TagSvc: filterCustomersByTags([tagIds], rfmLevel)
    TagSvc->>DB: SELECT customers JOIN tag_bindings
    DB-->>TagSvc: paginated results
    TagSvc-->>Admin: customer list with tags
```

<!-- 第8轮深度Review API补充 - 2026-05-28 -->

## 6.45 Customer模块API设计 (CustomerApi)

> **设计依据**：PRD 模块二（用户系统，FR-USER-002~015）、模块七（物流/地址，FR-LOG-011~017）、模块十（企业认证/品牌，FR-AUTH-014~017、FR-BRAND-001~004）、模块十二（子账号体系，FR-SUB-001~009）、模块六（支付，FR-PAY-028~030）
> **所属领域**：`App\Http\Controllers\Api\Customer`、`App\Http\Resources\Customer`、`App\Http\Requests\Customer`
> **前置章节**：6.16 企业认证系统、6.24 用户认证子系统、6.26 子账号管理服务、6.27 客户地址与品牌管理、6.3 支付系统核心服务

### 6.45.1 设计概述

Customer模块API面向前台客户（含主账号与子账号），提供客户信息管理、地址簿、品牌资质、子账号、支付密码、账户流水、VIP服务、企业认证等 38 个REST端点。所有端点均通过 `auth:sanctum` 中间件保护（存在性检查等个别开放端点除外）。子账号操作通过 `sub_permission:` 中间件进行位掩码权限校验。

控制器严格遵循 **薄控制器** 原则：接收请求 → 委托 Service/Action → 返回 Resource。单方法不超过 15 行。

---

### 6.45.2 路由定义

```php
<?php

// routes/api.php —— 前台 API 路由（v1）Customer 模块补充

use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerAddressController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerBrandController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\SubAccountController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerAuthController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerWalletController;
use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CustomerVipController;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route;

Route::prefix('api/Customer')->middleware(['api', 'throttle:api'])->group(function () {

    // ── 公开端点（无需登录）──
    Route::withoutMiddleware(['auth:sanctum'])->group(function () {
        Route::get('IsExistsCustomerByMobilePhone', [CustomerController::class, 'isExistsByMobilePhone']);
        Route::get('IsExistsCustomerByName', [CustomerController::class, 'isExistsByName']);
        Route::get('IsExistsCustomerByQQ', [CustomerController::class, 'isExistsByQQ']);
    });

    // ── 需登录端点 ──
    Route::middleware('auth:sanctum')->group(function () {

        // 客户信息
        Route::get('BasicInfo', [CustomerController::class, 'basicInfo']);
        Route::get('GetById', [CustomerController::class, 'show']);
        Route::get('GetSimpleById', [CustomerController::class, 'simpleShow']);
        Route::put('UpdateCustomerBasicInfo', [CustomerController::class, 'updateBasicInfo']);

        // 企业认证
        Route::get('GetCustomerAuthInfo', [CustomerAuthController::class, 'authInfo']);
        Route::post('SetCustomerAuthWaiting', [CustomerAuthController::class, 'setAuthWaiting']);
        Route::post('SetCustomerSigned', [CustomerAuthController::class, 'setSigned']);

        // 新客户礼包
        Route::post('NewCustomerReceive', [CustomerController::class, 'newCustomerReceive']);

        // 客户经理
        Route::get('GetCustomerManager', [CustomerController::class, 'getManager']);

        // 客户地址
        Route::get('GetByCustomerAddressCustomerId', [CustomerAddressController::class, 'list']);
        Route::post('CreateCustomerAddress', [CustomerAddressController::class, 'create']);
        Route::put('UpdateCustomerAddress', [CustomerAddressController::class, 'update']);
        Route::delete('DeleteCustomerAddress', [CustomerAddressController::class, 'delete']);
        Route::post('SetCustomerDefaultAddress', [CustomerAddressController::class, 'setDefault']);

        // 客户品牌
        Route::get('GetCustomerBrands', [CustomerBrandController::class, 'list']);
        Route::post('CreateCustomerBrand', [CustomerBrandController::class, 'create']);
        Route::put('UpdateCustomerBrand', [CustomerBrandController::class, 'update']);
        Route::delete('DeleteCustomerBrand', [CustomerBrandController::class, 'delete']);

        // 子账号（主账号专属，子账号无权限）
        Route::middleware('sub_permission:master')->group(function () {
            Route::get('GetSubAccountList', [SubAccountController::class, 'list']);
            Route::post('CreateSubAccount', [SubAccountController::class, 'create']);
            Route::put('UpdateSubAccount', [SubAccountController::class, 'update']);
            Route::put('UpdateSubAccountStatus', [SubAccountController::class, 'updateStatus']);
            Route::post('ResetSubAccountPassword', [SubAccountController::class, 'resetPassword']);
            Route::delete('DeleteSubAccount', [SubAccountController::class, 'delete']);
            Route::post('GrantedSubPermissions', [SubAccountController::class, 'grantPermissions']);
        });

        // 子账号权限查询（登录即可）
        Route::get('GetCustomerSubPermissions', [SubAccountController::class, 'myPermissions']);
        Route::get('GetSubPermissions', [SubAccountController::class, 'allPermissions']);

        // 支付密码
        Route::post('SetPayPassword', [CustomerWalletController::class, 'setPayPassword']);
        Route::put('UpdatePayPassword', [CustomerWalletController::class, 'updatePayPassword']);
        Route::post('VerifyPayPassword', [CustomerWalletController::class, 'verifyPayPassword']);

        // 账户与流水
        Route::get('GetCustomerAccountStatistics', [CustomerWalletController::class, 'accountStatistics']);
        Route::get('GetCustomerAccountTransactions', [CustomerWalletController::class, 'accountTransactions']);

        // VIP 服务
        Route::get('GetVIPServices', [CustomerVipController::class, 'vipServices']);
        Route::get('GetCustomerVipPurchaseRecord', [CustomerVipController::class, 'vipPurchaseRecord']);
        Route::get('IsCanRenew', [CustomerVipController::class, 'isCanRenew']);
    });
});
```

---

### 6.45.3 Controller类

#### 6.45.3.1 CustomerController —— 客户基本信息

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Actions\Marketing\GrantNewCustomerGiftAction;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\UpdateCustomerBasicInfoRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CustomerResource;
use App\Http\Resources\CustomerSimpleResource;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Services\User\CustomerManagerService;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

class CustomerController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private CustomerManagerService $managerService,
        private GrantNewCustomerGiftAction $grantNewCustomerGift,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 获取当前登录客户基本信息
     * GET api/Customer/BasicInfo
     */
    public function basicInfo(Request $request): CustomerResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        return new CustomerResource($customer->load(['account', 'wallet']));
    }

    /**
     * 根据ID获取客户详情
     * GET api/Customer/GetById
     */
    public function show(Request $request): CustomerResource
    {
        $customerId = $request->input('customer_id', auth('customer')->id());
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        $this->authorize('view', $customer);
        return new CustomerResource($customer->load(['account', 'wallet', 'brands', 'addresses']));
    }

    /**
     * 获取简化版客户信息
     * GET api/Customer/GetSimpleById
     */
    public function simpleShow(Request $request): CustomerSimpleResource
    {
        $customerId = $request->input('customer_id', auth('customer')->id());
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        return new CustomerSimpleResource($customer);
    }

    /**
     * 更新客户基本信息
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdateCustomerBasicInfo
     */
    public function updateBasicInfo(UpdateCustomerBasicInfoRequest $request): CustomerResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $customer->update($request->validated());
        return new CustomerResource($customer->fresh());
    }

    /**
     * 检查手机号是否已注册
     * GET api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByMobilePhone
     */
    public function isExistsByMobilePhone(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['mobile_phone' => ['required', 'string']]);
        $exists = Customer::where('mobile_phone', $request->input('mobile_phone'))->exists();
        return response()->json(['exists' => $exists]);
    }

    /**
     * 检查客户名是否已存在
     * GET api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByName
     */
    public function isExistsByName(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['customer_name' => ['required', 'string', 'max:100']]);
        $exists = Customer::where('customer_name', $request->input('customer_name'))->exists();
        return response()->json(['exists' => $exists]);
    }

    /**
     * 检查QQ号是否已存在
     * GET api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByQQ
     */
    public function isExistsByQQ(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['qq' => ['required', 'string']]);
        $exists = Customer::whereRaw("JSON_CONTAINS(qq_accounts, ?)", ['"' . $request->input('qq') . '"'])->exists();
        return response()->json(['exists' => $exists]);
    }

    /**
     * 新客户领取礼包
     * POST api/Customer/NewCustomerReceive
     */
    public function newCustomerReceive(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->grantNewCustomerGift->execute($customer->id);
        return response()->json(['message' => '领取成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 获取专属客户经理
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerManager
     */
    public function getManager(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $manager = $this->managerService->getCustomerManager($customer->id);
        return response()->json(['data' => $manager]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.2 CustomerAuthController —— 企业认证与签约

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Domains\Auth\Actions\CustomerSignAction;
use App\Domains\Auth\Actions\SubmitCustomerAuthAction;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\SubmitCustomerAuthRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CustomerAuthResource;
use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class CustomerAuthController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private SubmitCustomerAuthAction $submitAuth,
        private CustomerSignAction $signAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 获取客户认证信息
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerAuthInfo
     */
    public function authInfo(Request $request): CustomerAuthResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        return new CustomerAuthResource($customer);
    }

    /**
     * 提交认证资料，设置待审核
     * POST api/Customer/SetCustomerAuthWaiting
     */
    public function setAuthWaiting(SubmitCustomerAuthRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->submitAuth->execute($customer->id, $request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '认证资料已提交，等待审核']);
    }

    /**
     * 客户电子签约
     * POST api/Customer/SetCustomerSigned
     */
    public function setSigned(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['agreement_version' => ['required', 'string', 'max:32]]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->signAction->execute($customer->id, $request->input('agreement_version'));
        return response()->json(['message' => '签约成功']);
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.3 CustomerAddressController —— 客户地址簿

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\CreateCustomerAddressRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\UpdateCustomerAddressRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CustomerAddressResource;
use App\Models\User\CustomerAddress;
use App\Services\User\CustomerAddressService;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;

class CustomerAddressController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private CustomerAddressService $addressService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 获取客户地址列表
     * GET api/Customer/GetByCustomerAddressCustomerId
     */
    public function list(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $type = $request->input('type');
        $page = $request->input('page', 1);
        $perPage = $request->input('per_page', 20);

        $paginator = $this->addressService->listAddresses($customer->id, $type, $page, $perPage);
        return CustomerAddressResource::collection($paginator);
    }

    /**
     * 创建客户地址
     * POST api/Customer/CreateCustomerAddress
     */
    public function create(CreateCustomerAddressRequest $request): CustomerAddressResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $address = $this->addressService->createAddress($customer->id, $request->validated());
        return new CustomerAddressResource($address);
    }

    /**
     * 更新客户地址
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdateCustomerAddress
     */
    public function update(UpdateCustomerAddressRequest $request): CustomerAddressResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $address = CustomerAddress::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('address_id'));
        $address->update($request->validated());
        return new CustomerAddressResource($address->fresh());
    }

    /**
     * 删除客户地址
     * DELETE api/Customer/DeleteCustomerAddress
     */
    public function delete(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['address_id' => ['required', 'integer']]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $address = CustomerAddress::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('address_id'));
        $address->delete();
        return response()->json(['message' => '地址已删除']);
    }

    /**
     * 设置默认地址
     * POST api/Customer/SetCustomerDefaultAddress
     */
    public function setDefault(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['address_id' => ['required', 'integer']]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $address = CustomerAddress::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('address_id'));
        $address->setAsDefault();
        return response()->json(['message' => '默认地址已设置']);
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.4 CustomerBrandController —— 客户品牌资质

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\CreateCustomerBrandRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\UpdateCustomerBrandRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CustomerBrandResource;
use App\Models\User\CustomerBrand;
use App\Services\User\CustomerBrandService;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;

class CustomerBrandController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private CustomerBrandService $brandService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 获取客户品牌列表
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerBrands
     */
    public function list(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $status = $request->input('status');
        $page = $request->input('page', 1);
        $perPage = $request->input('per_page', 20);

        $paginator = $this->brandService->listBrands(
            $customer->id,
            $status ? \App\Enums\BrandAuditStatus::tryFrom($status) : null,
            $page,
            $perPage
        );
        return CustomerBrandResource::collection($paginator);
    }

    /**
     * 创建客户品牌
     * POST api/Customer/CreateCustomerBrand
     */
    public function create(CreateCustomerBrandRequest $request): CustomerBrandResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $brand = $this->brandService->createBrand($customer->id, $request->validated());
        return new CustomerBrandResource($brand);
    }

    /**
     * 更新客户品牌
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdateCustomerBrand
     */
    public function update(UpdateCustomerBrandRequest $request): CustomerBrandResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $brand = $this->brandService->updateBrand(
            $customer->id,
            $request->input('brand_id'),
            $request->validated()
        );
        return new CustomerBrandResource($brand);
    }

    /**
     * 删除客户品牌
     * DELETE api/Customer/DeleteCustomerBrand
     */
    public function delete(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['brand_id' => ['required', 'integer']]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->brandService->deleteBrand($customer->id, $request->input('brand_id'));
        return response()->json(['message' => '品牌已删除']);
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.5 SubAccountController —— 子账号管理

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Actions\User\SubAccount\CreateSubAccountAction;
use App\Enums\SubPermission;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\CreateSubAccountRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\GrantSubPermissionsRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\ResetSubAccountPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\UpdateSubAccountRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\SubAccountResource;
use App\Models\User\SubAccount;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Hash;

class SubAccountController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private CreateSubAccountAction $createSubAccount,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 获取子账号列表
     * GET api/Customer/GetSubAccountList
     */
    public function list(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $perPage = $request->input('per_page', 20);
        $list = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->orderByDesc('created_at')
            ->paginate($perPage);
        return SubAccountResource::collection($list);
    }

    /**
     * 创建子账号
     * POST api/Customer/CreateSubAccount
     */
    public function create(CreateSubAccountRequest $request): SubAccountResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = $this->createSubAccount->execute(
            $customer,
            $request->input('sub_name'),
            $request->input('mobile_phone'),
            $request->input('password'),
            $request->input('permission_mask'),
            $request->input('sms_code')
        );
        return new SubAccountResource($subAccount);
    }

    /**
     * 更新子账号
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdateSubAccount
     */
    public function update(UpdateSubAccountRequest $request): SubAccountResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('sub_account_id'));
        $subAccount->update($request->validated());
        return new SubAccountResource($subAccount->fresh());
    }

    /**
     * 更新子账号状态（启用/禁用）
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdateSubAccountStatus
     */
    public function updateStatus(Request $request): SubAccountResource
    {
        $request->validate([
            'sub_account_id' => ['required', 'integer'],
            'active' => ['required', 'boolean'],
        ]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('sub_account_id'));
        $subAccount->update(['active' => $request->boolean('active')]);
        return new SubAccountResource($subAccount->fresh());
    }

    /**
     * 重置子账号密码
     * POST api/Customer/ResetSubAccountPassword
     */
    public function resetPassword(ResetSubAccountPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('sub_account_id'));
        $subAccount->update([
            'password' => Hash::make($request->input('new_password')),
        ]);
        return response()->json(['message' => '密码重置成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 删除子账号
     * DELETE api/Customer/DeleteSubAccount
     */
    public function delete(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $request->validate(['sub_account_id' => ['required', 'integer']]);
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('sub_account_id'));
        $subAccount->delete();
        return response()->json(['message' => '子账号已删除']);
    }

    /**
     * 授予子账号权限
     * POST api/Customer/GrantedSubPermissions
     */
    public function grantPermissions(GrantSubPermissionsRequest $request): SubAccountResource
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $subAccount = SubAccount::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->findOrFail($request->input('sub_account_id'));
        $subAccount->update(['sub_permission' => $request->input('permission_mask')]);
        return new SubAccountResource($subAccount->fresh());
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前子账号权限
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerSubPermissions
     */
    public function myPermissions(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $user = auth('customer')->user();
        if ($user instanceof SubAccount) {
            return response()->json([
                'permission_mask' => $user->sub_permission,
                'permissions' => SubPermission::namesFromMask($user->sub_permission),
            ]);
        }
        return response()->json([
            'permission_mask' => 0,
            'permissions' => ['总账号'],
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取所有可选子权限列表
     * GET api/Customer/GetSubPermissions
     */
    public function allPermissions(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $permissions = array_map(fn (SubPermission $p) => [
            'value' => $p->value,
            'label' => $p->label(),
        ], SubPermission::cases());
        return response()->json(['data' => $permissions]);
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.6 CustomerWalletController —— 支付密码与账户

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Domains\Auth\Actions\SetPayPasswordAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Services\PayPasswordSecurityService;
use App\Domains\Payment\Services\WalletService;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\SetPayPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\UpdatePayPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Customer\VerifyPayPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\AccountTransactionResource;
use App\Models\AccountTransaction;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;

class CustomerWalletController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private WalletService $walletService,
        private PayPasswordSecurityService $payPasswordSecurity,
        private SetPayPasswordAction $setPayPassword,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 设置支付密码
     * POST api/Customer/SetPayPassword
     */
    public function setPayPassword(SetPayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->setPayPassword->execute($customer->id, $request->input('password'));
        return response()->json(['message' => '支付密码设置成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 修改支付密码
     * PUT api/Customer/UpdatePayPassword
     */
    public function updatePayPassword(UpdatePayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->setPayPassword->execute(
            $customer->id,
            $request->input('new_password'),
            $request->input('old_password')
        );
        return response()->json(['message' => '支付密码修改成功']);
    }

    /**
     * 验证支付密码
     * POST api/Customer/VerifyPayPassword
     */
    public function verifyPayPassword(VerifyPayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $this->payPasswordSecurity->verifyPayPassword($customer->id, $request->input('password'));
        return response()->json(['valid' => true]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取客户账户统计
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerAccountStatistics
     */
    public function accountStatistics(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $balance = $this->walletService->getBalance($customer->id);
        return response()->json([
            'data' => [
                'balance' => $balance['balance'],
                'frozen_amount' => $balance['frozenAmount'],
                'available_balance' => $balance['availableBalance'],
                'alert_amount' => $balance['alertAmount'],
                'total_recharge' => $balance['total_recharge'] ?? 0,
                'total_consume' => $balance['total_consume'] ?? 0,
            ],
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取客户账户交易流水
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerAccountTransactions
     */
    public function accountTransactions(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $type = $request->input('type');
        $page = $request->input('page', 1);
        $perPage = $request->input('per_page', 20);

        $query = AccountTransaction::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->orderByDesc('created_at');

        if ($type !== null) {
            $query->where('type', $type);
        }

        return AccountTransactionResource::collection($query->paginate($perPage));
    }
}
```

#### 6.45.3.7 CustomerVipController —— VIP服务

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Domains\Vip\Models\VipService;
use App\Enums\VipLevel;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Resources\VipPurchaseRecordResource;
use App\Http\Resources\VipServiceResource;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;

class CustomerVipController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * 获取VIP服务信息
     * GET api/Customer/GetVIPServices
     */
    public function vipServices(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $vip = VipService::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->first();

        $currentLevel = VipLevel::tryFrom($customer->vip_level);

        return response()->json([
            'data' => [
                'vip_level' => $customer->vip_level,
                'vip_level_name' => $currentLevel?->label() ?? '普通用户',
                'pay_vip_end_time' => $customer->pay_vip_end_time?->toIso8601String(),
                'grow_value' => $customer->grow_value,
                'current_vip_service' => $vip ? new VipServiceResource($vip) : null,
                'next_level' => $this->nextLevelInfo($currentLevel, $customer->grow_value),
            ],
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取VIP购买记录
     * GET api/Customer/GetCustomerVipPurchaseRecord
     */
    public function vipPurchaseRecord(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $page = $request->input('page', 1);
        $perPage = $request->input('per_page', 20);

        $records = VipService::where('customer_id', $customer->id)
            ->where('type', 5) // VIP购买
            ->orderByDesc('created_at')
            ->paginate($perPage);

        return VipPurchaseRecordResource::collection($records);
    }

    /**
     * 检查VIP是否可续费
     * GET api/Customer/IsCanRenew
     */
    public function isCanRenew(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customer = auth('customer')->user();
        $service = app(\App\Domains\Vip\Services\VipRenewalService::class);

        return response()->json([
            'can_renew' => $service->canRenew($customer),
            'grace_period_days' => config('vip.renewal.grace_period_days', 30),
        ]);
    }

    private function nextLevelInfo(?VipLevel $current, int $growValue): ?array
    {
        if (!$current || $current->value >= VipLevel::max()->value) {
            return null;
        }
        $next = VipLevel::from($current->value + 1);
        return [
            'level' => $next->value,
            'level_name' => $next->label(),
            'required_grow_value' => $next->requiredGrowthValue(),
            'current_grow_value' => $growValue,
            'remaining' => max(0, $next->requiredGrowthValue() - $growValue),
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Requests\Customer;

use Illuminate\Foundation\Http\FormRequest;

/**
 * 更新客户基本信息
 */
class UpdateCustomerBasicInfoRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool
    {
        return auth('sanctum')->check();
    }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'contact_name' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:50'],
            'email' => ['nullable', 'email', 'max:100'],
            'avatar_url' => ['nullable', 'url', 'max:500'],
            'customer_type' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'in:0,1,2,3'],
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
            'legal_person_id_card' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:18'],
            'business_license_img' => ['required', 'image', 'max:5120'],
            'auth_picture_type' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'in:1,2'],
            'contact_name' => ['required', 'string', 'max:50'],
            'contact_phone' => ['required', 'regex:/^1[3-9]\d{9}$/'],
            'register_address' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:300'],
            'office_address' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:300'],
            'valid_date' => ['nullable', 'date'],
```

### 6.45.5 Resource响应类

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

/**
 * 客户基本信息 Resource（扩展原 8.1.2 节 CustomerResource）
 */
class CustomerResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'customer_name' => $this->customer_name,
            'contact_name' => $this->contact_name,
            'mobile_phone' => $this->when(
                $request->user()?->can('viewSensitive', $this->resource),
                \Str::mask($this->mobile_phone, '*', 3, 4)
            ),
            'email' => $this->email,
            'avatar' => $this->avatar_url,
            'customer_type' => $this->customer_type,
            'vip_level' => $this->vip_level,
            'vip_level_name' => $this->when($this->vip_level > 0, fn() => match ($this->vip_level) {
                1 => '普通会员', 2 => '银卡会员', 3 => '金卡会员',
                4 => '铂金会员', 5 => '钻石会员', 6 => '至尊会员',
                7 => '黑金会员', 8 => '荣耀会员',
                default => '未知',
            }),
            'auth_status' => $this->auth_status,
            'auth_status_name' => match ((int) $this->auth_status) {
                0 => '未认证', 1 => '认证中', 2 => '已认证',
                3 => '认证失败', 4 => '已冻结', 20 => '代认证通过',
                default => '未知',
            },
            'signed_time' => $this->signed_time?->toIso8601String(),
            'grow_value' => $this->grow_value,
            'pay_vip_end_time' => $this->pay_vip_end_time?->toIso8601String(),
            'balance' => $this->whenLoaded('account', fn() => $this->account->balance),
            'frozen_amount' => $this->whenLoaded('account', fn() => $this->account->frozen_amount),
            'created_at' => $this->created_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

/**
 * 客户认证信息 Resource
 */
class CustomerAuthResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'customer_id' => $this->id,
            'company_name' => $this->company_name,
            'credit_code' => $this->credit_code,
            'legal_person' => $this->legal_person,
            'business_license_img' => $this->business_license_img,
            'auth_status' => (int) $this->auth_status,
            'auth_status_name' => match ((int) $this->auth_status) {
                0 => '未认证', 1 => '认证中', 2 => '已认证',
                3 => '认证失败', 4 => '已冻结', 20 => '代认证通过',
                default => '未知',
            },
            'auth_picture_type' => $this->auth_picture_type,
            'contact_name' => $this->contact_name,
            'contact_phone' => $this->contact_phone,
            'register_address' => $this->register_address,
            'office_address' => $this->office_address,
            'valid_date' => $this->valid_date,
            'verify_reason' => $this->when($this->auth_status == 3 || $this->auth_status == 4, $this->verify_reason),
            'signed_time' => $this->signed_time?->toIso8601String(),
            'is_signed' => $this->signed_time !== null,
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
            'city' => $this->city_name,
            'district' => $this->county_name,
            'detail_address' => $this->detail_address,

            'type_name' => match ((int) $this->type) {
                0 => '收货地址',
                1 => '发票地址',
                2 => '退货地址',
                default => '未知',
            },

            'created_at' => $this->created_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
```

```php
            'status_name' => $this->status?->label() ?? '未知',
            'verify_reason' => $this->when($this->status?->value === 3, $this->verify_reason),
            'start_valid_date' => $this->start_valid_date?->toIso8601String(),
            'end_valid_date' => $this->end_valid_date?->toIso8601String(),
            'created_at' => $this->created_at?->toIso8601String(),
```
