### 6.45.6 API端点清单

| 序号 | API端点 | HTTP方法 | Controller方法 | 中间件 | 关联Service/Action |
|:---:|---------|:-------:|----------------|--------|-------------------|
| 1 | `api/Customer/BasicInfo` | GET | `CustomerController::basicInfo` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 2 | `api/Customer/GetById` | GET | `CustomerController::show` | `auth:sanctum` | CustomerPolicy::view |
| 3 | `api/Customer/GetSimpleById` | GET | `CustomerController::simpleShow` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 4 | `api/Customer/UpdateCustomerBasicInfo` | PUT | `CustomerController::updateBasicInfo` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 5 | `api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByMobilePhone` | GET | `CustomerController::isExistsByMobilePhone` | — | — |
| 6 | `api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByName` | GET | `CustomerController::isExistsByName` | — | — |
| 7 | `api/Customer/IsExistsCustomerByQQ` | GET | `CustomerController::isExistsByQQ` | — | — |
| 8 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerAuthInfo` | GET | `CustomerAuthController::authInfo` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 9 | `api/Customer/SetCustomerAuthWaiting` | POST | `CustomerAuthController::setAuthWaiting` | `auth:sanctum` | `SubmitCustomerAuthAction` |
| 10 | `api/Customer/SetCustomerSigned` | POST | `CustomerAuthController::setSigned` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerSignAction` |
| 11 | `api/Customer/NewCustomerReceive` | POST | `CustomerController::newCustomerReceive` | `auth:sanctum` | `GrantNewCustomerGiftAction` |
| 12 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerManager` | GET | `CustomerController::getManager` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerManagerService` |
| 13 | `api/Customer/GetByCustomerAddressCustomerId` | GET | `CustomerAddressController::list` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerAddressService::listAddresses` |
| 14 | `api/Customer/CreateCustomerAddress` | POST | `CustomerAddressController::create` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerAddressService::createAddress` |
| 15 | `api/Customer/UpdateCustomerAddress` | PUT | `CustomerAddressController::update` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 16 | `api/Customer/DeleteCustomerAddress` | DELETE | `CustomerAddressController::delete` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 17 | `api/Customer/SetCustomerDefaultAddress` | POST | `CustomerAddressController::setDefault` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerAddress::setAsDefault()` |
| 18 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerBrands` | GET | `CustomerBrandController::list` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerBrandService::listBrands` |
| 19 | `api/Customer/CreateCustomerBrand` | POST | `CustomerBrandController::create` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerBrandService::createBrand` |
| 20 | `api/Customer/UpdateCustomerBrand` | PUT | `CustomerBrandController::update` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerBrandService::updateBrand` |
| 21 | `api/Customer/DeleteCustomerBrand` | DELETE | `CustomerBrandController::delete` | `auth:sanctum` | `CustomerBrandService::deleteBrand` |
| 22 | `api/Customer/GetSubAccountList` | GET | `SubAccountController::list` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 23 | `api/Customer/CreateSubAccount` | POST | `SubAccountController::create` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | `CreateSubAccountAction` |
| 24 | `api/Customer/UpdateSubAccount` | PUT | `SubAccountController::update` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 25 | `api/Customer/UpdateSubAccountStatus` | PUT | `SubAccountController::updateStatus` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 26 | `api/Customer/ResetSubAccountPassword` | POST | `SubAccountController::resetPassword` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 27 | `api/Customer/DeleteSubAccount` | DELETE | `SubAccountController::delete` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 28 | `api/Customer/GrantedSubPermissions` | POST | `SubAccountController::grantPermissions` | `auth:sanctum` + `sub_permission:master` | — |
| 29 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerSubPermissions` | GET | `SubAccountController::myPermissions` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 30 | `api/Customer/GetSubPermissions` | GET | `SubAccountController::allPermissions` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 31 | `api/Customer/SetPayPassword` | POST | `CustomerWalletController::setPayPassword` | `auth:sanctum` | `SetPayPasswordAction` |
| 32 | `api/Customer/UpdatePayPassword` | PUT | `CustomerWalletController::updatePayPassword` | `auth:sanctum` | `SetPayPasswordAction` |
| 33 | `api/Customer/VerifyPayPassword` | POST | `CustomerWalletController::verifyPayPassword` | `auth:sanctum` | `PayPasswordSecurityService::verifyPayPassword` |
| 34 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerAccountStatistics` | GET | `CustomerWalletController::accountStatistics` | `auth:sanctum` | `WalletService::getBalance` |
| 35 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerAccountTransactions` | GET | `CustomerWalletController::accountTransactions` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 36 | `api/Customer/GetVIPServices` | GET | `CustomerVipController::vipServices` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 37 | `api/Customer/GetCustomerVipPurchaseRecord` | GET | `CustomerVipController::vipPurchaseRecord` | `auth:sanctum` | — |
| 38 | `api/Customer/IsCanRenew` | GET | `CustomerVipController::isCanRenew` | `auth:sanctum` | — |

---

### 6.45.7 关键业务规则

| 规则 | 实现位置 | 说明 |
|------|---------|------|
| 子账号操作仅限主账号 | `sub_permission:master` 中间件 | 子账号无法创建/管理其他子账号 |
| 地址上限 20 | `CustomerAddressService::MAX_ADDRESSES` | 超限返回 409 |
| 品牌上限 50 | `CustomerBrandService::MAX_BRANDS` | 超限返回 409 |
| 已审核品牌名不可改 | `CustomerBrandService::updateBrand()` | 状态为 APPROVED 时拦截名称变更 |
| 品牌删除前校验订单引用 | `CustomerBrandService::deleteBrand()` | 存在未完成订单则返回 409 |
| 同类型仅 1 个默认地址 | `CustomerAddress::setAsDefault()` | 事务内取消旧默认 |
| 支付密码独立 bcrypt | `SetPayPasswordAction` | 与登录密码隔离 |
| 支付密码连续错误 5 次锁定 24h | `PayPasswordSecurityService` | Redis 计数器 + 锁定键 |
| 金额统一 MoneyCast | `CustomerAccount`、`AccountTransaction` Model | 数据库分存储，Resource 元输出 |
| 敏感字段加密 | `CustomerAddress` Accessors | Crypt::encryptString / decryptString |

---

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class CustomerController {

    CustomerAddressController --> CustomerAddressResource : returns
    CustomerBrandController --> CustomerBrandResource : returns
```

---

## 6.46 Order模块API设计 (OrderApi)

> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：薄控制器（Thin Controller）、Action原子化、FormRequest校验解耦、Resource响应标准化。

---

### 6.46.1 路由定义

所有Order模块路由统一挂载于 `routes/api.php` 的 `Route::prefix('api')->middleware([JwtAuthMiddleware::class, RateLimitMiddleware::class])` 分组下（公共查询接口除外）。

**PRD原始路径与RESTful映射对照表**：

| 序号 | PRD API路径 | HTTP方法 | RESTful路径 | Controller方法 | 中间件 | 关联Action类 |
|------|------------|----------|-------------|----------------|--------|-------------|
| 1 | `api/Order/CreateOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/CreateOrder` | `store` | `auth:sanctum`, `throttle:60,1` | `CreateOrderAction` |
| 2 | `api/Order/BatchCreateOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/BatchCreateOrder` | `batchStore` | `auth:sanctum`, `throttle:30,1` | `BatchCreateOrderAction` |
| 3 | `api/Order/ConfirmOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/ConfirmOrder` | `confirm` | `auth:sanctum` | `ConfirmOrderAction` |
| 4 | `api/Order/Cancel` | POST | `/api/Order/Cancel` | `cancel` | `auth:sanctum` | `CancelOrderAction` |
| 5 | `api/Order/BatchCancelSameDayShippingService` | POST | `/api/Order/BatchCancelSameDayShippingService` | `batchCancelSameDay` | `auth:sanctum` | `BatchCancelSameDayShippingAction` |
| 6 | `api/Order/Reorder` | POST | `/api/Order/Reorder` | `reorder` | `auth:sanctum` | `ReorderAction` |
| 7 | `api/Order/GetOrders` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrders` | `index` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrdersAction` |
| 8 | `api/Order/GetById` | GET | `/api/Order/GetById/{id}` | `show` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderByIdAction` |
| 9 | `api/Order/GetByOrderSN` | GET | `/api/Order/GetByOrderSN` | `showBySn` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderBySnAction` |
| 10 | `api/Order/GetByOrderStatus` | GET | `/api/Order/GetByOrderStatus` | `indexByStatus` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrdersByStatusAction` |
| 11 | `api/Order/GetByOrderType` | GET | `/api/Order/GetByOrderType` | `indexByType` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrdersByTypeAction` |
| 12 | `api/Order/GetByCustomerOrder` | GET | `/api/Order/GetByCustomerOrder` | `indexByCustomer` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetCustomerOrdersAction` |
| 13 | `api/Order/GetOrderStatusNum` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrderStatusNum` | `statusNum` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderStatusNumAction` |
| 14 | `api/Order/GetOrderCountByOrderStatus` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrderCountByOrderStatus` | `countByStatus` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderCountByStatusAction` |
| 15 | `api/Order/GetOrderSNByOrderId` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrderSNByOrderId` | `getSnById` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderSnByIdAction` |
| 16 | `api/Order/CreateCloudhouseOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/CreateCloudhouseOrder` | `createCloudhouse` | `auth:sanctum` | `CreateCloudhouseOrderAction` |
| 17 | `api/Order/BatchCreateCloudhouseOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/BatchCreateCloudhouseOrder` | `batchCreateCloudhouse` | `auth:sanctum` | `BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderAction` |
| 18 | `api/Order/ImportCloudhouseOrder` | POST | `/api/Order/ImportCloudhouseOrder` | `importCloudhouse` | `auth:sanctum` | `ImportCloudhouseOrderAction` |
| 19 | `api/Order/GetCloudhouseOrderDetail` | GET | `/api/Order/GetCloudhouseOrderDetail` | `cloudhouseDetail` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetCloudhouseOrderDetailAction` |
| 20 | `api/Order/GetOrderCloudhouseInfos` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrderCloudhouseInfos` | `cloudhouseInfos` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderCloudhouseInfosAction` |
| 21 | `api/Order/SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddress` | POST | `/api/Order/SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddress` | `setCloudhouseAddress` | `auth:sanctum` | `SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddressAction` |
| 22 | `api/Order/UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddress` | POST | `/api/Order/UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddress` | `updateCloudhouseAddress` | `auth:sanctum` | `UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddressAction` |
| 23 | `api/Order/UpdateOrderDeliveryAddress` | POST | `/api/Order/UpdateOrderDeliveryAddress` | `updateDeliveryAddress` | `auth:sanctum` | `UpdateOrderDeliveryAddressAction` |
| 24 | `api/Order/SetDeliverySenderInfo` | POST | `/api/Order/SetDeliverySenderInfo` | `setSenderInfo` | `auth:sanctum` | `SetDeliverySenderInfoAction` |
| 25 | `api/Order/SetMultipleDelivery` | POST | `/api/Order/SetMultipleDelivery` | `setMultipleDelivery` | `auth:sanctum` | `SetMultipleDeliveryAction` |
| 26 | `api/Order/ComputePackagingFee` | POST | `/api/Order/ComputePackagingFee` | `computePackagingFee` | `auth:sanctum` | `ComputePackagingFeeAction` |
| 27 | `api/Order/GetAllProductCategories` | GET | `/api/Order/GetAllProductCategories` | `allCategories` | — | `GetAllProductCategoriesAction` |
| 28 | `api/Order/ClickCategory` | POST | `/api/Order/ClickCategory` | `clickCategory` | `auth:sanctum` | `ClickCategoryAction` |
| 29 | `api/Order/GetProductUIOrderConfigByCategoryId` | GET | `/api/Order/GetProductUIOrderConfigByCategoryId` | `uiConfigByCategory` | — | `GetProductUIOrderConfigAction` |
| 30 | `api/Order/GetOrderProductCommentByOrderSN` | GET | `/api/Order/GetOrderProductCommentByOrderSN` | `getCommentBySn` | `auth:sanctum` | `GetOrderCommentBySnAction` |
| 31 | `api/Order/UpdateOrderProductComment` | POST | `/api/Order/UpdateOrderProductComment` | `updateComment` | `auth:sanctum` | `UpdateOrderCommentAction` |
| 32 | `api/Order/ValidateOrderFile` | POST | `/api/Order/ValidateOrderFile` | `validateFile` | `auth:sanctum` | `ValidateOrderFileAction` |
| 33 | `api/Order/ConfirmUpload` | POST | `/api/Order/ConfirmUpload` | `confirmUpload` | `auth:sanctum` | `ConfirmUploadAction` |
| 34 | `api/Order/DownloadRemoteFiles` | POST | `/api/Order/DownloadRemoteFiles` | `downloadRemoteFiles` | `auth:sanctum` | `DownloadRemoteFilesAction` |
| 35 | `api/Order/CopyAIRetouchingFiles` | POST | `/api/Order/CopyAIRetouchingFiles` | `copyAiRetouchingFiles` | `auth:sanctum` | `CopyAiRetouchingFilesAction` |
| 36 | `api/Order/BatchCreateOrderFileMerge` | POST | `/api/Order/BatchCreateOrderFileMerge` | `batchCreateWithFileMerge` | `auth:sanctum` | `BatchCreateOrderFileMergeAction` |

**路由文件完整代码 (`routes/api.php`)**：

```php
<?php

use App\Http\Controllers\Api\OrderController;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route;

// Order 模块路由分组
Route::prefix('Order')->middleware(['auth:sanctum', 'throttle:api'])->group(function () {
    // ── 订单创建 ──
    Route::post('CreateOrder', [OrderController::class, 'store']);
    Route::post('BatchCreateOrder', [OrderController::class, 'batchStore']);
    Route::post('ConfirmOrder', [OrderController::class, 'confirm']);
    Route::post('Cancel', [OrderController::class, 'cancel']);
    Route::post('BatchCancelSameDayShippingService', [OrderController::class, 'batchCancelSameDay']);
    Route::post('Reorder', [OrderController::class, 'reorder']);

    // ── 订单查询 ──
    Route::get('GetOrders', [OrderController::class, 'index']);
    Route::get('GetById/{id}', [OrderController::class, 'show']);
    Route::get('GetByOrderSN', [OrderController::class, 'showBySn']);
    Route::get('GetByOrderStatus', [OrderController::class, 'indexByStatus']);
    Route::get('GetByOrderType', [OrderController::class, 'indexByType']);
    Route::get('GetByCustomerOrder', [OrderController::class, 'indexByCustomer']);
    Route::get('GetOrderStatusNum', [OrderController::class, 'statusNum']);
    Route::get('GetOrderCountByOrderStatus', [OrderController::class, 'countByStatus']);
    Route::get('GetOrderSNByOrderId', [OrderController::class, 'getSnById']);

    // ── 云仓订单 ──
    Route::post('CreateCloudhouseOrder', [OrderController::class, 'createCloudhouse']);
    Route::post('BatchCreateCloudhouseOrder', [OrderController::class, 'batchCreateCloudhouse']);
    Route::post('ImportCloudhouseOrder', [OrderController::class, 'importCloudhouse']);
    Route::get('GetCloudhouseOrderDetail', [OrderController::class, 'cloudhouseDetail']);
    Route::get('GetOrderCloudhouseInfos', [OrderController::class, 'cloudhouseInfos']);
    Route::post('SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddress', [OrderController::class, 'setCloudhouseAddress']);
    Route::post('UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddress', [OrderController::class, 'updateCloudhouseAddress']);

    // ── 配送与地址 ──
    Route::post('UpdateOrderDeliveryAddress', [OrderController::class, 'updateDeliveryAddress']);
    Route::post('SetDeliverySenderInfo', [OrderController::class, 'setSenderInfo']);
    Route::post('SetMultipleDelivery', [OrderController::class, 'setMultipleDelivery']);

    // ── 费用计算 ──
    Route::post('ComputePackagingFee', [OrderController::class, 'computePackagingFee']);

    // ── 评价 ──
    Route::get('GetOrderProductCommentByOrderSN', [OrderController::class, 'getCommentBySn']);
    Route::post('UpdateOrderProductComment', [OrderController::class, 'updateComment']);

    // ── 分类与UI（公开接口免登录） ──
    Route::get('GetAllProductCategories', [OrderController::class, 'allCategories'])
        ->withoutMiddleware(['auth:sanctum']);
    Route::post('ClickCategory', [OrderController::class, 'clickCategory']);
    Route::get('GetProductUIOrderConfigByCategoryId', [OrderController::class, 'uiConfigByCategory'])
        ->withoutMiddleware(['auth:sanctum']);

    // ── 文件服务 ──
    Route::post('ValidateOrderFile', [OrderController::class, 'validateFile']);
    Route::post('ConfirmUpload', [OrderController::class, 'confirmUpload']);
    Route::post('DownloadRemoteFiles', [OrderController::class, 'downloadRemoteFiles']);
    Route::post('CopyAIRetouchingFiles', [OrderController::class, 'copyAiRetouchingFiles']);
    Route::post('BatchCreateOrderFileMerge', [OrderController::class, 'batchCreateWithFileMerge']);
});
```

---

### 6.46.2 Controller类

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Actions\Order\BatchCancelSameDayShippingAction;
use App\Actions\Order\BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\BatchCreateOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\BatchCreateOrderFileMergeAction;
use App\Actions\Order\CancelOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ClickCategoryAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ComputePackagingFeeAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ConfirmOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ConfirmUploadAction;
use App\Actions\Order\CopyAiRetouchingFilesAction;
use App\Actions\Order\CreateCloudhouseOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\CreateOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\DownloadRemoteFilesAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetAllProductCategoriesAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetCloudhouseOrderDetailAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetCustomerOrdersAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderCloudhouseInfosAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderCommentBySnAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderCountByStatusAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderByIdAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderBySnAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderSnByIdAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderStatusNumAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrdersAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrdersByStatusAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrdersByTypeAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetProductUIOrderConfigAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ImportCloudhouseOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ReorderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddressAction;
use App\Actions\Order\SetDeliverySenderInfoAction;
use App\Actions\Order\SetMultipleDeliveryAction;
use App\Actions\Order\UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddressAction;
use App\Actions\Order\UpdateOrderCommentAction;
use App\Actions\Order\UpdateOrderDeliveryAddressAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ValidateOrderFileAction;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\BatchCancelSameDayRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\BatchCreateOrderFileMergeRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\BatchCreateOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\CancelOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ClickCategoryRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ComputePackagingFeeRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ConfirmOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ConfirmUploadRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\CopyAiRetouchingFilesRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\CreateCloudhouseOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\CreateOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\DownloadRemoteFilesRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetByOrderSnRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetByStatusRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetByTypeRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetCloudhouseOrderDetailRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetCommentBySnRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetOrderCloudhouseInfosRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetOrdersRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ImportCloudhouseOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ReorderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\SetCloudhouseAddressRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\SetDeliverySenderInfoRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\SetMultipleDeliveryRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\UpdateCloudhouseAddressRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\UpdateCommentRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\UpdateDeliveryAddressRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ValidateOrderFileRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CloudhouseOrderDetailResource;
use App\Http\Resources\CloudhouseOrderResource;
use App\Http\Resources\OrderCollection;
use App\Http\Resources\OrderCommentResource;
use App\Http\Resources\OrderResource;
use App\Http\Resources\OrderStatusNumResource;
use App\Http\Resources\PackagingFeeResource;
use App\Http\Resources\ProductCategoryResource;
use App\Http\Resources\ProductUIConfigResource;
use App\Http\Resources\UploadConfirmResource;
use App\Http\Resources\ValidateFileResource;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\AnonymousResourceCollection;

/**
 * Order模块API控制器
 *
 * 设计约束：
 * - 单方法 ≤ 15 行
 * - 仅负责 IO 转换（Request → Action → Resource）
 * - 禁止在Controller中编写业务规则、事务管理、异常捕获
 */
class OrderController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private CreateOrderAction $createOrder,
        private BatchCreateOrderAction $batchCreateOrder,
        private ConfirmOrderAction $confirmOrder,
        private CancelOrderAction $cancelOrder,
        private BatchCancelSameDayShippingAction $batchCancelSameDay,
        private ReorderAction $reorder,
        private GetOrdersAction $getOrders,
        private GetOrderByIdAction $getOrderById,
        private GetOrderBySnAction $getOrderBySn,
        private GetOrdersByStatusAction $getOrdersByStatus,
        private GetOrdersByTypeAction $getOrdersByType,
        private GetCustomerOrdersAction $getCustomerOrders,
        private GetOrderStatusNumAction $getOrderStatusNum,
        private GetOrderCountByStatusAction $getOrderCountByStatus,
        private GetOrderSnByIdAction $getOrderSnById,
        private CreateCloudhouseOrderAction $createCloudhouseOrder,
        private BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderAction $batchCreateCloudhouseOrder,
        private ImportCloudhouseOrderAction $importCloudhouseOrder,
        private GetCloudhouseOrderDetailAction $getCloudhouseDetail,
        private GetOrderCloudhouseInfosAction $getCloudhouseInfos,
        private SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddressAction $setCloudhouseAddress,
        private UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddressAction $updateCloudhouseAddress,
        private UpdateOrderDeliveryAddressAction $updateDeliveryAddress,
        private SetDeliverySenderInfoAction $setSenderInfo,
        private SetMultipleDeliveryAction $setMultipleDelivery,
        private ComputePackagingFeeAction $computePackagingFee,
        private GetAllProductCategoriesAction $getAllCategories,
        private ClickCategoryAction $clickCategory,
        private GetProductUIOrderConfigAction $getUiConfig,
        private GetOrderCommentBySnAction $getCommentBySn,
        private UpdateOrderCommentAction $updateComment,
        private ValidateOrderFileAction $validateFile,
        private ConfirmUploadAction $confirmUpload,
        private DownloadRemoteFilesAction $downloadRemoteFiles,
        private CopyAiRetouchingFilesAction $copyAiRetouchingFiles,
        private BatchCreateOrderFileMergeAction $batchCreateFileMerge,
    ) {}

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  订单创建类 (Create)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 1. 创建订单
     */
    public function store(CreateOrderRequest $request): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->createOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    /**
     * 2. 批量创建订单
     */
    public function batchStore(BatchCreateOrderRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->batchCreateOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 3. 确认订单
     */
    public function confirm(ConfirmOrderRequest $request): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->confirmOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    /**
     * 4. 取消订单
     */
    public function cancel(CancelOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->cancelOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '订单已取消']);
    }

    /**
     * 5. 批量取消当日出货服务
     */
    public function batchCancelSameDay(BatchCancelSameDayRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->batchCancelSameDay->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '批量取消完成', 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /**
     * 6. 一键翻单/再下单
     */
    public function reorder(ReorderRequest $request): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->reorder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  订单查询类 (Query)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 7. 获取订单列表
     */
    public function index(GetOrdersRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->getOrders->execute($request->filters(), $request->perPage());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 8. 根据ID获取订单详情
     */
    public function show(int $id): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->getOrderById->execute($id);
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    /**
     * 9. 根据订单编号获取订单详情
     */
    public function showBySn(GetByOrderSnRequest $request): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->getOrderBySn->execute($request->validated('order_sn'));
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    /**
     * 10. 按状态查询订单
     */
    public function indexByStatus(GetByStatusRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->getOrdersByStatus->execute($request->validated('status'), $request->perPage());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 11. 按类型查询订单
     */
    public function indexByType(GetByTypeRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->getOrdersByType->execute($request->validated('order_type'), $request->perPage());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 12. 查询客户相关订单
     */
    public function indexByCustomer(GetOrdersRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->getCustomerOrders->execute($request->filters(), $request->perPage());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 13. 获取订单各状态数量
     */
    public function statusNum(Request $request): OrderStatusNumResource
    {
        $data = $this->getOrderStatusNum->execute(auth('sanctum')->id());
        return new OrderStatusNumResource($data);
    }

    /**
     * 14. 按状态统计订单数量
     */
    public function countByStatus(GetByStatusRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $count = $this->getOrderCountByStatus->execute($request->validated('status'));
        return response()->json(['count' => $count]);
    }

    /**
     * 15. 根据订单ID获取订单编号
     */
    public function getSnById(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $sn = $this->getOrderSnById->execute($request->input('order_id'));
        return response()->json(['order_sn' => $sn]);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  云仓订单类 (Cloudhouse)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 16. 创建云仓订单
     */
    public function createCloudhouse(CreateCloudhouseOrderRequest $request): OrderResource
    {
        $order = $this->createCloudhouseOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderResource($order);
    }

    /**
     * 17. 批量创建云仓订单
     */
    public function batchCreateCloudhouse(BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->batchCreateCloudhouseOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }

    /**
     * 18. 导入云仓订单
     */
    public function importCloudhouse(ImportCloudhouseOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->importCloudhouseOrder->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '导入完成', 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /**
     * 19. 获取云仓订单详情
     */
    public function cloudhouseDetail(GetCloudhouseOrderDetailRequest $request): CloudhouseOrderDetailResource
    {
        $detail = $this->getCloudhouseDetail->execute($request->validated('order_sn'));
        return new CloudhouseOrderDetailResource($detail);
    }

    /**
     * 20. 获取订单云仓信息列表
     */
    public function cloudhouseInfos(GetOrderCloudhouseInfosRequest $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $infos = $this->getCloudhouseInfos->execute($request->filters(), $request->perPage());
        return CloudhouseOrderResource::collection($infos);
    }

    /**
     * 21. 设置云仓订单配送地址
     */
    public function setCloudhouseAddress(SetCloudhouseAddressRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->setCloudhouseAddress->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '云仓配送地址已设置']);
    }

    /**
     * 22. 更新云仓订单配送地址
     */
    public function updateCloudhouseAddress(UpdateCloudhouseAddressRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->updateCloudhouseAddress->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '云仓配送地址已更新']);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  配送与地址类 (Delivery)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 23. 更新订单配送地址
     */
    public function updateDeliveryAddress(UpdateDeliveryAddressRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->updateDeliveryAddress->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '配送地址已更新']);
    }

    /**
     * 24. 设置发货人信息
     */
    public function setSenderInfo(SetDeliverySenderInfoRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->setSenderInfo->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '发货人信息已设置']);
    }

    /**
     * 25. 设置多地址配送
     */
    public function setMultipleDelivery(SetMultipleDeliveryRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->setMultipleDelivery->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '多地址配送已设置']);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  费用计算类 (Pricing)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 26. 计算包装费
     */
    public function computePackagingFee(ComputePackagingFeeRequest $request): PackagingFeeResource
    {
        $fee = $this->computePackagingFee->execute($request->validated());
        return new PackagingFeeResource($fee);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  分类与UI类 (Category & UI)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 27. 获取全部产品分类（公开接口）
     */
    public function allCategories(Request $request): AnonymousResourceCollection
    {
        $categories = $this->getAllCategories->execute();
        return ProductCategoryResource::collection($categories);
    }

    /**
     * 28. 分类点击埋点
     */
    public function clickCategory(ClickCategoryRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->clickCategory->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '埋点已记录']);
    }

    /**
     * 29. 根据分类ID获取产品UI下单配置（公开接口）
     */
    public function uiConfigByCategory(Request $request): ProductUIConfigResource
    {
        $config = $this->getUiConfig->execute($request->input('category_id'));
        return new ProductUIConfigResource($config);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  评价类 (Comment)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 30. 根据订单编号获取订单商品评价
     */
    public function getCommentBySn(GetCommentBySnRequest $request): OrderCommentResource
    {
        $comment = $this->getCommentBySn->execute($request->validated('order_sn'));
        return new OrderCommentResource($comment);
    }

    /**
     * 31. 更新订单商品评价
     */
    public function updateComment(UpdateCommentRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->updateComment->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => '评价已更新']);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  文件服务类 (File)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    /**
     * 32. 校验订单文件
     */
    public function validateFile(ValidateOrderFileRequest $request): ValidateFileResource
    {
        $result = $this->validateFile->execute($request->validated());
        return new ValidateFileResource($result);
    }

    /**
     * 33. 确认文件上传
     */
    public function confirmUpload(ConfirmUploadRequest $request): UploadConfirmResource
    {
        $result = $this->confirmUpload->execute($request->validated());
        return new UploadConfirmResource($result);
    }

    /**
     * 34. 下载远程文件
     */
    public function downloadRemoteFiles(DownloadRemoteFilesRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $urls = $this->downloadRemoteFiles->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['data' => $urls]);
    }

    /**
     * 35. 复制AI修图文件
     */
    public function copyAiRetouchingFiles(CopyAiRetouchingFilesRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->copyAiRetouchingFiles->execute($request->validated());
        return response()->json(['message' => 'AI修图文件已复制', 'data' => $result]);
    }

    /**
     * 36. 批量创建订单并合并文件
     */
    public function batchCreateWithFileMerge(BatchCreateOrderFileMergeRequest $request): OrderCollection
    {
        $orders = $this->batchCreateFileMerge->execute($request->validated());
        return new OrderCollection($orders);
    }
}
```

**控制器设计约束**：

| 约束项 | 规则 |
|--------|------|
| 方法长度 | ≤ 15 行，禁止嵌套 if/for |
| 职责范围 | 仅 IO 转换（Request → Action → Resource） |
| 事务管理 | 禁止在 Controller 中使用 `DB::transaction`，由 Action 负责 |
| 业务逻辑 | 禁止在 Controller 中编写业务规则 |
| 异常处理 | 不捕获异常，统一由 `Handler.php` 转换 |

---

### 6.46.3 FormRequest验证类

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Requests\Order;

use Illuminate\Foundation\Http\FormRequest;

// ── 1. 创建订单 ──
class CreateOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'items' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1'],
            'items.*.product_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:products,id'],
            'items.*.quantity' => ['required', 'integer', 'min:1', 'max:99999'],
            'items.*.cp_summary' => ['required', 'string', 'max:512'],
            'address_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:customer_addresses,id'],
            'delivery_type' => ['required', 'integer', 'in:0,1,2,3'],
            'customer_coupon_id' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'exists:customer_coupons,id'],
            'remark' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:500'],
            'invoice_title_id' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'exists:invoice_titles,id'],
        ];
    }

    protected function passedValidation(): void
    {
        $this->merge(['customer_id' => auth('sanctum')->id()]);
    }
}

// ── 2. 批量创建订单 ──
class BatchCreateOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'orders' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1', 'max:50'],
            'orders.*.items' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1'],
            'orders.*.address_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:customer_addresses,id'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 3. 确认订单 ──
class ConfirmOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => ['required', 'string', 'exists:orders,order_sn'],
            'confirm_items' => ['required', 'array'],
            'pay_channel' => ['required', 'string', 'in:wechat,alipay,pre_deposit,transfer'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 4. 取消订单 ──
class CancelOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => ['required', 'string', 'exists:orders,order_sn'],
            'reason_code' => ['required', 'integer', 'between:0,9'],
            'reason_desc' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:200'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 5. 批量取消当日出货 ──
class BatchCancelSameDayRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sns' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1', 'max:100'],
            'order_sns.*' => ['required', 'string', 'exists:orders,order_sn'],
            'reason_code' => ['required', 'integer', 'between:0,9'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 6. 一键翻单 ──
class ReorderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'source_type' => ['required', 'in:order,favorite_order,favorite'],
            'source_id' => ['required', 'integer'],
            'address_id' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'exists:customer_addresses,id'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 7-15. 订单查询通用基类 ──
class GetOrdersRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'page' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'min:1'],
            'per_page' => ['nullable', 'integer', 'min:1', 'max:100'],
            'keyword' => ['nullable', 'string', 'max:100'],
            'start_date' => ['nullable', 'date'],
            'end_date' => ['nullable', 'date', 'after_or_equal:start_date'],
        ];
    }

    public function filters(): array
    {
        return $this->only(['keyword', 'start_date', 'end_date']);
    }

    public function perPage(): int
    {
        return $this->integer('per_page', 15);
    }
}

class GetByOrderSnRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }
    public function rules(): array { return ['order_sn' => ['required', 'string', 'exists:orders,order_sn']]; }
}

class GetByStatusRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }
    public function rules(): array { return ['status' => ['required', 'integer']]; }
}

class GetByTypeRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }
    public function rules(): array { return ['order_type' => ['required', 'integer', 'in:1,2,3,4']]; }
}

// ── 16. 创建云仓订单 ──
class CreateCloudhouseOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'items' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1'],
            'items.*.sku_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:product_skus,id'],
            'items.*.quantity' => ['required', 'integer', 'min:1'],
            'warehouse_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:warehouses,id'],
            'delivery_address_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:customer_addresses,id'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 17. 批量创建云仓订单 ──
class BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'orders' => ['required', 'array', 'min:1', 'max:200'],
            'orders.*.sku_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:product_skus,id'],
            'orders.*.quantity' => ['required', 'integer', 'min:1'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 18. 导入云仓订单 ──
class ImportCloudhouseOrderRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'file' => ['required', 'file', 'mimes:xlsx,xls,csv', 'max:10240'],
            'warehouse_id' => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:warehouses,id'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 19. 云仓订单详情 ──

{
    public function authorize(): bool { return auth('sanctum')->check(); }

}

        ];
    }
}

}
```

### 6.46.4 Resource响应类

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\ResourceCollection;

// ── 订单明细项Resource ──
class OrderItemResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'product_id' => $this->product_id,
            'product_name' => $this->product_name,
            'cp_summary' => $this->cp_summary,
            'quantity' => $this->quantity,
            'unit_price' => $this->unit_price_yuan,
            'total_price' => $this->total_price_yuan,
            'thumbnail' => $this->thumbnail_url,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 订单配送Resource ──
class OrderDeliveryResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'address' => $this->address,
            'receiver_name' => $this->receiver_name,
            'receiver_phone' => $this->receiver_phone,
            'express_company' => $this->express_company,
            'tracking_no' => $this->tracking_no,
            'status' => $this->status?->label(),
            'shipped_at' => $this->shipped_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
}

// ── 订单状态数量Resource ──
class OrderStatusNumResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'pending_payment' => $this['pending_payment'] ?? 0,
            'in_production' => $this['in_production'] ?? 0,
            'shipped' => $this['shipped'] ?? 0,
            'completed' => $this['completed'] ?? 0,
            'cancelled' => $this['cancelled'] ?? 0,
            'pending_audit' => $this['pending_audit'] ?? 0,
            'pending_modify' => $this['pending_modify'] ?? 0,
            'total' => $this['total'] ?? 0,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 云仓订单详情Resource ──
class CloudhouseOrderDetailResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => $this->order_sn,
            'warehouse' => new WarehouseResource($this->whenLoaded('warehouse')),
            'sku_items' => CloudhouseSkuItemResource::collection($this->whenLoaded('skuItems')),
            'stock_status' => $this->stock_status,
            'available_quantity' => $this->available_quantity,
            'delivery_eta' => $this->delivery_eta,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 云仓订单列表Resource ──
class CloudhouseOrderResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => $this->order_sn,
            'warehouse_name' => $this->warehouse_name,
            'sku_count' => $this->sku_count,
            'total_quantity' => $this->total_quantity,
            'status' => $this->status->label(),
            'created_at' => $this->created_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
}

// ── 包装费Resource ──
class PackagingFeeResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'product_id' => $this->product_id,
            'quantity' => $this->quantity,
            'packaging_type' => $this->packaging_type,
            'fee_yuan' => $this->fee_yuan,
            'fee_fen' => $this->fee_fen,
            'details' => $this->details,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 产品分类Resource ──
class ProductCategoryResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'name' => $this->name,
            'parent_id' => $this->parent_id,
            'level' => $this->level,
            'icon' => $this->icon_url,
            'sort' => $this->sort_order,
            'children' => ProductCategoryResource::collection($this->whenLoaded('children')),
        ];
    }
}

// ── 产品UI配置Resource ──
class ProductUIConfigResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'category_id' => $this->category_id,
            'layout_type' => $this->layout_type,
            'param_groups' => $this->param_groups,
            'design_spec' => $this->design_spec,
            'price_calculator_config' => $this->price_calculator_config,
            'file_upload_config' => $this->file_upload_config,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 订单评价Resource ──
class OrderCommentResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => $this->order_sn,
            'product_id' => $this->product_id,
            'product_name' => $this->product_name,
            'comment' => $this->comment,
            'images' => $this->images,
            'level' => $this->level?->label(),
            'created_at' => $this->created_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
}

// ── 文件校验结果Resource ──
class ValidateFileResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'is_valid' => $this['is_valid'],
            'violations' => $this['violations'] ?? [],
            'suggestions' => $this['suggestions'] ?? [],
            'parsed_meta' => $this['parsed_meta'] ?? null,
        ];
    }
}

// ── 上传确认Resource ──
class UploadConfirmResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn' => $this['order_sn'],
            'confirmed_files' => $this['confirmed_files'] ?? [],
            'file_version' => $this['file_version'] ?? 1,
            'upload_status' => $this['upload_status'],
        ];
    }
}

// ── 支付记录Resource ──
class PaymentResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id' => $this->id,
            'pay_no' => $this->pay_no,
            'channel' => $this->channel?->label(),
            'amount' => $this->amount_yuan,
            'status' => $this->status?->label(),
            'paid_at' => $this->paid_at?->toIso8601String(),
        ];
    }
}
```

---

### 6.46.5 Action类映射汇总

| 序号 | Controller方法 | Action类 | 说明 |
|------|---------------|----------|------|
| 1 | `store` | `CreateOrderAction` | 创建订单，含计价、库存锁定、支付流水 |
| 2 | `batchStore` | `BatchCreateOrderAction` | 批量创建，事务包裹，失败回滚 |
| 3 | `confirm` | `ConfirmOrderAction` | 确认订单参数，生成待支付状态 |
| 4 | `cancel` | `CancelOrderAction` | 取消订单，释放库存，触发事件 |
| 5 | `batchCancelSameDay` | `BatchCancelSameDayShippingAction` | 批量取消当日出货，校验状态 |
| 6 | `reorder` | `ReorderAction` | 一键翻单，复制规格/文件 |
| 7 | `index` | `GetOrdersAction` | 分页查询当前客户订单 |
| 8 | `show` | `GetOrderByIdAction` | 按ID查询，含关联预加载 |
| 9 | `showBySn` | `GetOrderBySnAction` | 按订单编号查询 |
| 10 | `indexByStatus` | `GetOrdersByStatusAction` | 按内部状态FM过滤 |
| 11 | `indexByType` | `GetOrdersByTypeAction` | 按订单类型（普通/样品/云仓/账期）过滤 |
| 12 | `indexByCustomer` | `GetCustomerOrdersAction` | 查询指定客户订单（主账号视角） |
| 13 | `statusNum` | `GetOrderStatusNumAction` | 聚合各状态数量 |
| 14 | `countByStatus` | `GetOrderCountByStatusAction` | 单一状态计数 |
| 15 | `getSnById` | `GetOrderSnByIdAction` | ID→SN映射查询 |
| 16 | `createCloudhouse` | `CreateCloudhouseOrderAction` | 云仓单条下单，校验库存 |
| 17 | `batchCreateCloudhouse` | `BatchCreateCloudhouseOrderAction` | 云仓批量下单，Excel/JSON导入 |
| 18 | `importCloudhouse` | `ImportCloudhouseOrderAction` | 解析Excel导入云仓订单 |
| 19 | `cloudhouseDetail` | `GetCloudhouseOrderDetailAction` | 云仓订单详情，含SKU明细 |
| 20 | `cloudhouseInfos` | `GetOrderCloudhouseInfosAction` | 云仓订单列表查询 |
| 21 | `setCloudhouseAddress` | `SetCloudhouseOrderDeliveryAddressAction` | 设置云仓配送地址 |
| 22 | `updateCloudhouseAddress` | `UpdateOrderCloudhouseDeliveryAddressAction` | 更新云仓配送地址 |
| 23 | `updateDeliveryAddress` | `UpdateOrderDeliveryAddressAction` | 修改普通订单地址 |
| 24 | `setSenderInfo` | `SetDeliverySenderInfoAction` | 设置发货人信息 |
| 25 | `setMultipleDelivery` | `SetMultipleDeliveryAction` | 多地址拆分，运费折扣计算 |
| 26 | `computePackagingFee` | `ComputePackagingFeeAction` | 包装费计算引擎 |
| 27 | `allCategories` | `GetAllProductCategoriesAction` | 分类树查询（缓存） |
| 28 | `clickCategory` | `ClickCategoryAction` | 写入分类点击埋点 |
| 29 | `uiConfigByCategory` | `GetProductUIOrderConfigAction` | 品类参数模板/UI渲染配置 |
| 30 | `getCommentBySn` | `GetOrderCommentBySnAction` | 按SN查询评价 |
| 31 | `updateComment` | `UpdateOrderCommentAction` | 更新/追加评价 |
| 32 | `validateFile` | `ValidateOrderFileAction` | 设计规范校验（分辨率/色彩/格式） |
| 33 | `confirmUpload` | `ConfirmUploadAction` | 文件分片合并确认，写入file_versions |
| 34 | `downloadRemoteFiles` | `DownloadRemoteFilesAction` | 远程文件转存至MinIO |
| 35 | `copyAiRetouchingFiles` | `CopyAiRetouchingFilesAction` | 美图云修文件跨订单复用 |
| 36 | `batchCreateWithFileMerge` | `BatchCreateOrderFileMergeAction` | 批量下单+文件合并策略 |

---

### 6.46.6 设计约束与边界说明

1. **幂等性**：`CreateOrder`、`BatchCreateOrder`、`BatchCreateOrderFileMerge` 等写操作接口必须携带 `Idempotency-Key` 请求头，由 `IdempotencyMiddleware` 保障 24 小时内同一 Key 不重复执行。

2. **限流策略**：
   - 创建类接口：`throttle:30,1`（30次/分钟）
   - 查询类接口：`throttle:120,1`（120次/分钟）
   - 批量操作接口：`throttle:10,1`（10次/分钟）

3. **数据权限**：所有订单查询 Action 内部必须注入 `OrderPolicy`，自动附加 `customer_id = auth()->id()` 或子账号权限范围过滤，禁止在 Controller 中手动拼接 `where` 条件。

4. **金额统一**：Resource 中对外暴露的金额字段统一为 `*_yuan`（元，保留两位小数），内部存储为分（Integer），通过 `MoneyCast` 自动转换。

5. **文件服务边界**：`ValidateOrderFile`、`ConfirmUpload`、`DownloadRemoteFiles`、`CopyAIRetouchingFiles` 在 Controller 层统一收口于 Order 模块，实际由 `FileService` / `DesignSpecValidationService` 承载具体逻辑，保持 Order 模块的完整性。

6. **分类/UI接口边界**：`GetAllProductCategories`、`ClickCategory`、`GetProductUIOrderConfigByCategoryId` 在 PRD 中归属于 Order 模块（下单前链路），实现上可复用 `ProductCategoryService` 与 `ParamTemplateService`，Controller 仅做代理转发。

---

## 6.47 Pay模块API设计

> **文档定位**：补充SDD 6.2-A支付系统的API Controller与路由层设计，覆盖PRD支付相关功能需求（FR-PAY-001 ~ FR-PAY-030）。
> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：支付网关抽象、回调幂等、状态机驱动、敏感操作密码校验。

---

### 6.47.1 PayController 设计

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\ApplyPayUrlAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\CreatePayOrderAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\PreDepositPayAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\QueryPayOrderAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\TransferAccountAction;
use App\Domains\Payment\Services\PayNotificationService;
use App\Domains\Payment\Services\PayQueryService;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\ApplyPayUrlRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\ConfirmTransferReceiptRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\CreatePayOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\PreDepositPayRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\QueryPayOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\TransferAccountRequest;
use App\Traits\ApiResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

/**
 * Pay模块API控制器
 * 覆盖PRD: FR-PAY-001 ~ FR-PAY-030
 */
class PayController extends Controller
{
    use ApiResponse;

    public function __construct(
        private ApplyPayUrlAction $applyPayUrlAction,
        private CreatePayOrderAction $createPayOrderAction,
        private QueryPayOrderAction $queryPayOrderAction,
        private PreDepositPayAction $preDepositPayAction,
        private TransferAccountAction $transferAccountAction,
        private PayQueryService $payQueryService,
        private PayNotificationService $notificationService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 申请支付链接
     * FR-PAY-001
     * POST /api/Pay/ApplyPayUrl
     */
    public function applyPayUrl(ApplyPayUrlRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->applyPayUrlAction->execute(
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            payChannel: $request->input('pay_channel'),
            returnUrl: $request->input('return_url'),
            clientIp: $request->ip(),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'pay_url' => $result->payUrl,
            'pay_params' => $result->payParams,
            'expire_at' => $result->expireAt,
            'order_no' => $result->orderNo,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询可用收银台
     * FR-PAY-002
     * GET /api/Pay/AvailableCashier
     */
    public function availableCashier(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $cashiers = $this->payQueryService->getAvailableCashiers(
            amount: $request->input('amount'),
            orderType: $request->input('order_type'),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'cashiers' => $cashiers,
            'default_channel' => $cashiers[0]['channel'] ?? null,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 创建支付订单（统一下单）
     * FR-PAY-001-A / FR-PAY-023
     * POST /api/Pay/CreatePayOrder
     */
    public function createPayOrder(CreatePayOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $payOrder = $this->createPayOrderAction->execute(
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            payChannel: $request->input('pay_channel'),
            amount: $request->input('amount'),
            subject: $request->input('subject'),
            body: $request->input('body'),
            metadata: $request->input('metadata', []),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'pay_order_no' => $payOrder->pay_order_no,
            'pay_channel' => $payOrder->pay_channel,
            'amount' => $payOrder->amount,
            'status' => $payOrder->status,
            'created_at' => $payOrder->created_at,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询支付订单状态
     * FR-PAY-003
     * GET /api/Pay/QueryPayOrder
     */
    public function queryPayOrder(QueryPayOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $payOrder = $this->queryPayOrderAction->execute(
            payOrderNo: $request->input('pay_order_no'),
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'pay_order_no' => $payOrder->pay_order_no,
            'order_no' => $payOrder->order_no,
            'status' => $payOrder->status->value,
            'status_name' => $payOrder->status->label(),
            'pay_channel' => $payOrder->pay_channel,
            'amount' => $payOrder->amount,
            'paid_at' => $payOrder->paid_at,
            'expire_at' => $payOrder->expire_at,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询支付是否成功（轮询接口）
     * FR-PAY-003
     * GET /api/Pay/IsPaySucceed
     */
    public function isPaySucceed(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->payQueryService->isPaySucceed(
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            payOrderNo: $request->input('pay_order_no'),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'is_succeed' => $result->isSucceed,
            'status' => $result->status->value,
            'paid_at' => $result->paidAt,
            'pay_channel' => $result->payChannel,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 预存款支付（余额支付）
     * FR-PAY-008-D
     * POST /api/Pay/PreDepositPay
     */
    public function preDepositPay(PreDepositPayRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->preDepositPayAction->execute(
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            payPassword: $request->input('pay_password'),
            customerId: auth('api')->id(),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'order_no' => $result->orderNo,
            'is_paid' => $result->isPaid,
            'paid_amount' => $result->paidAmount,
            'balance_after' => $result->balanceAfter,
            'paid_at' => $result->paidAt,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 转账支付（对公转账）
     * FR-PAY-023
     * POST /api/Pay/TransferAccount
     */
    public function transferAccount(TransferAccountRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->transferAccountAction->execute(
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            voucherImage: $request->input('voucher_image'),
            transferAmount: $request->input('transfer_amount'),
            transferBank: $request->input('transfer_bank'),
            transferTime: $request->input('transfer_time'),
            remark: $request->input('remark'),
            customerId: auth('api')->id(),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'order_no' => $result->orderNo,
            'transfer_id' => $result->transferId,
            'status' => $result->status->value,
            'audit_status' => 'pending',
            'submitted_at' => $result->submittedAt,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 确认转账到账（财务后台审核后调用）
     * FR-PAY-024
     * POST /api/Pay/ConfirmTransferReceipt
     */
    public function confirmTransferReceipt(ConfirmTransferReceiptRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->transferAccountAction->confirmReceipt(
            transferId: $request->input('transfer_id'),
            orderNo: $request->input('order_no'),
            confirmedBy: auth('api')->id(),
            remark: $request->input('remark'),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'order_no' => $result->orderNo,
            'transfer_id' => $result->transferId,
            'status' => $result->status->value,
            'confirmed_at' => $result->confirmedAt,
            'confirmed_by' => $result->confirmedBy,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询收款账户信息
     * FR-PAY-005
     * GET /api/Pay/ReceiveAccount
     */
    public function receiveAccount(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $account = $this->payQueryService->getReceiveAccount(
            channel: $request->input('channel', 'all'),
        );

        return $this->success($account);
    }

    /**
     * 批量查询收款账户信息
     * FR-PAY-005
     * GET /api/Pay/BatchReceiveAccount
     */
    public function batchReceiveAccount(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $accounts = $this->payQueryService->getBatchReceiveAccounts(
            channels: $request->input('channels', []),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'accounts' => $accounts,
            'total' => count($accounts),
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询提现记录
     * FR-PAY-021
     * GET /api/Pay/GetWithdrawRecords
     */
    public function getWithdrawRecords(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $records = $this->payQueryService->getWithdrawRecords(
            customerId: auth('api')->id(),
            status: $request->input('status'),
            page: $request->input('page', 1),
            perPage: $request->input('per_page', 20),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'list' => $records->items(),
            'pagination' => [
                'total' => $records->total(),
                'per_page' => $records->perPage(),
                'current_page' => $records->currentPage(),
                'last_page' => $records->lastPage(),
            ],
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 微信支付异步通知
     * FR-PAY-008-B
     * POST /api/Pay/Notify/Wechat
     * 注意：无需JWT认证中间件，由微信支付平台直接调用
     */
    public function wechatNotify(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->notificationService->handleWechatNotify(
            payload: $request->getContent(),
            headers: $request->headers->all(),
        );

        // 返回微信要求的成功响应
        return response()->json([
            'code' => 'SUCCESS',
            'message' => 'OK',
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 支付宝异步通知
     * FR-PAY-008-B
     * POST /api/Pay/Notify/Alipay
     * 注意：无需JWT认证中间件，由支付宝平台直接调用
     */
    public function alipayNotify(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->notificationService->handleAlipayNotify(
            params: $request->all(),
        );

        // 返回支付宝要求的成功响应（纯文本"success"）
        return response('success');
    }
}
```

---

### 6.47.1-A GroupPayController 设计

> **文档定位**：补充PRD FR-PAY-009/010 分享群组支付功能的 Controller 设计。

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Domains\Payment\Services\GroupPayService;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\CreateGroupPayRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\JoinGroupPayRequest;
use App\Traits\ApiResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class GroupPayController extends Controller
{
    use ApiResponse;

    public function __construct(
        private GroupPayService $groupPayService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 发起群组支付
     * FR-PAY-010
     * POST /api/Pay/GroupPay/Create
     */
    public function create(CreateGroupPayRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $request->input('order_sn'))->firstOrFail();

        $groupPayment = $this->groupPayService->createGroupPayment(
            order: $order,
            membersConfig: $request->input('members', []),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'group_payment_id' => $groupPayment->id,
            'share_link' => $this->groupPayService->generateShareLink($groupPayment),
            'total_amount' => $groupPayment->total_amount,
            'status' => $groupPayment->status,
            'expired_at' => $groupPayment->share_link_expired_at,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 通过分享链接查询群组支付状态（无需登录）
     * FR-PAY-009
     * GET /api/Pay/GroupPay/Info/{token}
     */
    public function info(string $token): JsonResponse
    {
        $groupPayment = $this->groupPayService->validateShareLink($token);

        return $this->success([
            'group_payment_id' => $groupPayment->id,
            'order_sn' => $groupPayment->order->order_sn,
            'total_amount' => $groupPayment->total_amount,
            'status' => $groupPayment->status,
            'members' => $groupPayment->members->map(fn ($m) => [
                'share_amount' => $m->share_amount,
                'paid_amount' => $m->paid_amount,
                'status' => $m->status,
            ]),
            'expired_at' => $groupPayment->share_link_expired_at,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 参与群组支付
     * FR-PAY-010
     * POST /api/Pay/GroupPay/Join
     */
    public function join(JoinGroupPayRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $paymentResult = $this->groupPayService->joinAndPay(
            token: $request->input('token'),
            user: auth('api')->user(),
            payType: $request->input('pay_type'),
            payParams: $request->input('pay_params', []),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'transaction_no' => $paymentResult['transactionNo'] ?? null,
            'pay_params' => $paymentResult['payParams'] ?? null,
            'expired_at' => $paymentResult['expiredAt'] ?? null,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 查询我参与的群组支付列表
     * FR-PAY-009
     * GET /api/Pay/GroupPay/List
     */
    public function list(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->groupPayService->listByUser(
            userId: auth('api')->id(),
            page: $request->input('page', 1),
            perPage: $request->input('per_page', 20),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'list' => $result->items(),
            'pagination' => [
                'total' => $result->total(),
                'per_page' => $result->perPage(),
                'current_page' => $result->currentPage(),
                'last_page' => $result->lastPage(),
            ],
        ]);
    }
}
```

---

### 6.47.2 Pay模块路由设计

```php
<?php

use App\Http\Controllers\Api\PayController;
use App\Http\Middleware\JwtAuthMiddleware;
use App\Http\Middleware\RateLimitMiddleware;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route;

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 公共路由（无需认证）—— 支付回调接口
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Route::prefix('api')->group(function () {

    // 微信支付异步通知（无需JWT认证，由微信服务器调用）
    Route::post('/Pay/Notify/Wechat', [PayController::class, 'wechatNotify'])
        ->name('pay.notify.wechat')
        ->middleware([RateLimitMiddleware::class]);

    // 支付宝异步通知（无需JWT认证，由支付宝服务器调用）
    Route::post('/Pay/Notify/Alipay', [PayController::class, 'alipayNotify'])
        ->name('pay.notify.alipay')
        ->middleware([RateLimitMiddleware::class]);
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 认证路由（需要JWT认证 + 限流）—— 支付业务接口
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Route::prefix('api')->middleware([JwtAuthMiddleware::class, RateLimitMiddleware::class])->group(function () {

    // ── 支付订单管理 ──
    Route::post('/Pay/CreatePayOrder', [PayController::class, 'createPayOrder'])
        ->name('pay.create_order');

    Route::get('/Pay/QueryPayOrder', [PayController::class, 'queryPayOrder'])
        ->name('pay.query_order');

    Route::post('/Pay/ApplyPayUrl', [PayController::class, 'applyPayUrl'])
        ->name('pay.apply_url');

    Route::get('/Pay/AvailableCashier', [PayController::class, 'availableCashier'])
        ->name('pay.available_cashier');

    Route::get('/Pay/IsPaySucceed', [PayController::class, 'isPaySucceed'])
        ->name('pay.is_succeed');

    // ── 支付方式 ──
    Route::post('/Pay/PreDepositPay', [PayController::class, 'preDepositPay'])
        ->name('pay.pre_deposit');

    Route::post('/Pay/TransferAccount', [PayController::class, 'transferAccount'])
        ->name('pay.transfer_account');

    Route::post('/Pay/ConfirmTransferReceipt', [PayController::class, 'confirmTransferReceipt'])
        ->name('pay.confirm_transfer')
        ->middleware(['role:finance']); // 仅限财务角色

    // ── 账户信息查询 ──
    Route::get('/Pay/ReceiveAccount', [PayController::class, 'receiveAccount'])
        ->name('pay.receive_account');

    Route::get('/Pay/BatchReceiveAccount', [PayController::class, 'batchReceiveAccount'])
        ->name('pay.batch_receive_account');

    Route::get('/Pay/GetWithdrawRecords', [PayController::class, 'getWithdrawRecords'])
        ->name('pay.withdraw_records');

    // ── 群组支付 ──
    Route::post('/Pay/GroupPay/Create', [GroupPayController::class, 'create'])
        ->name('pay.group_pay.create');

    Route::get('/Pay/GroupPay/Info/{token}', [GroupPayController::class, 'info'])
        ->name('pay.group_pay.info')
        ->withoutMiddleware([JwtAuthMiddleware::class]); // 匿名可访问

    Route::post('/Pay/GroupPay/Join', [GroupPayController::class, 'join'])
        ->name('pay.group_pay.join');

    Route::get('/Pay/GroupPay/List', [GroupPayController::class, 'list'])
        ->name('pay.group_pay.list');
});
```

---

### 6.47.3 Pay模块API清单

| 接口路径 | HTTP方法 | 中间件 | PRD需求 | 说明 |
|----------|----------|--------|---------|------|
| `/api/Pay/CreatePayOrder` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-001-A | 创建支付订单（统一下单） |
| `/api/Pay/QueryPayOrder` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-003 | 查询支付订单状态 |
| `/api/Pay/ApplyPayUrl` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-001 | 申请支付链接 |
| `/api/Pay/AvailableCashier` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-002 | 可用收银台列表 |
| `/api/Pay/IsPaySucceed` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-003 | 支付是否成功（轮询） |
| `/api/Pay/PreDepositPay` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-008-D | 预存款/余额支付 |
| `/api/Pay/TransferAccount` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-023 | 对公转账支付 |
| `/api/Pay/ConfirmTransferReceipt` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware`, `role:finance` | FR-PAY-024 | 确认转账到账（财务审核） |
| `/api/Pay/ReceiveAccount` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-005 | 收款账户信息 |
| `/api/Pay/BatchReceiveAccount` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-005 | 批量收款账户 |
| `/api/Pay/GetWithdrawRecords` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-021 | 提现记录查询 |
| `/api/Pay/Notify/Wechat` | POST | `RateLimitMiddleware`（无JWT） | FR-PAY-008-B | 微信支付异步通知 |
| `/api/Pay/Notify/Alipay` | POST | `RateLimitMiddleware`（无JWT） | FR-PAY-008-B | 支付宝异步通知 |
| `/api/Pay/GroupPay/Create` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-010 | 发起群组支付 |
| `/api/Pay/GroupPay/Info/{token}` | GET | `RateLimitMiddleware`（无JWT） | FR-PAY-009 | 分享链接查询群组支付状态 |
| `/api/Pay/GroupPay/Join` | POST | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-010 | 参与群组支付 |
| `/api/Pay/GroupPay/List` | GET | `JwtAuthMiddleware`, `RateLimitMiddleware` | FR-PAY-009 | 查询我参与的群组支付 |

> **回调安全设计**：`Notify/Wechat` 与 `Notify/Alipay` 虽然不经过 `JwtAuthMiddleware`，但内部通过支付平台签名验证（`PayNotificationService`）确保请求来源可信。同时配置IP白名单与防重放攻击校验（nonce + timestamp）。
